------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE baixarcompos
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE baixarcompos
Lparameters pPro

With ThisForm
    If .ShouldProcess()
        .ExecuteQuery()
        
        _Oper = .DetermineOperationType()
        
        llOk = .CheckOk()
        
        If llOk
            .InsertIntoMvHst()
        EndIf 
    EndIf
EndWith 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE baixasubnivel
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE baixasubnivel
*** Tiago - 02/04/2014 - Método criado para atualizar as OPs como baixadas conforme a configuraçăo. Método criado para quando der erro de DEADLOCK

=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
_Nivel    = crSigCdOpd.Dopps
_NivelOp  = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
_NumNivel = crSigCdOpd.NDopps
_BaixaSubnivel = (crSigCdOpd.BxAutos = 1)
pTru = .t.

Select TmpOperacao
Scan
	Set Decimals to 0
	_Operacao  = Right(Str(TmpOperacao.Codigos, 12), 10)
	_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)
	_Nops = _nOperacao

	If CrSigCdOpd.Grodns = 1	
		_NivelOs = CrSigCdOpd.Nivels

		lcQuery = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datas, ContaDs From SigPdMvf ]+;
				[Where Nenvs = ]+Str(_nOperacao)+[ And Dopps = ']+_NivelOs+[' And Emps = ']+TmpNens.Emps+[' ]+;
				[ Order By CidChaves Desc]
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalEnve') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalEnve)')
			Return 0
		EndIf
		
		_ChaveNens = LocalEnve.Emps + LocalEnve.Dopps + Str(LocalEnve.Numps, 10)
		lcSql = [Select CidChaves, Retrabs, Chksubn From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+_ChaveNens+[']
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')

		lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
					 [Set NAceites = ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10)) + [ ] + ;
					 Iif(_BaixaSubnivel,[, ChkSubn = ?pTru ],[])+;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (OK - Update - SigCdNec)')
			Return 0
		Endif
	Else
		If _BaixaSubNivel
			_CheckBaixa = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
			llPcc = crSigCdOpd.Pccs					
			
			lcChv = ThisForm.pEmps + _CheckBaixa + Str(_Noperacao, 10)
			lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where empdnps = ']+lcchv+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
			Select LocalNens
			Scan
				lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
							 [Set ChkSubn = ?pTru, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
						   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 4)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
			EndScan

			lcChv = ThisForm.pEmps + _Nivelop + Str(_Nops, 10)
			lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where empdnps = ']+lcchv+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
			Select LocalNens
			If Not Eof()
				lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
							 [Set ChkSubn = ?pTru, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
						   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 5)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndIf
	Endif
Endscan
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cancelabaixa
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cancelabaixa
Lparameters pOperacao

lcEDNe = pOperacao

lcQuery = [Select distinct EmpdopNumb From SigBxEst Where EmpDopNums = ?lcEDNe ]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrBxIt') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxIt)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

If Reccount('CrBxIt') = 0
	Return .t.
Endif

Select CrSigGtmpR
Zap

lcCidQuery = fUniqueIds()

Select CrBxIt
Scan
	Select CrSigGtmpR
	Append Blank
	Replace EmpDopNums With CrBxIt.EmpDopNumb,;
			CidQuerys  With lcCidQuery,;
			CidChaves  With fUniqueIds()
EndScan
		
If !ThisForm.Podatamgr4.UpDate('CrSigGtmpR')
	=ThisForm.Podatamgr4.RollBack()
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrSigGtmpR 3)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
If ThisForm.PoDataMgr4.commit() < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Commit 4)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcQuery = [Select b.EmpdopNums, b.Cpros, b.CodBarras, b.QtBaixas, b.cidChaves, b.citens, b.Qtds From SigMvItn b, SigGtmpR a ]+;
		  [Where a.CidQuerys = '] + lcCidQuery + [' And a.EmpDopNums = b.EmpDopNums ]

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrBxItem1') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxItem1)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
ThisForm.PodataMgr4.fSqlApagarTmp('SigGtmpR', lcCidquery )

Select CrBxItem1
Index On EmpDopNums + Cpros Tag EmpDopNum

lcSql = [Select * From SigBxEst where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEDNe+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'CrBxEst') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxEst)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Select crBxEst
Scan
	_QtBaixar  = crBxEst.Qtdes
	_ChaveDelBx = crBxEst.Empbs + crbxest.Dopebs + Str( crbxest.Numebs, 6 ) 
	Select CrBxItem1
	Set Order to EmpDopnum
	Seek ( _ChaveDelBx + crBxEst.CPros )
	_BaixaTotal = .T.
	Scan While EmpdopNums + Cpros = _ChaveDelBx + crbxest.Cpros And _QtBaixar > 0
		If crBxEst.cItens <> crBxItem1.cItens
			Loop
		Endif
		_BaixaTotal = .F.
		If _QtBaixar < CrBxItem1.QtBaixas
			Replace CrBxItem1.QtBaixas With crBxItem1.QtBaixas - _QtBaixar
			_QtBaixar = 0
		Else
			_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - QtBaixas
			Replace CrBxItem1.QtBaixas With 0
		EndIf
		llBaixa = Iif(CrBxItem1.Qtds = CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,.t.,.f.)
		lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtBaixas = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,12,3)+[, ChkSubn = ?llBaixa Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem1.CidChaves+[']
		lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
		IF lnErro < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn)')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Endscan
	If !_BaixaTotal
		=ThisForm.PoDatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrEest','EmpDopNums',_ChaveDelbx)
		llsubn = .f.
		llDtBx = Null
		lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvCab Set ChkBxParcs = ?llsubn, ChkSubn = ?llSubn, DtBaixas = ?llDtBx, DataTrans = Null Where CidChaves = ']+CrEest.CidChaves+[']
		lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
		IF lnErro < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 11)')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Endif
	Select crBxEst
Endscan
Return .t.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE chkliberacao
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE chkliberacao
Lparameters ztipo

Do Form SigOpLib With zTipo TO _CodnConf
Return ( _CodnConf )

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE criacursor
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE criacursor
Select crSigCdNec
Select * From CrSigCdNec Where 0=1 Into Cursor TmpNens ReadWrite

Select *, 000000.000 as ps2FaseAnt, Space(3) as cUnips, .f. as OsRets, .f. as Retrabs, Space(14) as MatPrincs,;
	000000.000 as PsFaseAnt, Space(60) as Descs, ;
	0 as Rateio, .f. as Visivel, 000000.000 as QtFaseAnt, 000000 as Amarracao, 00 as TrfPesa, 0 as ServAuto,;
	SPACE(20) as dopcs, 0 as retrab, .f. as NChkSep, 000000.000 as aPesos, .f. as CarCompos ;
From CrSigCdNei Where 1=0 Into Cursor xNensi ReadWrite
Select xNensi
Index On Recno() For Visivel Tag Editar
Index On Cats Tag Cats
Index On Nops Tag Nops
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + Str( Recno(), 10 ) For Rateio # 1 Tag Gravar
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + Str( Rateio, 1 ) Tag Rateio
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats Tag NopCMat
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats + Cats Tag NopMatCat
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats + Cats For Visivel Tag NEnvMCat
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats + TpOps For Visivel Tag NEnvTpops
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats For Visivel Tag NEnvCMat
Index On Str(Nenvs,10) + Str(Nops,10) + cMats Tag nAceite
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats For Visivel Tag NopCMatV && Tiago - 30/01/2013
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats + Str(Amarracao,6) For !Visivel And FlagIncs Tag NopCMatnV && Tiago - 25/04/2016 - Criado índice para usar no botăo de alterar no SigPdMp2 para agregar os componentes
Set Order to Editar

Select * From xNensi Where 0=1 Into Cursor xNensiE ReadWrite
Index On Recno() For Visivel Tag Editar
Index On Cats Tag Cats
Index On Nops Tag Nops
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + Str( Recno(), 10 ) For Rateio # 1 Tag Gravar
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + Str( Rateio, 1 ) Tag Rateio
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats Tag NopCMat
Index On Str(Nops, 10) + CMats + Cats Tag NopMatCat
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats + Cats For Visivel Tag NEnvMCat
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats + TpOps For Visivel Tag NEnvTpops
Index On Str(NEnvs, 10) + CMats For Visivel Tag NEnvCMat
Set Order to Editar

Select * From xNensI Where 0=1 Into Cursor xNensiS ReadWrite
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs

Create Cursor xNensiR (nEnvs n(10), EmpDopNums c(31), Datas t, Destinos c(21), Retrabs c(40), Rclis c(30))
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs

Create Cursor xNensiN (Nops n(10), Cods c(10), Fixos n(1), Descs c(60), Qtds n(12,3), Conta2s c(10))
Index On Nops Tag Nops

Create Cursor xNensiNC (Nenvs n(10), Cods c(10), Descs c(60), Qtds n(12,3), aQtds n(12,3), Usuars c(10))
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs

Create Cursor xNensiP (Nenvs n(10), cMats c(14), Qtds n(12,3), Pesos n(12,3), Cgrus c(3))
Index On Str(Nenvs,10) + cMats Tag Nenvs
Index On Str(Nenvs,10) + Cgrus Tag NenvsCgrus

Create Cursor CsContas (Nenvs n(10), Grupos c(10), Contas c(10) )
Index On Str(Nenvs)+Grupos+Contas Tag NenvGruCon
Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs

Create Cursor xNensiJ (Nenvs n(10), Nops n(10), Cods c(3), Descs c(30), cRetrabs c(6))
Index on Nops Tag Nops

Select *, 0 as Autos, 00000 as BaseMins, 000000.000 as PesoAntigo, Space(30) as DRetrabs, .f. as Justs ;
From CrSigPdMvf where 0=1 Into Cursor xMfas ReadWrite

Select xMFas
Index on Dopes + Str( Numes, 6 ) + Str( Nops ) Tag DopNumOp
Index on Nenvs Tag Nenvs
Index on Nops Tag Nops

Select *, 0 as Autos, 00000 as BaseMins, 000000.000 as PesoAntigo ;
From CrSigPdMvf where 0=1 Into Cursor xMfas2 ReadWrite
Select xMFas2
Index on Nops Tag Nops

Create Cursor xOpi ( Nops n(10), Oper c(31), Qtds n(10,3), CPros c(14), Indiv l, Amarra n(10), ;
					Nenvs n(10), Emps c(3), Dopes c(20), Numes n(6), Conta c(10), Empds c(3), ;
					CodCors c(4), CodTams c(4), cBars n(14), Obrigs l, Divs L, citens n(10) )
Index on Nops tag Nops
Set Order to

Create Cursor xPesa ( cBars n(14), Oper c(31), CPros c(14), Qtds n(10,3), Peso n(10,3), Amarra n(10), Nenvs n(10), Emps c(3), Dopes c(20),;
					  Numes n(6), Nops n(10), Conta c(10), Obs c(10), Cors c(4), Tams c(4), MatPs c(14), Peso2 n(10,3), pesoms n(10,3), ;
					  Usulibs c(10), Pesofixs n(10,3), Especial L, Divs L, CustoFs n(12,3), citens n(10))
Index On Nops Tag Nops
Index on Amarra Tag Amarra
Set Order to 

Create Cursor xMaterial ( Nenvs n(10), Cpros c(14), MatPs c(14))
Index on Nenvs Tag Nenvs

Create Cursor csCabec (EmpDs c(03), Emps c(03), Dopes c(20), Numes n(06), ;
					   MascNum c(10), Datas d(08), GrupoDs c(10), ContaDs c(10), ;
					   GrupoOs c(10), ContaOs c(10), Valos n(12,2), ;
					   ValInis n(12,2), Usuars c(10), TotQtds n(8,2), ;
					   GrVends c(10), Vends c(10), EmpDopNums c(29), Tabdps c(10), ;
					   Gerado c(10), GerEmps c(3), GerDopes c(20), GerNumes n(6), lPrecos c(20)) 
Select csCabec
Index On EmpDopNums Tag EmpDopNum

Create Cursor csItens (CItens n(03), Emps c(03), Dopes c(20), Numes n(06), ;
					   Cpros c(14), Dpros c(40), Reffs c(40), IFors c(10), ;
					   Opers c(01), Moedas c(03), MoeFats c(03), MoeVals n(12,6), ;
					   Qtds n(9,2), AQtds n(9,2), Units n(12,4), Totas n(12,2), ;
					   QtBaixas n(9,2), Fators n(8,3), FatVals N(12,6), cUnips c(3), Moevs c(3), ;
					   Pesos n(9,2), CUnis c(03), UniVals n(12,4), EmpDopNums c(29))
Select csItens
Index On EmpDopNums Tag EmpDopNum

Create Cursor CsEstPe (Codigos n(10), EmpDopNums c(29), Emps c(3), dopes c(20), Numes n(6))
Index on EmpdopNums Tag EmpDopNums

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE delecao
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE delecao
Lparameters _Operacao

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvHst Where OriDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[' ]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvHst 3)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCab)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete    = [Delete From SigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvItn 3)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCpv Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCpv)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvCcr Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crMccr') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrMccr 3)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Select CrMccr
Scan
	=fRecalculaS( CrMccr.Grupos, CrMccr.Contas, CrMccr.Datas, CrMccr.Moedas, ThisForm.Podatamgr  )
EndScan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCcr Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
lnErro = Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
IF lnErro < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCcr)')
	Return .f.
Endif
	
lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvPar Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrPar') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrPar 3)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Store 0 to lnValoBxs

Select crPar
Scan
	lcFpags  = crPar.FPags
	lcCheque = crPar.Bancos + crPar.Agencias + crPar.Contas + crPar.Numeros 
	Thisform.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigOpFp','CrSigOpFp','Fpags',lcFpags)
	If crSigCdOpe.Caixas = 1 And crSigCdOpe.COpers = 2 And ;
			crSigOpFp.ValPends = 1 And !Empty(lcCheque)
		If ThisForm.PoDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPbx','CrPrBx','nCheques',CrPar.Numeros)
			Select CrPrBx
			Index On Bancos + Agencias + NContas + NCheques Tag Ncheques
			=Seek(lcCheque)
			Scan While crPrBx.Bancos+crPrBx.Agencias+crPrBx.NContas+crPrBx.NCheques=lcCheque
				llDep = .t.
				lcUpdate = [UpDate SigCdPbx Set Deposits = ?llDep Where CidChaves = ']+CrPrBx.CidChaves+[']
				lnErro = ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
				IF lnErro < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigCdPbx 2)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			EndScan
		Endif
	EndIf
	lnValoBxs = lnValoBxs + Iif( crSigOpFp.Baixas = 1, Round( xPar.CotFPgs * xPar.Valos, 2 ), 0 )
EndScan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvPar Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvPar)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigTtCcd Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigTtCcd)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigCdCmm Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCdCmm)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcQuery = [Select NumLotes From SigChLcq Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrCheh') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrCheH)')
	Return .f.
Endif

Select CrCheH
Scan
	If NumLotes > 0
		_Lote = NumLotes
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigCheH Where NumLotes = ]+Str(_Lote)
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCheH)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndIf
EndScan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigChLcq Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigChLcq)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCqChm Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrChm') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrChm 3)')
	Return .f.
Endif

Select crChm
Scan
	lcNums   = crChm.Nums
	lcCheque = crChm.Bancos + crChm.Agencias + crChm.NContas + crChm.NCheques
	lcDelete = [Delete From SigCqChm Where CidChaves = ']+CrChm.cidChaves+[']
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCqChm)')
		Return .f.
	Endif
	
	lcWher = [Select * From SigCqChm Where nCheques=']+CrChm.nCheques+[' ]
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWher,'CrChm2')	
	IF lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrChm2)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	_Apaga = .f.
	Select * From CrChm2 where Bancos+Agencias+ncontas+Ncheques=lcCheque And EmpDopNums # _Operacao ;
	Into Cursor CrChm3 ReadWrite
	Index On DtSis Tag DtSis
	If Reccount() = 0
		_Apaga = .t.
	Else
		Go Bott
		lcUMovs      = CrChm3.Codigos
		lcNumCheques = CrChm3.Numeros
	EndIf
	
	lcWher = [Select * From SigChe Where Nums=']+lcNums+[' ]
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWher,'CrChe')	
	IF lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrChe)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	Select crChe
	Index On Bancos + Agencias + nContas + ncheques Tag Cheque
	Seek (lcCheque)
	
	=fCriarCurSit(crChe.Iclis)

	If _Apaga
		insert into crSigExChq (agencias,bancos,vencs,ncheques,ncontas,nums,;
			umovs,valors,contas,grupos,iclis,autos,;
			datatrans,emps,notas,usuars,dataexcls,cidchaves) ;
		values (crche.agencias,crche.bancos,crche.vencs,crche.ncheques,crche.ncontas,crche.nums,;
			crche.umovs,crche.valors,crche.contas,crche.grupos,crche.iclis,crche.autos,;
			datatrans,crche.emps,crche.notas,usuar,_pData, fUniqueIds())

		lcDelete = [Delete From SigChe Where Nums = ']+CrChe.Nums+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigChe)')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Else
		lDtAlt = _pData
		lcUpDate = [Update SigChe Set Umovs = ']+lcUmovs+[', Numeros=']+lcNumCheques+[', ]+;
				   [DtAlts = ?lDtAlt Where Nums = ']+CrChe.nums+[']
		lnErro   = ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
		IF lnErro < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigChe)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		
		lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvPar Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrPar') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrPar 4)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select CrPar
		Index On Bancos + Agencias + Contas + Numeros Tag Cheque
		Scan
			If crPar.Bancos + crPar.Agencias + crPar.Contas + crPar.Numeros = lcCheque
				lcPago = '1'
				ldDat = _pData
				
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvPar Set VPags = 0, Pagos = ?lcPago, DtAlts = ?ldDat ] + ;
						    [Where Cidchaves = '] + CrPar.CidChaves + [']
						    
				If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvPar)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				Exit
			Endif
		EndScan
	EndIf
EndScan
	
lcDelete = [Delete From SigCdCar Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCdCar)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigCdCtt Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCdCtt)')
	Return .f.
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigCdCrd Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCdCrd)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
	
lcDelete = [Delete From SigOpDev Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigOpDev 2)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvPec Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvPec)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvMov Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvMov)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtv Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtv)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvNfi Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Operacao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvNfi)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Return .t.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE exclmov
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE exclmov
LParameters _GravaDel

Local Exclui, Checka, lnnumes, lcCodCors, lcCodTams, lcCodProd, _BxParcial, lcWhere, lcNumChqs
Local lcCheque, lcFPags, lcLoteCart, llDesMarcaCC, llEtiSemHist, lnCfgOpCrs, lcTransacao
Local lcNotas, lcNumCheques, lcUMovs, _ChaveDelBx, _ChaveDelPro, _pData, lnValoBxs, llComTef

lcCidQuery = fUniqueIds()

_pData   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.GetDatetime()
lcUltGrv = TmpEest.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6) + '-Excluir'

Wait Window 'Aguarde. Excluindo Movimentaçőes!!! ' Nowait

Goto Top In TmpEest

=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)
=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigOpCdc','CrSigOpCdc','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)

_Conserto   = ( crSigCdOpe.Consers = 1 )
lcTransacao = 'OP: ' + AllTrim(TmpEest.Emps) + '-' + AllTrim(TmpEest.Dopes) + '-' + AllTrim(Str(TmpEest.Numes,6))
lnCfgOpCrs  = crSigCdOpe.OpCrs
_BxEstpe    = .f.
_BxPagos    = ( CrSigCdOpe.BxPagos = 1 )
_BaixaSn    = ( CrSigCdOpe.BaixaSns = 1 )
llComTef    = .f.
RetNImp     = .f.
Exclui      =.t.

Create Cursor TmpEtiquetas ( CodBarras N(8), Opers C(1) )

Create Cursor TmpBxPends (BxEmps C(3), BxDopes C(20), BxNumes N(6))
Index On BxEmps + BxDopes + Str(BxNumes,6) Tag BxEmpDopN

Create Cursor csTmpOpAut (AutEmps C(3), AutDopes C(20), AutNumes N(6))
Index On AutEmps + AutDopes + Str(AutNumes,6) Tag EmpDopNum

Create Cursor csTmpOpeaut (AutEmps C(3), AutDopes C(20), AutNumes N(6))
Index On AutEmps + AutDopes + Str(AutNumes,6) Tag EmpDopNum

Select TmpEest
Go Top
_Posicao = TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str( TmpEest.Numes, 6 )
lcEDNe   = TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str( TmpEest.Numes, 6 )

If Thisform.pcescolha='EXCLUIR'
	ThisForm.PoDataMgr.cursorQuery('SigMvNfi','CrNfis','EmpDopNums',_posicao)
	Select crNFis
	Go top
	If (ThisForm.PodataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdSer','CrSerie','EmpCods',Thisform.pEmps + crNFis.Series) Or ;
		ThisForm.PodataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdSer','CrSerie','EmpCods',Space(3) + crNFis.Series) )
		If ( crSerie.ImpNfs = 1 AND CrNfis.Impress > 0 ) or ;
				CrSerie.ImpNfs = 3 And MessageBox('Confirma Cancelamento da Nota Fiscal?',4+32,'Atençăo!!!') = 6
			llCanc = .t.
			lcUpdate = [UpDate SigMvNfi Set Cancelas = ?llCanc Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrNfis.EmpdopNums+[']
			lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
			IF lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvNfi)')
				Return .f.
			Endif
		Else
			lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvNfi Where EmpDopNums = ?lcEDNe ]
			lnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
			IF lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvNfi)')
				Return .f.
			Endif
			Select crNfis
			Go top
			If Inlist( crSigCdOpe.NFiscals, 1, 2 ) And !Eof( 'crNFis' )
				=fCanUniqueKey( Val( crNFis.NFis ), TmpEest.Emps + "NOTA FISCAL" + crNFis.Series )
				=fCanUniqueKey( crNFis.Selos, TmpEest.Emps + 'SELO NOTA FISCAL' + crNFis.Series )
			Endif
		Endif
	Endif
Endif
trans   = crSigCdOpe.transs
_BxParc = crSigCdOpe.BxParcials
_BxAuto = crSigCdOpe.BxAutos
	
lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvPec Where EmpDopNums = ']+_posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrEstPe') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrEstPe)')
	Return .f.
Endif

=ThisForm.PodataMgr.cursorQuery('SigMvItn','CrEesti','EmpDopNums',TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str( TmpEest.Numes, 6 ))
=ThisForm.PodataMgr.cursorQuery('SigMvIts','CrEsti2','EmpDopNums',TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str( TmpEest.Numes, 6 ))

Select CrEsti2
Index On Citens Tag Citens
	
Select crEesti
Scan
	If !Empty( crEesti.CodBarras )
		Insert Into TmpEtiquetas ( CodBarras, Opers ) Values ( crEesti.CodBarras, crEesti.Opers )
	Else
		Select crEsti2
		Set Order to Citens
		Set Key to crEesti.CItens
		Scan
			If !Empty( crEsti2.CodBarras )
				Insert Into TmpEtiquetas ( CodBarras, Opers ) ;
						Values ( crEsti2.CodBarras, crEesti.Opers )
			Endif
		EndScan
	EndIf
		
	If Seek(crEesti.CPros, 'csOpeAut', 'CPros') And ;
			Not Seek(TmpEest.Emps + csOpeAut.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6), 'csTmpOpAut', 'EmpDopNum' )
		Insert Into csTmpOpAut( AutEmps, AutDopes, AutNumes ) ;
				Values ( TmpEest.Emps, csOpeAut.Dopes, TmpEest.Numes )
	Endif
	If Seek(crEesti.CPros, 'csOpeTrf', 'Cpros') And ;
			Not Seek(TmpEest.Emps + csOpeTrf.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6), 'csTmpOpeAut', 'EmpDopNum' )
		Insert Into csTmpOpeAut( AutEmps, AutDopes, AutNumes ) ;
				Values ( TmpEest.Emps, csOpetrf.Dopes, TmpEest.Numes )
	Endif

	lcEmp = Iif(Empty(crSigCdOpe.EmpPads),TmpEest.Emps,crSigCdOpe.EmpPads)

	If crSigCdOpe.Consers = 1 And !Empty(crSigCdPam.OpConsers) And ;
			Not Seek(lcEmp + crSigCdPam.OpConsers + crEesti.Notas, 'csTmpOpAut', 'EmpDopNum' )
		Insert Into csTmpOpAut( AutEmps, AutDopes, AutNumes ) ;
				Values ( LcEmp, crSigCdPam.OpConsers, Val(crEesti.Notas) )
	Endif

	If CrSigOpCdc.InibePa = 3 And ;
			Not Seek(lcEmp + csOpeAut.Dopes + crEesti.Notas, 'csTmpOpAut', 'EmpDopNum' )
		Insert Into csTmpOpAut( AutEmps, AutDopes, AutNumes ) ;
				Values ( LcEmp, csOpeAut.Dopes, Val(crEesti.Notas) )
	Endif

EndScan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = ?lcEDNe ]
lnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
IF lnErro < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvItn)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

If _BxParc = 1 Or _Bxauto = 1 Or _BxParc = 3

	lcQuery = [Select distinct EmpdopNumb From SigBxEst Where EmpDopNums = ?lcEDNe ]
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrBxIt') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxIt)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select CrSigGtmpR
	Zap
	
	Select CrBxIt
	Scan
		Select CrSigGtmpR
		Append Blank
		Replace EmpDopNums With CrBxIt.EmpDopNumb,;
				CidQuerys  With lcCidQuery,;
				CidChaves  With fUniqueIds()
	EndScan
	
	If !ThisForm.Podatamgr4.UpDate('CrSigGtmpR')
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr4.RollBack()
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrSigGtmpR 3)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	If ThisForm.PoDataMgr4.commit() < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Commit 4)')
		Return .f.
	Endif

	lcQuery = [Select b.EmpdopNums,b.Cpros,b.CodBarras,b.QtBaixas,b.cidChaves,b.citens,b.Qtds,b.QtProds,b.QtReservas ]+;
				[From SigMvItn b, CptGTmpd a ]+;
			  [Where a.CidQuerys = '] + lcCidQuery + [' And a.EmpDopNums = b.EmpDopNums ]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrBxItem1') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxItem1)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	lcQuery = [Select b.EmpDopNums, b.Citens, b.Cpros, b.CodCors, b.CodTams, b.QtBaixas, b.CidChaves, b.QtdEmbs, b.Qtds,b.QtProds,b.QtReservas,b.CodEmbs From cptgtmpd a, SigMvIts b ]+;
			  [Where a.CidQuerys = '] + lcCidQuery + [' And a.EmpDopNums = b.EmpDopNums ]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrBxItem2') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrBxItem2)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	ThisForm.PodataMgr4.fSqlApagarTmp('CptGTmpD', lcCidquery )

	Select CrBxItem1
	Index On EmpDopNums + Cpros Tag EmpDopNum
	
	Select CrBxItem2
	Index On EmpdopNums + Cpros + CodCors + CodTams Tag EmpDopc
	Index On EmpDopNums + Str(Citens,4) Tag EmpDopNum
	
	=ThisForm.PoDataMgr.cursorquery('SigBxEst','CrBxEst','EmpDopNums',lcEDNe)

Endif

If _BxParc = 1 Or _BxAuto = 1
	
	Select crBxEst
	Scan
		_BxEstpe = .t.
		If Not Seek('','TmpBxPends','BxEmpDopN')
			Insert Into TmpBxPends (BxEmps, BxDopes, BxNumes) Values ;
				(crBxEst.EmpBs, crBxEst.DopeBs, crBxEst.NumeBs)
		Endif
		_QtBaixar  = crBxEst.Qtdes
		_ChaveDelBx = crBxEst.Empbs + crbxest.Dopebs + Str( crbxest.Numebs, 6 ) 
		If Empty(crBxEst.CodCors) And Empty(crBxEst.CodTams) AND EMPTY(CrBxEst.CodEmbs)
			Select CrBxItem1
			Set Order to EmpDopnum
			Seek ( _ChaveDelBx + crBxEst.CPros )
			_BaixaTotal = .T.
			Scan While EmpdopNums + Cpros = _ChaveDelBx + crbxest.Cpros And _QtBaixar > 0
				If CrSigCdOpe.ChkQtdss = 3 And crBxEst.CodBarras # crBxItem1.Codbarras
					Loop
				Endif
				_BaixaTotal = .F.
				If _QtBaixar < CrBxItem1.QtBaixas
					_Saldo = crBxItem1.QtBaixas - _QtBaixar
					Replace CrBxItem1.QtBaixas With Iif(_Saldo < 0, 0, _Saldo)
					_QtBaixar = 0
				Else
					_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - QtBaixas
					Replace CrBxItem1.QtBaixas With 0
				EndIf
				llBaixa = Iif(CrBxItem1.Qtds = CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,.t.,.f.)
				lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtBaixas = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,12,3)+[, ChkSubn = ?llBaixa Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem1.CidChaves+[']
				lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
				IF lnErro < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn)')
					Return .f.
				Endif
			Endscan
 			Else
			Select CrBxItem2
			Set Order to EmpDopNum
			Seek ( _ChaveDelBx + Str(crBxEst.CItens,4) )
			_BaixaTotal = .T.
			Scan While CrBxItem2.EmpDopNums + Str(CrBxItem2.CItens,4) = _ChaveDelBx + Str(crBxEst.CItens,4) And _QtBaixar > 0
				If CrBxItem2.CPros + CrBxItem2.CodCors + CrBxItem2.CodTams + CrBxItem2.CodEmbs # crBxEst.CPros + crBxEst.CodCors + crBxEst.CodTams + CrBxEst.CodEmbs
					Loop
				EndIf
				_BaixaTotal = .F.
				_QtBaixado = 0
				If _QtBaixar < CrBxItem2.QtBaixas
					_Saldo = CrBxItem2.QtBaixas - _QtBaixar
					Replace CrBxItem2.QtBaixas With Iif(_Saldo < 0,0,_Saldo)
					_QtBaixado = _QtBaixar * CrBxItem2.QtdEmbs
					_QtBaixar = 0
				Else
					_QtBaixado = _QtBaixar * CrBxItem2.QtdEmbs
					_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - CrBxItem2.QtBaixas
					Replace CrBxItem2.QtBaixas With 0
				EndIf
				llBaixa = Iif(CrBxItem2.Qtds=CrBxItem2.QtBaixas,.t.,.f.)
				lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvIts Set QtBaixas = ]+Str(CrBxItem2.QtBaixas,12,3)+[, ChkSubn = ?llBaixa Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem2.CidChaves+[']
				lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
				IF lnErro < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvIts)')
					Return .f.
				Endif
				
				Select CrBxItem1
				Set Order to EmpDopNum
				Seek ( CrBxItem2.EmpDopNums)
				Do While CrBxItem1.EmpDopNums = CrBxItem2.EmpDopNums And _QtBaixado > 0
					If CrBxItem1.CItens = crBxItem2.CItens
						Select CrBxItem1
						_Saldo = CrBxItem1.QtBaixas - _QtBaixado
						Replace CrBxItem1.QtBaixas With Iif(_Saldo<0,0,_Saldo)
						_QtBaixado = 0
						llBaixa = Iif(CrBxItem1.Qtds=CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,.t.,.f.)
						lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtBaixas = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtBaixas,12,3)+[, ChkSubn = ?llBaixa Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem1.CidChaves+[']
						lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
						IF lnErro < 1
							MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn 2)')
							Return .f.
						Endif
					EndIf
					Skip
				EndDo
				Select CrBxItem2
			Endscan
		EndIf

		If !_BaixaTotal
			=ThisForm.PoDatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrEest','EmpDopNums',_ChaveDelbx)
			llsubn = .f.
			llDtBx = Null
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvCab Set ChkBxParcs = ?llsubn, ChkSubn = ?llSubn, DtBaixas = ?llDtBx, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where CidChaves = ']+CrEest.CidChaves+[']
			lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
			IF lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 11)')
				Return .f.
			Endif

			lcUpdate = [Update SigMvEte Set ChkSubn = ?llSubn Where EmpDopNums = ']+_ChaveDelbx+[']
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr6.PnIdConn  > 0
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr6.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			Else
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			EndIf
			If LnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvEte)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf

			If Seek(CrEest.Dopes,'CrSigCdMei','Dopes')
				lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtt Where EmpdopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpDopNums+[']
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
				If lnErro < 0
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtt - Excluir 1)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			Endif

		Endif

		Select crBxEst

	Endscan
	
	If _GravaDel
		Select TmpBxPends
		Scan
			Select CrBxItem1
			Set Order to EmpDopNum
			Seek TmpBxPends.BxEmps + TmpBxPends.BxDopes + Str(TmpBxPends.BxNumes,6)
			_BxParcial = .F.
			Scan While EmpDopNums = TmpBxPends.BxEmps + TmpBxPends.BxDopes + Str(TmpBxPends.BxNumes,6) And Not _BxParcial
				If CrBxItem1.QtBaixas # 0
					_BxParcial = .T.
				EndIf
			Endscan
			=ThisForm.PoDatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrEest','EmpDopNums',TmpBxPends.BxEmps + TmpBxPends.BxDopes + Str(TmpBxPends.BxNumes,6))
			llsubn = _bxParcial
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvCab Set ChkBxParcs = ?llsubn, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where CidChaves = ']+CrEest.CidChaves+[']
			lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
			IF lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 12)')
				Return .f.
			Endif
			If Seek(CrEest.Dopes,'CrSigCdMei','Dopes')
				lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtt Where EmpdopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
				If lnErro < 0
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtt - excluir 2)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			Endif
		EndScan
	Endif
Else
	If _BxParc = 3
		Select crBxEst
		Scan 
			_ChaveDelBx = crbxest.Empbs + crbxest.Dopebs + Str( crbxest.Numebs, 6 ) 
			_QtBaixar   = crBxEst.QtdFs
			If Empty(crBxEst.CodCors) And Empty(crBxEst.CodTams) AND EMPTY(CrBxEst.CodEmbs)
				Select CrBxItem1
				Set Order to EmpDopNum
				=Seek( _ChaveDelBx + crbxest.Cpros )
				_BaixaTotal = .T.
				Scan While CrBxItem1.EmpDopNums + crBxItem1.Cpros = _ChaveDelBx + crbxest.Cpros And _QtBaixar > 0
					_BaixaTotal = .F.
					If _QtBaixar < CrBxItem1.QtProds
						Replace CrBxItem1.QtProds With CrBxItem1.QtProds - _QtBaixar,;
								CrBxItem1.QtReservas With CrBxItem1.QtReservas - _QtBaixar
						_QtBaixar = 0
					Else
						_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - crBxItem1.QtProds
						Replace CrBxItem1.Qtprods With 0,;
								CrBxItem1.QtReservas With 0
					Endif
					lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtProds = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtProds,12,2)+[, QtReservas = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtReservas,12,2)+[ ]+;
							   [Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem1.CidChaves+[']
					lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
					IF lnErro < 1
						MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn 3)')
						Return .f.
					Endif
				Endscan
			Else
				Select CrBxItem2
				Set Order to EmpDopc
				Seek ( _ChaveDelBx + crBxEst.CPros + crBxEst.CodCors + crBxEst.CodTams )
				_BaixaTotal = .T.
				Scan While CrBxItem2.EmpDopNums + CrBxItem2.Cpros + crBxItem2.CodCors + CrBxItem2.CodTams = _ChaveDelBx + crbxest.Cpros + crBxEst.CodCors + crBxEst.CodTams And _QtBaixar > 0
					_BaixaTotal = .F.
					_QtBaixado = 0
					If CrBxItem2.QtProds = 0
						Loop
					Endif
					If _QtBaixar < CrBxItem2.QtProds
						Replace crBxItem2.QtProds With CrBxItem2.QtProds - _QtBaixar,;
								CrBxItem2.QtReservas With CrBxItem2.QtReservas - _QtBaixar
						_QtBaixado = _QtBaixar * CrBxItem2.QtdEmbs
						_QtBaixar = 0
					Else
						_QtBaixado = _QtBaixar * CrBxItem2.QtdEmbs
						_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - CrBxItem2.QtProds
						Replace CrBxItem2.QtProds With 0,;
								CrBxItem2.QtReservas With 0
					Endif
					lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvIts Set QtProds = ]+Str(CrBxItem2.QtProds,12,2)+[, QtReservas = ]+Str(CrBxItem2.QtReservas,12,2)+[ ]+;
							   [Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem2.CidChaves+[']
					lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
					IF lnErro < 1
						MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvIts 2)')
						Return .f.
					Endif

					Select CrBxItem1
					Set Order to EmpDopNum
					Seek ( CrBxItem2.EmpDopNums )
					Do While CrBxItem1.EmpDopNums = CrBxItem2.EmpdopNums And _QtBaixado > 0
						If CrBxItem1.CItens = CrBxItem2.CItens
							Select CrBxItem1
							Replace CrBxItem1.QtProds With CrBxItem1.QtProds - _QtBaixado,;
									CrBxItem1.QtReservas With CrBxItem1.QtReservas - _QtBaixado
							_QtBaixado = 0
							lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtProds = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtProds,12,2)+[, QtReservas = ]+Str(CrBxItem1.QtReservas,12,2)+[ ]+;
									   [Where CidChaves = ']+CrBxItem1.CidChaves+[']
							lnErro   = ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'')
							IF lnErro < 1
								MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn 4)')
								Return .f.
							Endif
						EndIf
						Skip
					EndDo
					Select CrBxItem2
				EndScan
			EndIf
			Select crBxEst
		EndScan
	Endif	
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvIts Where EmpDopNums = ?lcEDNe ]
lnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
IF lnErro < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvIts)')

lcSql = [Select * From SigOpPii Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEDNe+[']
Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalOpiC')

Select LocalOpiC
Scan
	lcSql = [Select * From SigOpPic where Nops = ]+Str(LocalOpiC.Nops)
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpOpi')
	
	Select TmpOpi
	Scan
		pIds = TmpOpi.cidchaves
		If Empds + Dopes + Str(Numes,6) = LocalOpic.EmpOs + LocalOpic.DopeOs + Str(LocalOpic.NumeOs,6)
			Replace Qtds With Qtds + LocalOpic.Qtds in TmpOpi
			lcSql = [Update SigOpPic Set Qtds = ]+Str(TmpOpi.Qtds,12,3)+[ Where Cidchaves = ']+pids+[']
			ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'')
		Else
			If Empds + Dopes + Str(Numes,6) = LocalOpic.EmpDs + LocalOpic.DopeDs + Str(LocalOpic.NumeDs,6)
				Delete In TmpOpi
				lcSql = [Delete From SigOpPic Where Cidchaves = ']+pids+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'')
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndScan
EndScan

=ThisForm.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrEest','EmpDopNums',tmpeest.emps + tmpeest.Dopes + str( tmpeest.numes, 6 ))
lcOldEmpds = crEest.Empds
Set Step On 
If crSigCdOpe.Transs = 3 And (Not IsEmpty(crSigCdOpe.DopesTrfs) Or (Not IsEmpty(crSigCdOpe.DopeETrfs) And Not IsEmpty(crSigCdOpe.EmpPads)))
	lcEmpDopNum2 = TmpEest.Emps + CrSigCdOpe.DopeETrfs + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6)
	lcQuery = [Select Emps, Empds, Dopes, Numes From SigMvCab Where Not EmpDs = ']+Space(3)+[' ] +;
			  [And Empds = ']+TmpEest.Emps+[' and Dopes = ']+CrSigCdOpe.DopesTrfs+[' And Numes = ]+Str(TmpEest.Numes,6)+[]+;
			  [Union All ] +;
			  [Select Emps, EmpDs, Dopes, Numes From SigMvCab Where ]+;
			  [EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum2+[' And EmpDs = ']+CrSigCdOpe.EmpPads+[']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CsTmpTrfs') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CsTmpTrfs)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select csTmpTrfs
	
	Scan
		lcEmpDopNum = csTmpTrfs.Emps + csTmpTrfs.Dopes + Str(csTmpTrfs.Numes,6)
		lcDelete    = [Delete From SigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvItn 2)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
*!*			lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.Emps+[']
		lcQuery = [Select Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.Emps+[']
		
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crhis') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHis 2)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select CrHis
		Scan
			lcOldEmpds = csTmpTrfs.Emps
			_Data      = crhis.datas
			_CPro      = crhis.cpros
			_Grup      = crhis.grupos
			_Estq      = crhis.estos
			_Cor       = crhis.codcors
			_Tam       = crhis.codtams
			=SqlCalcP2( lcOldEmpds, _grup, _estq, _cpro, _data, _Cor, _Tam, ThisForm.Podatamgr  )

			=fRecalculaC(lcOldEmpDs, _CPro, _Data, Thisform.Podatamgr ) 
		EndScan
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.emps+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvHst 2)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcDelete = [Delete From SigOpEtq Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigOpEtq)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcEmpDopNum = ( csTmpTrfs.EmpDs + csTmpTrfs.Dopes + Str(csTmpTrfs.Numes,6) )
*!*			lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.Emps+[']
		lcQuery = [Select Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.Emps+[']		
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crhis') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHis 3)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		
		Select crHis
		Scan
			lcOldEmpds = csTmpTrfs.EmpDs
			_Data      = crhis.datas
			_CPro      = crhis.cpros
			_Grup      = crhis.grupos
			_Estq      = crhis.estos
			_Cor       = crhis.codcors
			_Tam       = crhis.codtams
			=SqlCalcP2( lcOldEmpds, _grup, _estq, _cpro, _data, _Cor, _Tam, ThisForm.Podatamgr)

			=fRecalculaC(lcOldEmpDs, _CPro, _Data, Thisform.Podatamgr )
		EndScan
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvHst Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' And Empos = ']+CsTmpTrfs.emps+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvHst 3)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcEmpDopNum = csTmpTrfs.Emps + csTmpTrfs.Dopes + Str(csTmpTrfs.Numes,6)
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCab)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndScan			
EndIf

If ( crSigCdOpe.Transs = 5 And Not IsEmpty(crSigCdOpe.DopesTrfs) ) Or InList(CrSigOpCdc.GerOpes,1,2)
	lcEmpDopNum2 = TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6)
	lcSql = [Select EmpDnCrds, EmpDopNums From SigMvCab Where EmpDnCrds = ']+lcEmpDopNum2+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'CsTmpTrfs') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CsTmpTrfs)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select csTmpTrfs
	Scan
		lcEmpDopNum = csTmpTrfs.EmpDopNums
		lcQuery = [Select Datas,Cpros,Grupos,Estos,CodCors,CodTams,Emps From SigMvHst Where OriDopNums = ']+lcEmpDopNum+[' ]
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrHis') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHis 2)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select CrHis
		Scan
			=SqlCalcP2( CrHis.Emps, CrHis.Grupos, CrHis.Estos, CrHis.Cpros, CrHis.Datas, CrHis.CodCors, CrHis.CodTams, ThisForm.Podatamgr  )
			=fRecalculaC( CrHis.Emps, CrHis.Cpros, CrHis.Datas, ThisForm.Podatamgr  ) 
		EndScan
		
		If Not ThisForm.Delecao( lcEmpDopNum )
			Return .f.
		Endif

	EndScan
Else
	lcSql = [Select EmpDnCrds, EmpDopNums From SigMvCab Where 0=1]
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'CsTmpTrfs') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CsTmpTrfs)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
Select CsTmpTrfs
Index On EmpDopNums Tag EmpDopNums

=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)
If crSigCdOpe.Estoqs = 1 Or CrSigCdOpe.Dopes = CrSigCdPam.TransfEncs
	Select TmpEtiquetas
	Scan
		If ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigOpEtq','CrEti','Cbars',TmpEtiquetas.Codbarras)
			Select crEti
			If (crEti.Emps + crEti.Dopes + Str(crEti.Numes,6) = TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6))
				If ( Thisform.pcescolha = 'ALTERAR' ) And ( crSigOpCdc.AltEtiqs = 1 )
					Select xEesti
					Set Order to CodBarras
					Seek (TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras)
					If Eof()
						lcDelete = [Delete From SigOpEtq Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
						If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
							=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigOpEtq)')
							Return .f.
						EndIf
					EndIf
					Select xEesti
					Set Order to
				Else
					lcDelete = [Delete From SigOpEtq Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,' ') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigOpEtq 2)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
				EndIf
			Else
				Store Space(10) to _GrupoEti, _ContaEti, _DopeHis
				_DataEti  = Null
				_EmposEti = crEti.Empos
				
				lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvHst Where CodBarras = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,8)+[ Order By Seqs Desc ]
				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crhis') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHis 4)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				Select crHis
				llEtiSemHist = Eof('crHis')
				Entra = .F.
				Scan
					_EmposEti = crHis.Emps
					Entra = .T.
					
					If crHis.OriDopNums = Tmpeest.Emps + Tmpeest.Dopes + Str( Tmpeest.Numes, 6 )
						Loop
					Endif
					
					If crSigCdOpe.Transs = 3 And Not Empty(crSigCdOpe.DopeETrfs) And ;
							crHis.Dopes = crSigCdOpe.DopeETrfs And ;
							crHis.Numes = TmpEest.Numes And ;
							crHis.Empos = TmpEest.Emps And ;
							( crHis.Emps = TmpEest.Emps Or crHis.Emps = TmpEest.EmpDs )
						Loop
					EndIf
					If CrSigCdOpe.Transs = 5 And Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.DopeStrfs)
						If Seek(CrHis.OriDopNums,'CsTmpTrfs','EmpDopNums')
							Loop
						Endif
					Endif

					_DopeHis = CrHis.Dopes
						
					If crHis.Opers = 'S'
						Exit
					Endif

					If crHis.Opers = 'E'
						_GrupoEti = crHis.Grupos
						_ContaEti = crHis.Estos
						_DataEti  = crHis.Datas
						Exit
					Endif
				Endscan
				
				llDtMov = _pData
				If Entra
					lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdMlc Where Barras = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,8)+[ Order By Datas Desc ]
					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrMloc') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrMLoc)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					Select crMloc
					Go Top
					
					lcSql = [Select AltEtiqs From SigOpCdc Where dopes = ']+TmpEest.Dopes+[']
					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql, 'CrDop') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrDop)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					If InList(CrDop.AltEtiqs,3,4)
						If Not Inlist(crSigCdOpe.CupFis,1)
							lcSql = [Select a.Pesos, a.Qtds, a.Cidchaves, a.Opers, b.dopes, b.AltEtiqs From SigMvHst a, SigOpCdc b ]+;
									[Where a.CodBarras = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.Codbarras,8)+[ And a.Dopes = b.Dopes ]+;
									[And a.oriDopNums <> ']+TmpEest.EmpDopNums+[' ]+;
									[Order by a.CidChaves Desc ]
							If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql, 'CrHisEtq') < 1)
								=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHisEtq)')
								Return .f.
							EndIf
							Select CrHisEtq
							Go Top
							DO While !Eof()
								If Not InList(AltEtiqs,3,4)
									Exit
								EndIf
								Skip
							EndDo
							If Eof()
								Go bott
							Endif
							Replace Qtds  With CrHisEtq.Qtds,;
									Pesos With CrHisEtq.Pesos in CrEti
							aQtd = CrEti.Qtds
							aPes = CrEti.Pesos
							If Reccount('CrHisEtq') > 0
								Skip -1
							Endif
							DO While !Bof()
								If AltEtiqs = 4
									Replace Qtds  With Qtds  + (crHisEtq.Qtds  * Iif(CrHisEtq.Opers='E',1,-1)),;
											Pesos With Pesos + (crHisEtq.Pesos * Iif(crHisEtq.Opers='E',1,-1)) In CrEti
								Else
									Replace Qtds   With CrHisEtq.Qtds  ,;
											Pesos  With CrHisEtq.Pesos ,;
											aQtds  With aQtd,;
											aPesos With aPes In CrEti
								EndIf
								Skip -1
								If Not Bof()
									aQtd = CrEti.Qtds
									aPes = CrEti.Pesos
								Endif
							EndDo
						
							lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set ]+Iif(CrDop.AltEtiqs=4,[],[Grupos=']+_GrupoEti+[', Contas=']+_ContaEti+[', ])+;
									   [Empos=']+_EmposEti+[', Qtds = ]+Str(CrEti.Qtds,12,3)+[, Pesos = ]+Str(CrEti.Pesos,12,3)+[, ]+;
									   [aQtds = ]+Str(CrEti.aQtds,12,3)+[, aPesos  = ]+Str(CrEti.aPesos,12,3)+[, ]+;
									   [Datas=?_DataEti, DtMovs=?llDtMov, Localizas =']+Crmloc.LocNews+[' ]+;
									   [Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
						Else
							lcSql = [Select a.Pesos,a.Qtds,a.Cidchaves,a.Opers,b.dopes,a.Grupos,a.Estos,b.AltEtiqs From SigMvHst a, SigOpCdc b ]+;
									[Where a.CodBarras = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.Codbarras,8)+[ And a.Dopes = b.Dopes ]+;
									[And a.OriDopNums = ']+TmpEest.EmpDopNums+[' ]+;
									[Order by a.CidChaves Desc ]
							If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql, 'CrHisEtq') < 1)
								=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHisEtq)')
								Return .f.
							EndIf
							Select CrHisEtq
							Go Top
							_GrupoEti = CrHisEtq.Grupos
							_ContaEti = CrHisEtq.Estos

							Replace Qtds  With Qtds + CrHisEtq.Qtds In CrEti
							lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set Grupos=']+_GrupoEti+[', Contas=']+_ContaEti+[', ]+;
									   [Qtds = ]+Str(CrEti.Qtds,12,3)+[, ]+;
									   [Datas=?_DataEti, DtMovs=?llDtMov, Localizas =']+Crmloc.LocNews+[' ]+;
									   [Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
						Endif
					Else
						lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set Grupos=']+_GrupoEti+[', Contas=']+_ContaEti+[', Empos=']+_EmposEti+[', ]+;
								   [Datas=?_DataEti, DtMovs=?llDtMov, Localizas =']+Crmloc.LocNews+[' Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
					Endif
					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,' ') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigOpEtq)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					
				Else
					If llEtiSemHist	And TmpEtiquetas.Opers = 'E' && Etiqueta sem Histórico, Marca Etiqueta como Vendida
						llDtMov = _pData
						lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set Grupos=']+Space(10)+[', Contas=']+Space(10)+[', Empos=']+CrEti.Emps+[', ]+;
								   [DtMovs=?llDtMov Where cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
						If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,' ') < 1)
							=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigOpEtq 2)')
							Return .f.
						EndIf
					EndIf
				EndIf
			Endif
		Endif
		Select TmpEtiquetas
	EndScan
EndIf

Select TmpEtiquetas
Scan
	If Thisform.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigOpEtq','CrEti','Cbars',TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras)
		lcQuery = [Select dopes,datas,seqs,codbarras From SigMvHst Where CodBarras = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,8)+[ And OriDopNums <> ']+TmpEest.empDopNums+[' Order By Seqs Desc ]
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crhis') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrHis 5)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select crHis
		Go Top
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',crhis.Dopes)
		If InList(crSigCdOpe.DtBars,1,2)
			llDtBal  = Iif(crSigCdOpe.DtBars = 1, crHis.Datas, Null)
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set DtBals = ?llDtBal Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,' ') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigOpEtq 3)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		Else
			lcQuery = [Select a.Codbarras, b.Datas, a.Dopes From SigMvItn a, SigMvCab b ]+;
					  [Where a.CodBarras=]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,8)+[ And a.EmpDopNums=b.EmpDopNums Order By b.Datas Desc ]
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalEesti') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalEesti 3)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
			Select LocalEesti
			Scan
				=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',LocalEesti.Dopes)
				If InList(crSigCdOpe.DtBars,1,2)
					llDtBal  = Iif(crSigCdOpe.DtBars = 1, LocalEesti.Datas, Null)
					lcUpDate = [UpDate SigOpEtq Set DtBals = ?llDtBal Where Cbars = ]+Str(TmpEtiquetas.CodBarras,14)
					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,' ') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigOpEtq 4)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					Exit
				Endif
			EndScan
		EndIf
	Endif
EndScan

Store 0 to lnValoBxs

Select crPar
Scan
	lcFpags  = crPar.FPags
	lcCheque = crPar.Bancos + crPar.Agencias + crPar.Contas + crPar.Numeros 
	Thisform.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigOpFp','CrSigOpFp','Fpags',lcFpags)
	If crSigCdOpe.Caixas = 1 And crSigCdOpe.COpers = 2 And ;
			crSigOpFp.ValPends = 1 And !Empty(lcCheque)
		If ThisForm.PoDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPbx','CrPrBx','nCheques',CrPar.Numeros)
			Select CrPrBx
			Index On Bancos + Agencias + NContas + NCheques Tag Ncheques
			=Seek(lcCheque)
			Scan While crPrBx.Bancos+crPrBx.Agencias+crPrBx.NContas+crPrBx.NCheques=lcCheque
				llDep = .t.
				lcUpdate = [UpDate SigCdPbx Set Deposits = ?llDep Where CidChaves = ']+CrPrBx.CidChaves+[']
				lnErro = ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
				IF lnErro < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigCdPbx 2)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			EndScan
		Endif
	EndIf
	lnValoBxs = lnValoBxs + Iif( crSigOpFp.Baixas = 1, Round( xPar.CotFPgs * xPar.Valos, 2 ), 0 )
EndScan

Select crChm
Scan
	lcNums   = crChm.Nums
	lcCheque = crChm.Bancos + crChm.Agencias + crChm.NContas + crChm.NCheques
	lcDelete = [Delete From SigCqChm Where CidChaves = ']+CrChm.cidChaves+[']
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigCqChm)')
		Return .f.
	Endif
	
	lcWher = [Select * From SigCqChm Where nCheques=']+CrChm.nCheques+[' ]
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWher,'CrChm2')	
	IF lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrChm2)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	_Apaga = .f.
	Select * From CrChm2 where Bancos+Agencias+ncontas+Ncheques=lcCheque And EmpDopNums # _Posicao ;
	Into Cursor CrChm3 ReadWrite
	Index On DtSis Tag DtSis
	If Reccount() = 0
		_Apaga = .t.
	Else
		Go Bott
		lcUMovs      = CrChm3.Codigos
		lcNumCheques = CrChm3.Numeros
	EndIf
	
	lcWher = [Select * From SigChe Where Nums=']+lcNums+[' ]
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWher,'CrChe')	
	IF lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrChe)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	Select crChe
	Index On Bancos + Agencias + nContas + ncheques Tag Cheque
	Seek (lcCheque)
	
	=fCriarCurSit(crChe.Iclis)

	If _Apaga
		insert into crSigExChq (agencias,bancos,vencs,ncheques,ncontas,nums,;
			umovs,valors,contas,grupos,iclis,autos,;
			datatrans,emps,notas,usuars,dataexcls,cidchaves) ;
		values (crche.agencias,crche.bancos,crche.vencs,crche.ncheques,crche.ncontas,crche.nums,;
			crche.umovs,crche.valors,crche.contas,crche.grupos,crche.iclis,crche.autos,;
			datatrans,crche.emps,crche.notas,usuar,_pData, fUniqueIds())

		lcDelete = [Delete From SigChe Where Nums = ']+CrChe.Nums+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigChe)')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Else
		lDtAlt = _pData
		lcUpDate = [Update SigChe Set Umovs = ']+lcUmovs+[', Numeros=']+lcNumCheques+[', ]+;
				   [DtAlts = ?lDtAlt Where Nums = ']+CrChe.nums+[']
		lnErro   = ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
		IF lnErro < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigChe)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		
		lcQuery = [Select * From SigMvPar Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrPar') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrPar 4)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select CrPar
		Index On Bancos + Agencias + Contas + Numeros Tag Cheque
		Scan
			If crPar.Bancos + crPar.Agencias + crPar.Contas + crPar.Numeros = lcCheque
				lcPago = '1'
				ldDat = _pData
				
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvPar Set VPags = 0, Pagos = ?lcPago, DtAlts = ?ldDat ] + ;
						    [Where Cidchaves = '] + CrPar.CidChaves + [']
						    
				If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvPar)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				Exit
			Endif
		EndScan
	EndIf
EndScan
