Select crDevol
Scan
	If Not Empty(crDevol.Codigos)
		Set Decimals to 0
		nDope = Val( Left( Str( crDevol.Codigos, 10 ), 4 ) )
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','ndopes',nDope)
		Dope = crSigCdOpe.Dopes
		Nume    = Val( Right( Str( crDevol.Codigos, 10 ), 6 ) )
		lcNotas = Transf(Nume,'@L 999999')
		Set Decimals to 2
		If lnCfgOpCrs = 1
			Declare LaCampo(1,2)
			LaCampo(1,1)='EmpDopNums'
			LaCampo(1,2)=TmpEest.Emps + Dope + Str(Nume,6)
		Else
			If lnCfgOpCrs = 3
				Declare LaCampo(2,2)
				LaCampo(1,1)='Dopes'
				LaCampo(2,1)='Notas'
				LaCampo(1,2)=Dope
				laCampo(2,2)=lcNotas
			Endif
		EndIf
		If InList(lnCfgOpCrs,1,3) And ThisForm.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrTmpEest',@LaCampo)
			lcSubn = .f.
			ldDtAlt= _pData
			llDtBx = Null
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvCab Set ChkSubn = ?lcSubn, ChkBxParcs = ?lcSubn, DtAlts = ?ldDtAlt, DtBaixas = ?llDtBx, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where CidChaves = ']+CrTmpEest.CidChaves+[']
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 13)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf

			lcUpdate = [Update SigMvEte Set ChkSubn = ?lcSubn Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrTmpEest.EmpDopNums+[']
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr6.PnIdConn  > 0
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr6.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			Else
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			EndIf
			If lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvEte )')
				Return .f.
			EndIf

			If Seek(CrTmpEest.Dopes,'CrSigCdMei','Dopes')
				lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtt Where EmpdopNums = ']+CrTmpEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
				If lnErro < 0
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtt - excluir 3)')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			Endif
		Else
			If InList( lnCfgOpCrs, 1, 3 )
				lcTransacao = lcTransacao + Iif( lnCfgOpCrs = 1, 'CR: ' + AllTrim(TmpEest.Emps) + ;
							 '-' + AllTrim(Dope) + '-' + AllTrim(Str(Nume)), ;
							Iif( lnCfgOpCrs = 3, 'CR: ' + AllTrim(Dope) + '-' + lcNotas, ;
							'Configuraçăo OpCrs: ' + AllTrim(Str(lnCfgOpCrs)) ) )
				fGravarLog( 'X', TmpEest.Dopes, Thisform.pcescolha, lcTransacao )
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndIf
EndScan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigOpDev Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigOpDev 2)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

If Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.nOpCrs)  &&CrSigCdOpe.OpCrs = 5 And Exclusăo da Operaçăo de crédito
	lcSql = [Select CidChaves,empDnCrds,EmpDopNums from SigMvCab where EmpDnCrds = ']+_Posicao+[']
	If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'Tmp') < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCab (Tmp))')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	Select Tmp
	Scan
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCab Where CidChaves = ']+Tmp.CidChaves+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCab (Excluir OpCr))')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvPec Where EmpDopNums = ']+Tmp.EmpDopNums+[']
		If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvPec (Excluir Opcr))')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndScan
Endif

If Used('csTmpCart')
	Select csTmpCart
	Scan
		llDesMarcaCC = .T.
 		lcWhere = [Select Cidchaves, obses From SigCdCtt Where ncarts = ]+Str(CsTmpCart.Ncarts,10)+[ And Emps = ']+CsTmpCart.Empos+[']
		If ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWhere,'CrTmpCart') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrTmpCart 3)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select CrTmpCart
		Go Top
		If Not IsEmpty(CrTmpCart.Obses)
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigCdCtt Set Obses = Null Where CidChaves = ']+CrTmpCart.CidChaves+[']
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigCdCtt 2)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
	 		lcWhere = [Select Cidchaves, obses From SigCdCtt Where nLotecs = ]+Str(crTmpCart.nLoteCs,10)+[ And Emps = ']+CrTmpCart.Emps+[']
			If ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWhere,'CrCart') < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrCart 2)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
			Select CrCart
			Go Top
			Scan While llDesMarcaCC
				If Not IsEmpty(CrCart.Obses)
					llDesMarcaCC = .F.
				EndIf
			EndScan
			If llDesMarcaCC
		 		lcWhere = [Select Cidchaves From SigCdCar Where nLotecs = ]+Str(crTmpCart.nLoteCs,10)+[ And Emps = ']+CrTmpCart.Emps+[']
				If ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWhere,'CrCar') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrCar')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				Select CrCar
				If Reccount() > 0
					lcUpDate = [UpDate SigCdCar Set utilizados  = 0 Where CidChaves = ']+CrCar.CidChaves+[']
					If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
						MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigCdCar)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
				Endif
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndScan
EndIf

=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)

If _GravaDel
	insert into crSigExMvc (acres,datars,datas,desc2s,descs,Dopes,;
		empds,emps,grupoos, contaos, grupods, contads, nemps,;
		notas,numes,obses,opers,valacres,valdes2s,valdescs,valos,;
		grvends,vends,usuars,dataexcl,datatrans, Ecfs, CidChaves, EmpDopNums) ;
	values (tmpeest.acres,Nvl(tmpeest.datars,_pData),tmpeest.datas,tmpeest.desc2s,tmpeest.descs,;
			tmpeest.Dopes, lcOldEmpds, tmpeest.emps,;
			tmpeest.grupoos, tmpeest.contaos, tmpeest.grupods, tmpeest.contads,;
			tmpeest.nemps,TmpEest.notas,tmpeest.numes,Nvl(tmpeest.obses,''),;
			tmpeest.opers,tmpeest.valacres,tmpeest.valdes2s,tmpeest.valdescs,;
			tmpeest.valos, tmpeest.grvends, tmpeest.vends,usuar,_pData,ctod(SPACE(8)), ;
			TmpEest.Ecfs, fUniqueIds(), tmpeest.emps + tmpeest.Dopes + Str(tmpeest.Numes, 6))

	If InList(CrSigCdOpe.CupFis,1,3)
		Select crEesti
		Scan
			If Empty(Cpros) Or Qtds = 0
				Loop
			Endif
			Scatter Memvar
			m.CidChaves = fUniqueIds()
			m.EmpDopNums = TmpEest.Emps + TmpEest.Dopes + Str(TmpEest.Numes,6)
			Insert Into CrSigExMvi From Memvar
		EndScan
	EndIf
	
EndIf

lcSql = [Select * From SigOpCsn Where cDopes = ']+TmpEest.Dopes+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocSnOpe') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (LocSnOpe')
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select LocSnOpe
Index on cNivels Tag Dopes

Select crEstPe
Scan
	NDope = Val( Left( Str( Codigos, 10 ), 4 ) )
	=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','ndopes',nDope)
	dope=crSigCdOpe.Dopes
	Nume = Val( Right( Str( Codigos, 10 ), 6 ) )
	lcSql = [Select Dopes, AgdAutos, ddNfs From SigOpCdc Where Dopes = ']+dope+[']
	=Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpDcOpe')

	=Seek(Dope,'LocSnOpe','Dopes')

	set decimals to 2
	lcEdn = Iif(IsEmpty(CrEstPe.EmpSubns),TmpEest.Emps,CrEstPe.EmpSubns)+ Dope + Str(Nume,6)
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrEest','EmpdopNums', lcEdn )
		llSubn = .f.
		lnValo = CrEest.ValoBxs - CrEstPe.ValoBxs
		llDtBx = Null
		llPago = Iif(_BxPagos,.f.,CrEest.ChkPagos)
		ldDtAg = Iif(TmpDcOpe.AgdAutos = 1,Null, CrEest.DtAgends)
		ldDtAud= Iif(TmpDcOpe.AgdAutos = 1,Null, CrEest.DtAudits)
		lcAudit= Iif(TmpDcOpe.AgdAutos = 1,'  ', CrEest.Auditors)
		lcNemp = Iif(CrSigOpCdc.ddnfs  = 1,'  ', CrEest.Nemps)
		lnUtil = Iif(CrSigOpCdc.MarcUtils = 2,0, CrEest.Utilizados)

		lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvCab Set DtBaixas = ?llDtBx, ]+;
					[ValoBxs = ]+Str(lnValo,12,2)+[, ChkPagos = ?llPago, DtAgends = ?ldDtAg, ]+;
					[dtAudits = ?ldDtAud, Auditors = ?lcAudit, DataTrans = Null, Nemps = ?lcNemp, ]+;
					[UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv, Utilizados = ]+Str(lnUtil)+[ ]+;
					Iif(TmpEest.Dopes = CrSigCdPam.DopBxEsts,[, DtBxEstqs = Null ],[ ] )+;
					[Where CidChaves = ']+CrEest.CidChaves+[']
		If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
			MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 14')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		
		If _BaixaSn Or (Not Empty(CrEstPe.ValoBxs) And lnValoBxs > 0 )
			lcSql = [Select Sum(Qtdes) as Qtdes From SigBxEst Where EmpDopNumb = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
			If Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'CsTmpBxEst') < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CsTmpBxEst - excluir')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
			If CsTmpBxEst.Qtdes > 0
				llFalse = .f.
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set ChkSubn = ?llFalse, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 14')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			Else
				llFalse = .f.
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set ChkSubn = ?llFalse, ChkBxParcs = ?llFalse, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvCab 14')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvItn Set QtBaixas=0, ChkSubn = ?llFalse Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvItn 14')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvIts Set QtBaixas=0, ChkSubn = ?llFalse Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpdopNums+[']
				If ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'') < 1
					MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvIts 14')
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			Endif

			lcUpdate = [Update SigMvEte Set ChkSubn = ?llFalse Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpDopNums+[']
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr6.PnIdConn  > 0
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr6.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			Else
				LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			EndIf
			If lnErro < 1
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Update SigMvEte )')
				Return .f.
			EndIf

		Endif
		
		If Seek(CrEest.Dopes,'CrSigCdMei','Dopes')
			lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtt Where EmpdopNums = ']+CrEest.EmpDopNums+[']
			LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
			If lnErro < 0
				MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtt - excluir 5)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		Endif
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrSigCdOpe','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigOpCdd','CrSigOpCdd','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigOpCdc','CrSigOpCdc','dopes',TmpEest.Dopes)

		If CrSigCdOpe.cBxSubns = 1 Or LocSnOpe.cBxPagos = 1 Or LocSnOpe.PgSubnns = 1
			_nDope = Val(Left(Str(CrEstPe.Codigos,10),4))
			_nNume = Val(Right(Str(CrEstPe.Codigos,10),6))
			=ThisForm.PodataMgr.Cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrTmpOpe','nDopes',_nDope,[Dopes])
			lcEdn = Iif(IsEmpty(CrEstPe.EmpSubns),ThisForm.pemps,CrEstPe.EmpSubns)+CrTmpOpe.Dopes+Str(_nNume,6)
			=ThisForm.PodataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvPec','CrTmpEstPe','EmpDopNums',lcEdn)
			Select CrTmpEstPe
			Scan
				_nDope = Val(Left(Str(CrTmpEstPe.Codigos,10),4))
				_nNume = Val(Right(Str(CrTmpEstPe.Codigos,10),6))
				=ThisForm.PodataMgr.Cursorquery('SigCdOpe','CrTmpOpe','nDopes',_nDope,[Dopes])
				lcEdn = Iif(IsEmpty(CrTmpEstPe.EmpSubns),ThisForm.pEmps,CrTmpEstPe.EmpSubns)+CrTmpOpe.Dopes+Str(_nNume,6)
				=ThisForm.PodataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab','CrTmpEest','EmpDopNums',lcEdn)
				
				If CrSigCdOpe.cBxSubns = 1
					If CrTmpEest.ChkSubn = CrTmpEstPe.chkSubn And CrTmpEest.DtAGends = CrTmpEstPe.DtAgends
						MessageBox('A Operaçăo de Estoque '+lcEdn+' Foi Movimentada!!!',16,'Impossivel Exclusăo/Alteracao')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					llSubn  = CrTmpEstPe.ChkSubn
					llDtAgd = CrTmpEstPe.DtAgends
					llFalse = .f.
					ldDtNull= Null
					lcUpdate = [Update SigMvPec Set ChkSubn = ?llFalse, DtAGends = ?ldDtNull Where Cidchaves = ']+CrTmpEstpe.CidChaves+[']
					If ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Exclusăo Baixa SubNivel 1)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set ChkSubn = ?llSubn, DtAgends = ?llDtAgd, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrTmpEest.EmpDopNums+[']
					If ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Exclusăo Baixa SubNivel 2)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
				EndIf
				If LocSnOpe.cBxPagos = 1 Or LocSnOpe.PgSubnns = 1
					If CrTmpEest.ChkPagos = CrTmpEstPe.chkPagos
						MessageBox('A Operaçăo de Estoque '+lcEdn+' Foi Movimentada!!!',16,'Impossivel Exclusăo/Alteracao')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					llPago  = CrTmpEstPe.ChkPagos
					llFalse = .f.
					llTrue  = .t.
					ldDtNull= Null
					lcUpdate = [Update SigMvPec Set ChkPagos = ?llFalse Where Cidchaves = ']+CrTmpEstpe.CidChaves+[']
					If ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Exclusăo Baixa SubNivel 1)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
					lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set ChkPagos = ?llPago, DataTrans = Null, UltGrvs = ?lcUltGrv Where EmpDopNums = ']+CrTmpEest.EmpDopNums+[']
					If ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate,'') < 1
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Exclusăo Baixa SubNivel 2)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
				EndIf
				If Seek(CrTmpEest.Dopes,'CrSigCdMei','Dopes')
					lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtt Where EmpdopNums = ']+CrTmpEest.empDopNums+[']
					LnErro = ThisForm.PoDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'')
					If lnErro < 0
						MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtt - excluir 6)')
						Return .f.
					EndIf
				Endif
			EndScan
		Endif

	Else
		lcTransacao = TmpEest.Emps + ' ' + Dope + ' ' + AllTrim(Str(Nume,6)) + ' NĂO ENCONTRADO'
		fGravarLog( 'X', TmpEest.Dopes, Thisform.pcescolha, lcTransacao )
	EndIf
Endscan

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvItt Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvItt)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtd Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtd)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvPec Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvPec)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvMov Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvMov)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEtv Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEtv)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvEte Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvEte)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

If Used('TmpBxPends')
	Use In TmpBxPends
EndIf

If Used('TmpEtiquetas')
	Use In TmpEtiquetas
Endif

If Used('csTmpOpAut')
	Use In csTmpOpAut
Endif

lcDelete = [Delete From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+_Posicao+[']
If Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcDelete,'') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (Delete SigMvCab 5)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
Return .t.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE excluirop
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE excluirop
Private pDat, pOpI, pOpF
Local _ChaveDel1, _ChaveDel2, _ChaveEest

pDat = Datetime()

Select crSigCdNec
_Nops = Int(Numps / 10000)

*-- Rafael - 22/10/2016 - Quando for numeraçăo pela movimentaçăo o sistema nao usa sequencial
If CrSigCdOpd.Numeras = 4
	_Nops = Int(Numps)
EndIf 


ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalEest', 'Nops', _Nops, 'Emps, Dopes, Numes, cIdChaves, Nops, Rnops')
Select LocalEest
Scan
	_ChaveEest = LocalEest.Emps + LocalEest.Dopes + Str(LocalEest.Numes, 6)

	If LocalEest.Dopes = CrSigCdPam.DopEmphs Or LocalEest.Dopes = crSigCdPam.DopReqcs Or ;
		LocalEest.Dopes = crSigCdPam.DopPedcs Or LocalEest.Dopes = crSigCdPam.DopComps Or ;
		LocalEest.Dopes = CrSigCdPam.TransfRes Or ;
		(LocalEest.Dopes = CrSigCdPac.DopEsts And LocalEest.Rnops = LocalEest.Nops )
		
		lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = ']+ _ChaveEest +[']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvItn)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvIts Where EmpDopNums = ']+ _ChaveEest +[']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvIts)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+ _ChaveEest +[']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvCab)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		lcQuery = [Delete From SigBxEst Where EmpDopNums = ']+ _ChaveEest +[']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigBxEst)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvHst', 'LocalHis', 'OriDopNums', _ChaveEest, ;
									   'Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams, cIdChaves')
		Select LocalHis
		Scan
			=SqlCalcP2(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.Grupos, LocalHis.Estos, LocalHis.Cpros, LocalHis.Datas, LocalHis.CodCors, LocalHis.CodTams, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			=fRecalculaC(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.CPros, LocalHis.Datas, Thisform.Podatamgr )

			lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvHst ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalHis.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvHst 1)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan
		
	Else

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvItn', 'LocalEestI', 'EmpDopNums', _ChaveEest, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalEestI
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Update SigMvItn Set QtReservas = 0, QtProds = 0, QtBxProds = 0, DtAlts = ?pDat ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEestI.cIdChaves + [']
*!*	QtProds = QtReservas && Tiago - 20/05/2013 - Alterado para sempre atualizar o campo QTRESERVAS E QTPRODS = 0, pois antes ao excluir uma OP o item que foi reservado năo aparecia mais para industrializar				   
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvItn)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan
	
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvIts', 'LocalEstI2', 'EmpDopNums', _ChaveEest, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalEstI2
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Update SigMvIts Set QtReservas = 0, QtProds = 0, QtBxProds = 0 ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEstI2.cIdChaves + [']
*!*	QtProds = QtReservas && Tiago - 20/05/2013 - Alterado para sempre atualizar o campo QTRESERVAS E QTPRODS = 0, pois antes ao excluir uma OP o item que foi reservado năo aparecia mais para industrializar					   
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvIts)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan


		lcQuery = [Update SigMvCab ] + ;
					 [Set Nops = 0, ] + ;
					 	 [DtAlts = ?pDat ] + ;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEest.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvCab)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	Endif
EndScan

If (_Nops <> 0)

	*-- Rafael - 22/10/2016 - Quando for numeraçăo pela movimentaçăo o sistema nao usa sequencial
	If CrSigCdOpd.Numeras = 4
		pOpI = _Nops
		pOpF = _Nops
	Else
		pOpI = Int(Val(Str(_Nops, 6) + '0001'))
		pOpF = Int(Val(Str(_Nops, 6) + '9999'))
	EndIf 	
	
	pDpp = CrSigCdNec.Dopps
	
	lcQuery = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, cIdChaves ] + ;
			    [From SigCdNec ] + ;
			   [Where Numps BetWeen ?pOpI And ?pOpF And Dopps = ?pDpp ]+;
			   [Union all ]+;
			   [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, CidChaves From SigCdNec ]+;
			   [Where Nops Between ?pOpI And ?pOpF ]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalNens') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalNens)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select LocalNens
	Scan
		_ChaveDel1 = Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10)
		_ChaveDel2 = Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 06)

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdNei', 'LocalNensI', 'EmpDNPs', _ChaveDel1, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalNensi
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Delete From SigCdNei ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNensI.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigCdNei)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan
		
		*-- Rafael - 22/10/2016 - Sequencia do Conserto = NEMPS + NDOPES + NUMES
		If CrSigCdOpd.Numeras = 4
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpPic', 'LocalOpi', 'NumPs', LocalNens.Numps, 'cIdChaves')
		Else
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpPic', 'LocalOpi', 'Nops', LocalNens.Numps, 'cIdChaves')
		EndIf
				
		Select LocalOpi
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Delete From SigOpPic ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalOpi.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigOpPic)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvHst', 'LocalHis', 'OriDopNums', _ChaveDel2, ;
									   'Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams, cIdChaves')
		Select LocalHis
		Scan
			=SqlCalcP2(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.Grupos, LocalHis.Estos, LocalHis.Cpros, LocalHis.Datas, LocalHis.CodCors, LocalHis.CodTams, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			=fRecalculaC(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.CPros, LocalHis.Datas, ThisForm.Podatamgr )

			lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvHst ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalHis.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigMvHst 2)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigPdMvf', 'LocalMFas', 'EmpDNPs', _ChaveDel1, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalMFas
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Delete From SigPdMvf ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMFas.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigPdMvf)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan

		lcQuery = [Delete From SigCdNec ] + ;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ExcluirOp - SigCdNec)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndScan
EndIf

Return .t.

ENDPROC

*** Tiago - 10/04/2012 - Vianna - Detectei que a funçăo năo checava os componentes que estava agregados, pois o order by estava filtrando eles

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE geraeest
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE geraeest
lcSql = [Select * From SigOpOeo Where Dopps = ']+CrSigCdNec.Dopps+[' ]
If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalEopp') < 1
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (localeOpp)')
	Return 0
EndIf
If Reccount('LocalEOpp') = 0
	Return .t.
EndIf

Select CsCabec
Zap
Select CsItens
Zap

Select LocalEOpp
Scan
	lcSql = [Select * From SigCdOpe where Dopes = ']+LocalEOpp.Dopes+[']
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'CrSigCdOpe') < 1
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrSigCdOpe)')
		Return 0
	Endif
	=ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigOpCdd','CrSigOpCdd','dopes',LocalEOpp.Dopes)

	Insert Into CsCabec (EmpDs, Emps, Dopes, Datas) Values ;
			(CrSigCdNec.Emps,CrSigCdNec.Emps,CrSigCdOpe.Dopes,CrSigCdNec.Datas)

	Replace GrupoOs With Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.GruOrigs),CrSigCdOpe.GruOrigs,CrSigCdNec.GrupoOs),;
			ContaOs With Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.ConOrigs),CrSigCdOpe.ConOrigs,CrSigCdNec.ContaOs),;
			GrupoDs With Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.GruDests),CrSigCdOpe.GruDests,CrSigCdNec.GrupoDs),;
			ContaDs With Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpe.ConDests),CrSigCdOpe.ConDests,CrSigCdNec.ContaDs),;
			TabdPs  With CrSigCdOpe.TabdPs,;
			lPrecos With CrSigCdOpe.lPrecoPads in CsCabec

	lcSql = [Select b.cpros,b.Qtds,b.EmpDopNums,b.Numes,c.Ndopes From SigPdMvf a, SigOpPic b, SigCdOpe c ]+;
			[Where a.EmpDnPs = ']+CrSigCdNec.EmpDnPs+[' And a.Nops = b.Nops ]+;
			[And b.Dopes = c.Dopes ]
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalMfas') < 1
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (localMfas)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	
	lnItem = 1
	If Upper(Alltrim(LocaleOpp.TpProd)) = 'ACABADO'
		Select LocalMfas
		Scan
			=ThisForm.GeraEesti(LocalMfas.Cpros,'CsItens')
			Replace cItens With lnItem ,;
					Qtds   With LocalMfas.Qtds,;
					Emps   With CrSigCdNec.emps,;
					Dopes  With LocalEOpp.Dopes,;
					Totas  With Qtds * Units in CsItens
			lnItem = lnItem + 1
		EndScan
	Else
		If Upper(Alltrim(LocaleOpp.TpProd)) = 'COMPONENTE'
			lcSql = [Select a.cmats,a.qtds,a.Pesos From SigCdNei a ]+;
					[Where a.EmpDnPs = ']+CrSigCdNec.EmpDnPs+[' ]
			If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalNensi') < 1
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (localNensi)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Select LocalNensi
			Scan
				=ThisForm.GeraEesti(LocalNensi.cMats,'CsItens')
				Replace cItens With lnItem ,;
						Qtds   With LocalNensi.Qtds,;
						Emps   With CrSigCdNec.emps,;
						Dopes  With LocalEOpp.Dopes,;
						Totas  With Qtds * Units in CsItens
				lnItem = lnItem + 1
			EndScan
		Endif
	EndIf

	If Upper(Alltrim(LocalEOpp.TpSubn)) = Upper('Pedido Produçăo')
		Select Distinct nDopes,Numes From LocalMfas Into cursor CsSubNiveis
		Select CsSubNiveis
		Scan
			lnCod = ( nDopes * 1000000 ) + Numes
			Select CsEstPe
			Insert Into CsEstPe (Dopes,Codigos,Emps ) Values (LocalEOpp.Dopes,lnCod,CrSigCdNec.Emps)
		EndScan
	EndIf
EndScan
Update CsItens Set EmpDopNums = Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes,6)
Update CsCabec Set EmpDopNums = Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes,6)
Update CsEstPe Set EmpDopNums = Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes,6)

Do Form SigPrGst With ThisForm

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE geraeesti
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE geraeesti
Lparameters pProduto,pcArq

oper       = CrSigCdOpe.Opers
OpePad     = CrSigCdOpe.OpePads
precop     = CrSigCdOpe.precops
lcArq      = pcArq

lcSql = [select * from SigCdPro where cpros = ']+pproduto+[']
ThisForm.Podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcSql,'CrTmpPro')

Select ( pcArq )
Append Blank
Replace cpros   With CrTmpPro.Cpros ,;
		moefats With Iif( CrSigCdOpe.Precops = 1, crtmpPro.Moepvs, Iif( CrSigCdOpe.Precops = 2, crtmpPro.Moepcs, CrSigCdOpe.CMoes ) ) in &pcArq.

If InList(CrSigCdOpe.PrecoAuts,1,3)
	lcSql = [Select Codigos From SigCdLpc where lPrecos = ']+CsCabec.lPrecos+[']
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'CrtmplPre')
	If lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	lcwhere = [Select * From SigCdLpi Where Cpros = ']+CrTmpPro.Cpros+[' And LPrecos = ']+CsCabec.lPrecos+[']
	lnErro = ThisForm.podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWhere,'CrSigCdLpi')
	If lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Select CrSigCdLpi
	Go Top
	If Reccount() > 0 And (IsEmpty(crSigCdLpi.VencFs) Or BetWeen(CsCabec.Datas,crSigCdLpi.VencIs, crSigCdLpi.VencFs))
		lcMoeVs = crSigCdLpi.MoeVs
		Replace &pcArq..univals with crSigCdLpi.PVens, ;
				&pcArq..MoeFats   With crSigCdLpi.MoeVs, ;
				&pcArq..lPrecos   with Cscabec.LPrecos,  ;
				&pcArq..CodlPrecs With CrTmplPre.Codigos in &pcArq.
	Else
		If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 1
			lcMoeVs   = CrtmpPro.MoeVs
			lnUniVals = crtmpPro.PVens
		Else
			If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 2
				lcMoeVs   = crtmpPro.MoeCs
				lnUniVals = crtmpPro.PCuss
				If InList(CrSigOpCdd.chkIfors,1,2)
					_Ct = Iif(CrSigOpCdd.ChkIfors=1,CsCabec.ContaOs,CsCabec.Contads)
					lcQuery = [Select Moevs, Pvens From SigPrFnc Where Cpros = ']+CrTmpPro.Cpros+[' And Ifors = ']+_Ct+[']
					=ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcQuery,'CrTmpFpro')
					If Not Eof('CrTmpfPro') And CrTmpfPro.pvens > 0 and Not Empty(CrTmpfPro.Moevs)
						lcMoeVs   = crtmpfPro.MoeVs
						lnUniVals = crtmpfPro.PVens
					Endif
				Endif
				lcQuery = [Select MoeQs, QtdEqs ] + ;
						    [From SigCdMoe ] + ;
						   [Where CMoes = '] + lcMoeVs + [' ] + ;
						   [Order By MoeQs, QtdEqs]

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmpMoe') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crTmpMoe)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
				Go Top In crTmpMoe
					
				If Not Eof('crTmpMoe')
					If Not IsEmpty(crtmpMoe.Moeqs)
						lcMoeVs   = CrTmpMoe.Moeqs
						lnUniVals = lnUniVals * Iif( crtmpMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crtmpMoe.QtdEqs )
					Endif
				Endif
			Else
				If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 5
					lcMoeVs   = CrtmpPro.Moedas
					lnUniVals = crtmpPro.Valors
				Else
					If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 7
						lcMoeVs   = CrTmpPro.mUltComps
						lnUniVals = CrTmpPro.vUltComps
					Else
						If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 8
							=fCustoMedio(CsCabec.Emps,CrTmpPro.Cpros,CsCabec.Datas,ThisForm.Podatamgr)
							lcMoeVs   = TmpCusMed.Moedas
							lnUniVals = TmpCusMed.Valors
						Else
							lnUniVals = 0
							lcMoeVs   = CrSigCdOpe.CMoes
						EndIf
					Endif
				Endif
			Endif
		EndIf
		If CrSigCdOpe.PrecoPs = 11
			lcMoeVs   = crtmpPro.MoeCs
			lnUniVals = crtmpPro.custofs
		EndIf
		Select ( pcArq )
		Replace UniVals With lnUniVals in &pcArq.
	Endif
Else
	lcMoeVs = CrSigCdOpe.CMoes
Endif

Select ( pcArq )
Replace dpros  With crtmppro.dpros, ;
		cunis  With crtmppro.cunis, ;
		MoeVs  With lcMoeVs,;
		Moedas With lcMoeVs,;
		Reffs  With crtmpPro.Reffs, ;
		Units  With CrTmpPro.Pvens ,;
		CUniPs with CrTmpPro.cUniPs in &pcArq.

Select ( pcArq )
If Empty( &pcArq..opers )
	Replace &pcArq..opers with Iif( oper=1, 'E', Iif( oper = 2, 'S', Iif( oper = 3, OpePad, &pcArq..opers ) ) )
EndIf

*Thisform.Calc_ValIte()
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE impbol
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE impbol
Do Form SigOpIbo With Thisform, 2, This.Titulo,.f.,.f.,.f.,.f.,.f.,crSigCdOpd.qtddocs  &&SigOpIbo 
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE rettpop
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE rettpop
_OGrupo = TmpNens.GrupoOs

lcQuery = [Select Distinct TpOps From SigCdRpo Where Dopps = ']+CrSigCdOpd.Dopps+[' ]+;
		  [And Grupos = ']+_OGrupo+[' And Not TpOps = ' ']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmprOpt') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (TmprOpt)')
	Return ' '
EndIf
If Reccount('TmprOpt') = 0
	lcQuery = [Select Distinct TpOps From SigCdRpo Where Dopps = ']+CrSigCdOpd.Dopps+[' ]+;
			  [And Grupos = '  ' And Not TpOps = ' ']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmprOpt') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (TmprOpt)')
		Return ' '
	EndIf
EndIf

lcQuery = [Select Cods, Descs, pFalhas, Grupos ] + ;
			[From SigOpOpt ] + ;
		   [Where (Grupos = '] + _OGrupo + [' Or ] + ;
		   		  [Grupos = '] + Space(10) + [') And ] + ;
		   		  [Not Situas = 2]

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmpOpt') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (TmpOpt)')
	Return ' ' 
EndIf

Select TmpRopt
If Reccount() > 0
	Select a.* from TmpOpt a, TmpRopt b Where a.Cods = b.TpOps Into Cursor csSelecao ReadWrite
Else
	Select * From TmpOpt Into Cursor CsSelecao ReadWrite
EndIf
Select CsSelecao
Go Top
If Reccount() = 1
	lcRet = CsSelecao.Cods
Else
	lcRet = ''
EndIf
Use In TmpOpt
USE In CsSelecao
Return ( lcRet )

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE sqldados
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE sqldados
Private pEmp, pDtI, pDtF

pEmp = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.Value
pDtI = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_inicial.Value)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_final.Value, '23:59:59')

If ThisForm._pconsulta
	lcEDNss = ThisForm.pemps + ThisForm._dopp + Str(ThisForm.pNumes,10)
Endif

ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdNec')
Select crSigCdNec
Index On EmpDnPs Tag EmpDnPs
Go Top

Zap In CrProcurar

ThisForm.AntEmpr  = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.Value
ThisForm.AntDtIni = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.dt_Inicial.Value
ThisForm.AntDtFin = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_Periodo.Dt_final.Value

ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.
=fCarregaGrade(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade)
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
LParameters Dopp, pForm, _pNume, _pEmps, _pConsulta

Public _Nome
Local _Ende, llAcesso
Private pEmp, pDtI, pDtF

ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_inicial.Value     = Date()
ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_Final.Value       = Date()
ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.Value = _Empr

ThisForm._Dopp 	  = Dopp
ThisForm.AntEmpr  = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.Value
ThisForm.AntDtIni = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_inicial.Value
ThisForm.AntDtFin = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_Final.Value
ThisForm.pAntform = pForm
Thisform.pEmps    = Iif( Type('_pEmps') = 'C', _pEmps, _Empr )
Thisform.pNumes   = Iif(Type('_pNume') = 'N',_pNume, 0)
ThisForm.Locregister = 0

Thisform.Caption = ThisForm._dopp

pEmp = ThisForm.AntEmpr
pDtI = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.AntDtIni)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.AntDtFin, '23:59:59')

If _pConsulta
	lcEDNss = ThisForm.pemps + Thisform._Dopp + Str(ThisForm.pNumes,10)
	lcQryNens  = [Select * From SigCdNec ] + ;
				 [Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcEdnss+[']
Else
	lcQryNens  = [Select * From SigCdNec ] + ;
				 [Where Emps = ?pEmp And ] + ;
				 [Dopps = '] + ThisForm._Dopp + [' And ] + ;
				 [Datas BetWeen ?pDtI And ?pDtF]
EndIf

lcQryNensI = [Select * From SigCdNei]
lcQryMFas  = [Select * From SigPdMvf]
lcQryHis   = [Select * From SigMvHst]
lcQryMccr  = [Select * From SigMvCcr]
lcQryMcpv  = [Select * From SigMvCpv]
lcQryEti   = [Select * From SigOpEtq]
lcQryPEti  = [Select * From SigEtPos]
lcQryEest  = [Select * From SigMvCab]
lcQryEestI = [Select * From SigMvItn]
lcQryMvIts = [Select * From SigMvIts]
lcQrySubMv = [Select * From SigSubMv]
lcQryDelet = [Select * From SigExMvc]
lcQryInc   = [Select * From SigOpInc]
With ThisForm
	.podatamgr4 = CreateObject('fSqlConector', ThisForm.Name) &&Gravar Tabela SigGtmpR
	.poDataMgr  = CreateObject('fSqlConector', ThisForm.Name)

	If (.poDataMgr.pnIdconn > 0)
		With .poDataMgr
			.AddCursor('SigCdNec', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdNec', '', ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade, lcQryNens)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('Numps',    '', '', 'Código', 		  065, .t.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('Datas',    '', '', 'Data',   		  075, .t.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('TotPesos', '', '', 'Total de Peso', 065, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('GrupoOs',  '', '', 'Gr. Origem', 	  080, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('ContaOs',  '', '', 'Ct. Origem', 	  080, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('GrupoDs',  '', '', 'Gr. Destino',   080, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('ContaDs',  '', '', 'Ct. Destino',   080, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('Usuars',   '', '', 'Usuário', 	  065, .f.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('Docus' ,   '', '', 'Documento', 	  070, .t.)
			.pfSqlTabela(1).pColuna('nLotes' ,   '', '', 'Lote', 	  080, .t.)
			
			.AddCursor('SigCdNei',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdNei', '', '', lcQryNensI)
			.AddCursor('SigPdMvf',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigPdMvf', '', '', lcQryMFas)
			.AddCursor('SigMvHst',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvHst', '', '', lcQryHis)
			.AddCursor('SigMvCcr',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvCcr', '', '', lcQryMccr)
			.AddCursor('SigOpEtq',  'CBars', 	 'crSigOpEtq', '', '', lcQryEti)
			.AddCursor('SigEtPos',  'CidChaves', 'crSigEtPos', '', '', lcQryPEti)
			.AddCursor('SigMvCab',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvCab', '', '', lcQryEest)
			.AddCursor('SigMvItn',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvItn', '', '', lcQryEestI)
			.AddCursor('SigMvIts',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvIts', '', '', lcQryMvIts)			
			.AddCursor('SigSubMv',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigSubMv', '', '', lcQrySubMv)
			.AddCursor('SigExMvc',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigExMvc', '', '', lcQryDelet)
			.AddCursor('SigOpInc',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigOpInc', '', '', lcQryInc)
			.Addcursor('SigMvCcr',  'CidChaves', 'cqSigMvCcr', '', '', lcQryMccr)	&& Rafael - Configuraçăo Financeira
			.Addcursor('SigMvCpv',  'CidChaves', 'crSigMvCpv', '', '', lcQryMcpv)	&& Rafael - Configuraçăo Financeira
			.AddCursor('SigInAop',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigInAop', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigBxEst',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigBxEst', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigPrJus',  'cIdChaves', 'CrSigPrJus', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigMvPec',  'cIdChaves', 'CrSigMvPec', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigMvIts',  'cIdChaves', 'crSigMvIts', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigInBep',  'cIdChaves', 'CrSigInBep', '', '')
			.AddCursor('SigPdNlt',  'nLotes', 'crSigPdNlt',  '', '')			
		EndWith

		With .podatamgr4
			.Addcursor('SigGtmpR','Cidchaves','CrSigGtmpR','','')
		Endwith

		Select * From CrSigCdNec Into Cursor CrProcurar ReadWrite
		Select CrProcurar
		Index On Numps tag Numps

		ThisForm.SqlDados

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPam', 'crSigCdPam', .f., .f.)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPac', 'crSigCdPac')
		ThisForm.SigKey = CrSigCdPac.SigKeys

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdOpd', 'crSigCdOpd', .f., .f.)
		Select crSigCdOpd
		Index On Dopps Tag Dopps

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdSvc', 'crSigCdSvc', .f., .f.)
		Select crSigCdSvc
		Index On Ccats + Grupos + Contas Tag CaGruCo
		Index On Grupos + Contas + Ccats Tag GruCoCa

		lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Descrs, TrfPesas, CompAgrus, CtrLotes, UnifBals ] + ;
				    [From SigCdGcr ] + ;
				   [Where GerBals = 1]

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmpGccr') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (TmpGccr)')
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Select TmpGccr
		Index On Codigos Tag BalCodigo
		Index On Descrs  Tag BalDescrs

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.getDriver() = 'foxpro')
			lcDiretorio = Addbs(JustPath(ThisForm.poDataMgr.GetDatabase()))
			Use &lcDiretorio.\SigCdCli Alias TmpCli In 0
		Else
			lcQuery = [Select IClis, RClis, Grupos, Inativas ] + ;
					    [From SigCdCli ] + ;
				   	   [Where GerBals = 1]

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmpCli') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (TmpCli)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Select TmpCli
			Index On Grupos Tag BalGrupo
			Index On IClis  Tag BalCodigo
			Index On RClis  Tag BalNome
		EndIf

		Select crSigCdOpd
		Set Order To Dopps
		If Not Seek(ThisForm._Dopp)
			ThisForm.Release
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		_Acesso = 'P' + Padl(crSigCdOpd.NDopps, 8, '0') 

		=DoDefault(_Acesso)
		
		*ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Alterar.Enabled = .F.

		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_op.Value = 2

		ThisForm.Titulo = Proper(Alltrim(crSigCdOpd.TNivels)) + ' '
		ThisForm.Artigo = Lower(Alltrim(crSigCdOpd.Artigos))

		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.GradeOperaçăo.Column1.Header1.Caption = ThisForm.Titulo
		
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade
			.SetAll('DynamicForeColor','Iif(crSigCdNec.Retrabs And Not crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And Not CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(255,0,0),'+;
										'Iif(crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And Not crSigCdNec.Retrabs And Not CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(0,0,255),'+;
										'Iif(crSigCdNec.Retrabs And crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And Not CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(255,0,255),'+;
										'Iif(Not crSigCdNec.Retrabs And Not crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(128,0,0),'+;
										'Iif(crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And Not crSigCdNec.Retrabs And CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(0,0,160),'+;
										'Iif(crSigCdNec.Retrabs And crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(255,0,128),'+;
										'Iif(crSigCdNec.Retrabs And Not crSigCdNec.ChkSubn And CrSigCdNec.nConforms,RGB(128,0,128),'+;
										'RGB(0,0,0))))))))','Column')
			.SetAll('DynamicBackColor','Iif(CrSigCdNec.ProcBals And CrSigCdNec.ProcDbal,RGB(220,255,220),Iif(CrSigCdNec.ProcBals,RGB(255,209,164),Iif(CrSigCdNec.ProcDBal,RGB(255,255,196),RGB(255,255,255))))','Column')
		EndWith

		ThisForm.CriaCursor

		If Not CrSigCdPam.BlqmEmps And Empty(CrSigCdOpd.EmpLancs)
			ThisForm.Pagina.lista.cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.SetFocus
		Else
			ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.get_cd_empresa.Visible = .f.
			ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.say4.Visible = .f.
			ThisForm.Pagina.lista.cnt_periodo.dt_inicial.SetFocus
		EndIf

		If _pConsulta
			Select CrSigCdNec
			Set Order to EmpDnPs
			Seek _pEmps + ThisForm._dopp + Str( _pNume, 10 )
			This._pConsulta = .t.
			Thisform.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Click( 2 )
		Endif

	Else
		=Messagebox('Impossível Efetuar Conexăo Com o Servidor de Banco de Dados...', 0+48, 'CreateObject')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndWith

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Load
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Load
=fConfigGeral()

Create Cursor TmpOperacao (Codigos n(12), EmpDnPs c(33), TmpMins n(5), Apontas n(1), Autos L, GrupoO c(10), ContaO c(10))
Index On EmpDnPs Tag EmpDnPs
Index On Codigos Tag Codigos 
Set Order To 

=DoDefault()

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mativapagina1
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mativapagina1
Private pEmp, pDtI, pDtF

pEmp = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Get_cd_empresa.Value
pDtI = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_inicial.Value)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Cnt_periodo.Dt_final.Value, '23:59:59')

If ThisForm._pconsulta
	lcEDNss = ThisForm.pemps + Thisform._dopp + Str(ThisForm.pNumes,10)
EndIf

=DoDefault()

Select CrSigCdNec
Set Order To numPs
If (Reccount('crProcurar') > 0)
	Select crProcurar
	Scan
		lcChv = crProcurar.Numps
		If Not Seek(lcChv, 'crSigCdNec', 'Numps')
			Scatter MemVar Memo
		 	Insert Into crSigCdNec From MemVar
		EndIf 
	EndScan
EndIf
Select CrSigCdNec
Index On EmpDnPs Tag EmpDnPs
Go Top

If ThisForm.LocRegister > 0
	Select CrSigCdNec
	Set Near On
	=Seek(ThisForm.pemps + ThisForm._dopp + Str(ThisForm.Locregister,10))
	Set Near Off
EndIf

*!*	Thisform.Pagina.Lista.Enabled = .t.
*!*	ThisForm.Pagina.ActivePage = 1
*!*	ThisForm.KeyPreview = .t.

ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Refresh
ThisForm.LocRegister = 0

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_excluir
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_excluir
Parameters GravaDel

Private pNot, pDat
Local _ChaveDel, lcGrupos, lcContas, ldDatas, lcMoedas, lcSGrupos, lcSContas, lcSMoedas

pNot = .f.
pDat = Datetime()

Select crSigCdOpd
Set Order To Dopps
Seek TmpNens.Dopps
=Seek(crSigCdOpd.Nivels, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
_NivelOp = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
Seek TmpNens.Dopps
Set Step On 
Select TmpNens
Go Top
_ChaveDel1 = Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10)
_ChaveDel2 = Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 06)

lcQuery = [Delete From SigCdNei Where EmpDnPs = '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigCdNei)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

*!*	lcSql = [Select * From SigMvHst where OriDopNums = ']+_ChaveDel2+[']
lcSql = [Select Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams From SigMvHst where OriDopNums = ']+_ChaveDel2+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalHis') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigCdNei)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Select LocalHis
Scan
	=SqlCalcP2(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.Grupos, LocalHis.Estos, LocalHis.Cpros, LocalHis.Datas, LocalHis.CodCors, LocalHis.CodTams, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	=fRecalculaC(localHis.Emps, LocalHis.CPros, LocalHis.Datas, ThisForm.Podatamgr )
EndScan

lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvHst Where OridopNums = '] + _ChaveDel2 + [']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvHst)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

*** Tiago - 02/07/2013 - Se excluiu todas as movimentaçőes que tinham esse lote entăo pode excluir o lote
If Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'EXCLUIR')
	lcQuery = [Select EmpDnPs From SigCdNec Where nLotes = ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.nLotes)) + [ And EmpDnPs <> '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcQuery,'LocalNlt')
	Select LocalNlt
	If Eof()
		lcQuery = [Delete From SigPdNlt Where nLotes = ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.nLotes))
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigPdNlt)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf	
	Endif
Endif

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCcr', 'LocalMccr', 'EmpDopNums', _ChaveDel2, ;
							   'cIdChaves, Grupos, Contas, Moedas, Datas, SGrupos, SContas, SMoedas')

Select LocalMccr
Scan
	lcGrupos  = LocalMccr.Grupos
	lcContas  = LocalMccr.Contas
	lcMoedas  = LocalMccr.Moedas
	ldDatas   = Nvl(LocalMccr.Datas, Ctod(''))
	lcSgrupos = LocalMccr.SGrupos
	lcSContas = LocalMccr.SContas
	lcSMoedas = LocalMccr.SMoedas

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvCcr ] + ;
			   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMccr.cIdChaves + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvCcr)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	=fRecalculaS( lcGrupos,  lcContas,  ldDatas, lcMoedas,  ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	=fRecalculaS( lcSGrupos, lcSContas, ldDatas, lcSMoedas, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
EndScan

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpEtq', 'LocalEti', 'EmpDopNums', _ChaveDel2, 'CBars, Usados')
Select LocalEti
Scan
	If LocalEti.Usados
		lcQuery = [Update SigOpEtq ] + ;
					 [Set Emps = ' ', ] + ;
					 	 [Dopes = ' ', ] + ;
					 	 [Numes = 0, ] + ;
					 	 [Grupos = ' ', ] + ;
					 	 [Contas = ' ' ] + ;
				   [Where CBars = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalEti.CBars,14))
	Else
		lcQuery = [Delete From SigOpEtq ] + ;
				   [Where CBars = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalEti.CBars,14))
	EndIf

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigOpEtq)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	*** Tiago - 09/09/11 - Se for etiqueta = encerra com, limpa a etiqueta na tira para gerar outra quando finalizar a tira novamente
*!*		If !LocalEti.Usados and crSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 4
		lcQuery = [Update SigOpPic set Codbarras = 0 ] + ;
					   [Where Codbarras = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalEti.CBars,14))
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigOpEtq)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf		
*!*		EndIf
EndScan

lcQuery = [Delete From SigEtPos ] + ;
		   [Where EmpDopNums = '] + _ChaveDel2 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigEtPos)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalEest', 'EmpDnCrds', _ChaveDel2, 'EmpDopNums')
Select LocalEest
Scan

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvItn ] + ;
			   [Where EmpDopNums = '] + LocalEest.EmpDopNums + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvItn)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvIts ] + ;
			   [Where EmpDopNums = '] + LocalEest.EmpDopNums + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvIts)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigSubMv ] + ;
			   [Where EmpDopNums = '] + LocalEest.EmpDopNums + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigSubMv)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
*!*		lcSql = [Select * From SigMvHst where OriDopNums = ']+LocalEest.EmpDopNums+[']
	lcSql = [Select Emps, Grupos, Estos, Cpros, Datas, CodCors, CodTams From SigMvHst where OriDopNums = ']+LocalEest.EmpDopNums+[']	
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalHis') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigCdNei)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select LocalHis
	Scan
		=SqlCalcP2(LocalHis.Emps, LocalHis.Grupos, LocalHis.Estos, LocalHis.Cpros, LocalHis.Datas, LocalHis.CodCors, LocalHis.CodTams, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
		=fRecalculaC(localHis.Emps, localHis.CPros, localHis.Datas, ThisForm.Podatamgr )
	EndScan

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvHst Where OridopNums = '] + LocalEest.empDopNums + [']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvHst)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	If Not ThisForm.Cancelabaixa(LocalEest.EmpDopNums)
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	lcQuery = [Delete From SigBxEst ] + ;
			   [Where EmpDopNums = '] + LocalEest.EmpDopNums + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigBxEst)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCcr', 'LocalMccr', 'EmpDopNums', LocalEest.EmpDopNums, ;
								   'cIdChaves, Grupos, Contas, Moedas, Datas, SGrupos, SContas, SMoedas')

	Select LocalMccr
	Scan
		lcGrupos  = LocalMccr.Grupos
		lcContas  = LocalMccr.Contas
		lcMoedas  = LocalMccr.Moedas
		ldDatas   = Nvl(LocalMccr.Datas, Ctod(''))
		lcSgrupos = LocalMccr.SGrupos
		lcSContas = LocalMccr.SContas
		lcSMoedas = LocalMccr.SMoedas

		lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvCcr ] + ;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMccr.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvCcr 2)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf

		=fRecalculaS( lcGrupos,  lcContas,  ldDatas, lcMoedas,  ThisForm.poDataMgr)
		=fRecalculaS( lcSGrupos, lcSContas, ldDatas, lcSMoedas, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	EndScan
EndScan

lcQuery = [Delete From SigMvCab ] + ;
		   [Where EmpDnCrds = '] + _ChaveDel2 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigMvCab)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigPdMvf', 'LocalMFas', 'EmpDNps', _ChaveDel1, 'cIdChaves, Nenvs, Nops, Emps')
Select LocalMFas
Scan
	If (crSigCdOpd.BxAutos = 1 And ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'EXCLUIR' And Not InList(CrSigCdOpd.Grodns,1,2) )
		_OperExcl = Iif(Not Empty(LocalMFas.Nenvs), LocalMFas.Nenvs, LocalMFas.Nops)
		llPcc = .f. &&crSigCdOpd.Pccs
		
		lcChv = LocalMFas.Emps + crSigCdOpd.Nivels + Str(_OperExcl, 10)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdNec', 'LocalNens', 'EmpDNps', lcChv, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalNens
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
						 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - Update - SigCdNec 1)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan

		lcChv = LocalMfas.Emps + _NivelOp + Str(LocalMfas.Nops, 10)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdNec', 'LocalNens', 'EmpDNps', lcChv, 'cIdChaves')
		Select LocalNens
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
						 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - Update - SigCdNec 2)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndScan
	EndIf
	
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpPic', 'LocalOpi', 'Nops', LocalMFas.Nops, 'cIdChaves, Emps, Dopes, Numes, EmpDs')
	Select LocalOpi
	Scan
		_EmpD = Iif(Not Empty(LocalOpi.EmpDs), LocalOpi.EmpDs, LocalOpi.Emps)

		lcChv = _EmpD + LocalOpi.Dopes + Str(LocalOpi.Numes, 6)
		
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalEest', 'EmpDopNums', lcChv, 'cIdChaves, DtFechas')
		If Not IsEmpty(LocalEest.DtFechas)
			lcQuery = [Update SigMvCab ] + ;
						 [Set DtFechas = Null, ] + ;
						 	 [DtAlts = ?pDat ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEest.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - Update - SigMvCab)')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndScan

	lcQuery = [Delete From SigPdMvf ] + ;
			   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMFas.cIdChaves + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigPdMvf)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndScan

If (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'EXCLUIR')
	lcQuery = [Select cIdChaves ] + ;
			    [From SigCdNec ] + ;
			   [Where Emps = '] + TmpNens.Emps + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Dopps = '] + crSigCdOpd.Nivels + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [NAceites = ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10))

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalNens') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - LocalNens)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select LocalNens
	Scan
		lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
					 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot, ] + ;
					 	 [NAceites = 0 ] + ;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - Update - SigCdNec)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndScan
EndIf

lcQuery = [Delete From SigOpInc ] + ;
		   [Where EmpDnPs = '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigOpInc)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcQuery = [Delete From SigPrJus ] + ;
		  [Where EmpDnPs = '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigPrJus)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

lcQuery = [Delete From SigCdNec ] + ;
		   [Where EmpDnPs = '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigCdNec)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
If GravaDel
	lcQuery = [Update SigInAop Set EmpDnPs = ' ' Where EmpDnPs = ']+TmpNens.EmpDnPs+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, ' ') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigInAop)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	Insert Into crSigExMvc (Datars, Datas, Dopes, Emps, Grupoos, Contaos, Grupods, Contads, Numes, ;
							Obses, Valos, Usuars, DataExcl, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums) ;
					Values (TmpNens.Datars, TmpNens.Datas, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Grupoos, ;
							TmpNens.Contaos, TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, TmpNens.Numps, ;
							Nvl(TmpNens.Obss,''), TmpNens.TotPesos, Usuar, Datetime(), fUniqueIds(), ;
							TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6))
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigExMvc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - SigExMvc)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
Delete From crProcurar Where Numps = TmpNens.NumPs

lcQuery = [Select * From SigInBep Where EmpDnPs = ']+_ChaveDel1+[']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalCabEP') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - LocalCabEP)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

If Reccount('LocalCabEP') = 0
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcSql = [Select Distinct Dopes from SigCdMei Order by Dopes ]
ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'CrSigCdMei')
Select CrSigCdMei
Index On Dopes Tag dopes

=ThisForm.PodataMgr.cursorQuery('SigCdOpe','TmpOpe',.f.,.f.,[CodProPads, Dopes ])
	
Select * From CrSigMvCab Where 0=1 Into Cursor TmpEest ReadWrite

Select LocalCabEp
Scan
	lcSql = [Select * From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+LocalCabEp.EmpDopNums+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalEest') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - LocalEest)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	
	Select TmpEest
	Zap
	
	Select LocalEest
	Scatter Memvar

	Insert Into TmpEest From Memvar
	
	=ThisForm.PodataMgr.cursorQuery('SigOpCdc','TmpdcOpe','Dopes',TmpEest.Dopes,[InibePa,VerEstrs ])

	Select Distinct CodProPads as CPros, Dopes ;
	  From TmpOpe ;
	 Where (Dopes <> TmpEest.Dopes) And Not Empty(CodProPads) And TmpDcOpe.InibePa <> 2 ;
	  Into Cursor csOpeAut
	Index On CPros Tag CPros

	lcWher = [Select Dopeds as Dopes, Cpros From SigOpTrf ]+;
			 [Where Dopes = ']+TmpEest.Dopes+[' Group by Dopeds,Cpros]

	lnErro = ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcWher,'CsOpeTrf')
	If lnErro < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CsOpeTrf)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select CsOpeTrf
	Index On Cpros + Dopes Tag Cpros

	If Not ThisForm.Exclmov(GravaDel)
		Return .f.
	Endif
EndScan

lcQuery = [Delete From SigInBep ] + ;
		   [Where EmpDnPs = '] + _ChaveDel1 + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Excluir - SigInBep)')
	Return .f.
EndIf

Return .t.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_inserir
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_inserir
Private pDat, pQtd, pQt2
Local _Recno1, _Pesagem, _Nop, _TotalAnterior, _Diferenca, _RecnoRateio, _CompAgru, _numcs, lcEdn

Select xMFas
Go Top

_CompAgru = CrSigCdOpd.CompAgrus
=Seek(TmpNens.GrupoOs,'TmpGccr','BalCodigo')
If Inlist(TmpGccr.CompAgrus,1,3)
	_CompAgru = TmpGccr.CompAgrus
Endif

Select CrSigCdOpd
Set Order To Dopps
Seek TmpNens.Dopps

lcGruf = CrSigCdOpd.grufins
lcDopcs = CrSigCdOpd.dopcs

lcEdn = []
Set Step On 
Select CrSigCdNei
Zap
*** Tiago - 26/09/2012 - Năo estava sendo usado por nenhum cliente e ninguém sabia pra que servia
*** Vou utilizar a flag PCCS para marcar as OPs como canceladas pela operaçăo de finalizaçăo antecipada
*!*	If CrSigCdOpd.Pccs

*!*		Select xNensi
*!*		Set Order to
*!*		Replace all Nops with xMFas.Nops,;
*!*					Nenvs with xMFas.NEnvs

*!*		Set Order to Rateio
*!*		Delete all for IsEmpty( Nops ) And IsEmpty( CMats ) And IsEmpty( Cats ) And Rateio # 1
*!*		Go Top

*!*		Scan for Rateio = 5 And TpOps = CrSigCdOpd.Retalhos
*!*			_CMat = CMats
*!*			_Pesagem = Pesos
*!*			_Recno1 = Recno()
*!*			Scan for Rateio = 2 And CMats = _CMat
*!*				Replace Pesos with Pesos - _Pesagem,;
*!*						PsFaseAnt with PsFaseAnt - _Pesagem,;
*!*						Qtds with Qtds - _Pesagem,;
*!*						QtFaseAnt with QtFaseAnt - _Pesagem
*!*				Exit
*!*			Endscan
*!*			Go _Recno1
*!*		Endscan

*!*		Select xMFas
*!*		Set Order to Nops
*!*		Replace all Pesos with 0

*!*		Select xNensi
*!*		Set Order to
*!*		Replace all Nops with 0,;
*!*					Nenvs with 0 for Rateio = 5 And TpOps = CrSigCdOpd.Retalhos

*!*	Endif

Select xNensI
Select * From xNensI Where Not Empty(TPOPS) Into Cursor csCompOps Readwrite
Select csCompOps

Select xNensI
Set Order To
If CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests = 8
	Scan
		If FlagIncs And Nenvs <> 0 And Nops = 0
			Replace Nenvs With 0 In xNensI
		Endif
	Endscan
Endif

*!*	Sum Pesos To _TotPeso For Visivel And Not Servicos
Sum Pesos To _TotPeso For Visivel And Not Servicos And Iif(!CarCompos Or (CarCompos And Rateio <> 5),.T.,.F.)
Set Order To Rateio
Delete All For Empty(Nops) And Empty(CMats) And Empty(Cats) And (Rateio <> 1)
Delete All For !Visivel And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 1 && Tiago - 30/01/2013 - Deleta dos itens (pedras) que já estăo agregados, para năo dar erro no rateio quando for operaçăo SEPARA PEDRAS
Go Top

_Tpop = TPOPS
If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4)
	Select xPesa
	Set Order To Amarra

	Select Nops, Nenvs, MatPs, Sum(Peso) As Pesos ;
		From xPesa ;
		Group By Nops, Nenvs, MatPs ;
		Into Cursor xRateio

	Select xRateio
	Scan
		_Nops 		  = Nops	
		_Nenv 		  = Nenvs
		_MatP 		  = MatPs
		_Pesagem 	  = Pesos
		_PesoAnterior = 0
		_RecnoRateio  = 0
		
		*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Peso do Conserto
		_PesoConserto = 0
		_PesoAu 	  = 0
		
		Select xNensI
		Set Order To Nenvs

		llTemOuro  = .F.

		If Seek(_Nenv)
			Scan While Nenvs = _Nenv
				If CMats = _MatP
					llTemOuro = .T.
					Exit
				EndIf
			EndScan
			
			*-- Rafael - 08/11/2016 - Quando for envelopagem soma o Peso das OPs para calcular o Peso Total da Pesagem
			If Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.Nivels)
				=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdOpd', 'CrTmpOpd', 'Dopps', CrSigCdOpd.Nivels, 'ChkDests')				
				If CrTmpOpd.ChkDests = 1
					_Pesagem = 0
					
					Select xNensI
					Scan While Nenvs = _Nenv
						If Empty(CMats)
							Loop 
						EndIf 
						_Pesagem = _Pesagem + Pesos
					EndScan
				EndIf 
			EndIf 	

			*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Soma o Peso do Conserto
			Select xNensI
			Go Top
			Scan While Nenvs = _Nenv
				If CMats = 'CONSERTO'
					_PesoConserto = _PesoConserto + Pesos
				EndIf
			EndScan	
			
		Else
			*-- Caso nao tenha envelope localiza o ouro pelo numero da Op
			If Seek(_Nops)
				Scan While Nops = _Nops
					If CMats = _MatP
						llTemOuro = .T.
						Exit
					EndIf
				EndScan

				*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Soma o Peso do Conserto
				Select xNensI
				Go Top
				Scan While Nops = _Nops
					If CMats = 'CONSERTO'
						_PesoConserto = _PesoConserto + Pesos
					EndIf
				EndScan
			EndIf 		
		Endif

		*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Se a Pesagem do Material Conserto for igual a Pesagem da Peça năo lança o Ouro
		If _Pesagem = _PesoConserto And Not Empty(_PesoConserto)
			llTemOuro = .T.
		EndIf 
		
		If Not llTemOuro

*!*				Insert Into xNensI (Nenvs, Nops, Numps, CMats, PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Qtds, Rateio, Peso2s) ;
*!*					Values (_Nenv, _Nenv, TmpNens.Numps, _MatP, _Pesagem, _Pesagem, _Pesagem, 2, _Pesagem)
			
			*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Peso do Conserto
			_PesoAu = _Pesagem
			If Type([_PesoConserto])=[N] And _PesoConserto > 0
				_PesoAu = Iif((_PesoConserto <= _Pesagem),(_Pesagem - _PesoConserto),_Pesagem)
			EndIf 	
			
			Insert Into xNensI (Nenvs, Nops, Numps, CMats, PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Qtds, Rateio, Peso2s) ;
				Values (_Nenv, _Nenv, TmpNens.Numps, _MatP, _PesoAu, _PesoAu, _PesoAu, 2, _PesoAu)

		Endif

		Scan For Rateio = 3 And Nenvs = _Nenv And Not FlagIncs
			_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos
			*Replace Peso2s With xNensI.Pesos In xNensI
			
			*--Rafael - 28/07/2016 - Peso do Conserto
			If CMats = 'CONSERTO' 
				Replace Peso2s With 0 In xNensI
			Endif
		Endscan

		Scan For Rateio = 2 And Nenvs = _Nenv And Not FlagIncs
			If (_RecnoRateio = 0)
				_RecnoRateio = Recno()
			Endif
			_PesoAnterior = _PesoAnterior + PsFaseAnt
		Endscan

		_DiferencaPeso = _Pesagem - _PesoAnterior
		Scan For Rateio = 2 And Nenvs = _Nenv And Not FlagIncs
			*!*				Replace Pesos With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3), ;
			*!*						Qtds  With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
			*!*				_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos

			Replace Pesos With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
			_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos

			*** Tiago - 21/11/2011 - Vianna - Se o produto estiver para controlar QTD e PESO, ai checa através das unidades qual é o campo que está configurado para calcular o peso através do fator
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni', 'CUnis', xNensI.CUnis, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cestos')
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni2', 'CUnis', xNensI.CUniPs, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cestos')
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'CrTmpPro', 'CPros', xNensI.CMats, 'Cgrus')
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'CrTmpGru', 'CGrus', CrTmpPro.Cgrus, 'TpMovs,cores,tams')

			If ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
				Select xNensI
				Replace Qtds  With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
			Else
				If LocalUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(xNensI.CUniPs) And ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni2.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni2.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
					Select xNensI
					Replace Peso2s With (xNensI.Pesos / LocalUni2.Fators) In xNensI
				Endif
			Endif
			***

		Endscan

		If (_RecnoRateio <> 0) And (_Pesagem <> 0)
			Go _RecnoRateio
			Replace Pesos With Pesos + _Pesagem, ;
				Qtds  With Qtds  + _Pesagem
		Endif
	Endscan
Else
	Scan For Rateio = 1 And !CarCompos
		_Nenv 		   = Nenvs
		_Tpop 		   = TPOPS
		_Recno1 	   = Recno()
		_Pesagem 	   = Pesos
		_Qtde 		   = Qtds
		_TotalAnterior = 0
		_PesoAnterior  = 0
		_RecnoRateio   = 0

		If Empty(CMats)
			Scan For Rateio = 3 And (Nenvs = _Nenv Or _CompAgru = 1) And Not FlagIncs
				_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos
				Replace TPOPS With _Tpop
			Endscan

			Scan For Rateio = 2 And (Nenvs = _Nenv Or _CompAgru = 1) And Not FlagIncs
				If (_RecnoRateio = 0)
					_RecnoRateio = Recno()
				Endif

				_PesoAnterior = _PesoAnterior + PsFaseAnt
				Replace TPOPS With _Tpop
			Endscan

			_DiferencaPeso = _Pesagem - _PesoAnterior
			Scan For Rateio = 2 And (Nenvs = _Nenv Or _CompAgru = 1) And Not FlagIncs
				*!*					Replace Pesos With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3), ;
				*!*							Qtds  With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
				*!*					_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos

				Replace Pesos With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
				_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos

				*** Tiago - 21/11/2011 - Vianna - Se o produto estiver para controlar QTD e PESO, ai checa através das unidades qual é o campo que está configurado para calcular o peso através do fator
				Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni', 'CUnis', xNensI.CUnis, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cestos')
				Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni2', 'CUnis', xNensI.CUniPs, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cestos')
				Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'CrTmpPro', 'CPros', xNensI.CMats, 'Cgrus')
				Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'CrTmpGru', 'CGrus', CrTmpPro.Cgrus, 'TpMovs,cores,tams')

				If ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
					Select xNensI
					Replace Qtds  With Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)
				Else
					If LocalUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(xNensI.CUniPs) And ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni2.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni2.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
						Select xNensI
						Replace Peso2s With (xNensI.Pesos / LocalUni2.Fators) In xNensI
					Endif
				Endif
				***
			Endscan

			If (_RecnoRateio <> 0) And (_Pesagem <> 0 Or _Qtde <> 0)
				Go _RecnoRateio
				Replace Pesos With Pesos + _Pesagem, ;
					Qtds  With Qtds + _Pesagem
				_Pesagem = 0
			Endif
		Else
			_CMat = CMats
			If Thisform.pcescolha = 'ALTERAR' And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4 And _CompAgru = 1
				Scan For Inlist(Rateio, 2, 3) And (CMats = _CMat) And (Nenvs = _VNenv )
					If (_RecnoRateio = 0)
						_RecnoRateio = Recno()
					Endif

					_TotalAnterior = _TotalAnterior + QtFaseAnt
					_PesoAnterior  = _PesoAnterior + PsFaseAnt
					Replace TPOPS With _Tpop
				Endscan
			Else
				Scan For Inlist(Rateio, 2, 3) And (CMats = _CMat) And (Nenvs = _Nenv Or _CompAgru = 1)
					If (_RecnoRateio = 0)
						_RecnoRateio = Recno()
					Endif

					_TotalAnterior = _TotalAnterior + QtFaseAnt
					_PesoAnterior  = _PesoAnterior + PsFaseAnt
					Replace TPOPS With _Tpop
				Endscan
			Endif

			If (_TotalAnterior = 0)
				lcNovoTotal = 'Qtds'
			Else
				lcNovoTotal = 'Round(QtFaseAnt + (QtFaseAnt / Iif(_TotalAnterior = 0, 1, _TotalAnterior) * _DiferencaQtde), 3)'
			Endif

			If (_PesoAnterior = 0)
				lcNovoPeso = 'Pesos'
			Else
				lcNovoPeso = 'Round(PsFaseAnt + (PsFaseAnt / Iif(_PesoAnterior = 0, 1, _PesoAnterior) * _DiferencaPeso), 3)'
			Endif

			_DiferencaQtde = _Qtde - _TotalAnterior
			_DiferencaPeso = _Pesagem - _PesoAnterior

			If Thisform.pcescolha = 'ALTERAR' And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4 And _CompAgru = 1
				Scan For Inlist(Rateio, 2, 3) And (CMats = _CMat) And (Nenvs = _Nenv )
					Replace Pesos With &lcNovoPeso,;
						Qtds  With &lcNovoTotal
					If Pesos = 0 And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
						Replace Pesos With 0.001
					Endif
					_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos
					_Qtde = _Qtde - Qtds
				Endscan
			Else
				Scan For Inlist(Rateio, 2, 3) And (CMats = _CMat) And (Nenvs = _Nenv Or _CompAgru = 1)
					Replace Pesos With &lcNovoPeso,;
						Qtds  With &lcNovoTotal
					If Pesos = 0 And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
						Replace Pesos With 0.001
					Endif
					_Pesagem = _Pesagem - Pesos
					_Qtde = _Qtde - Qtds
				Endscan
			Endif

			If (_RecnoRateio <> 0) And (_Pesagem <> 0 Or _Qtde <> 0)
				Go _RecnoRateio
				Replace Pesos With Pesos + _Pesagem, ;
					Qtds  With Qtds + _Qtde
				If Pesos = 0 And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
					Replace Pesos With 0.001
				Endif
				_Pesagem = 0
			Endif
		Endif
		Go _Recno1
	Endscan
Endif

Select xMFas
Set Order To Nops
Replace All PesoAntigo With Pesos
Replace All Pesos With 0

Select xNensI
Set Order To Gravar
*Delete All For Empty(Nops)
*!*	Sum Pesos To _TotGrava For Not Servicos
Sum Pesos To _TotGrava For Not Servicos And Iif(!CarCompos Or (CarCompos And Rateio <> 5),.T.,.F.)
If (_TotPeso <> _TotGrava) And Not Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4) And Not Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras,4)
	
	*-- ATUALIZA O NUMERO DA OP	
	_MatP     = Space(14)
	_nEnvs    = 0
	_nOps     = 0
	_Peso     = 0
	_PesAnt   = 0
	_PesGrava = 0
	_Servico  = .F.
	
	Select xMFas
	Scan
		lcsql = [Select MatPrincs,Cgrus From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+xMFas.codpds+[']
		Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

		lcsql = [Select Mercs From SigCdGrp Where Cgrus = ']+LocalPro.Cgrus+[']
		Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalGru')

		lcsql = [Select MatPrincs From SigCdGpr Where Codigos = ']+LocalGru.Mercs+[']
		Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalGgrp')

		*--Rafael - 05/09/2016 - 
		lcSql = [Select Emps, Dopes, Numes, Qtds, CodCors, CodTams, Empds, CodTgops, citens From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(xMFas.Nops)
		Thisform.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')

		lcSql = [Select Globalizas, servicos From SigCdOpe Where Dopes = ']+LocalOpi.Dopes+[']
		ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpe')
		
		If Not _Servico
			_Servico = (LocalOpe.Servicos = 1)
		EndIf 	
		
		Select xMFas
		_Mat = Iif(!Empty(LocalPro.MatPrincs),LocalPro.MatPrincs,Iif(!Empty(LocalGgrp.MatPrincs),LocalGgrp.MatPrincs,CrSigCdPam.Ouros))
		
		If _Servico 

			_nEnvs  = xMFas.Nenvs
			_nOps   = xMFas.Nops
			
			*--Rafael - 05/09/2016 - 
			_PesAnt = xMFas.PesoAntigo

			If Not Empty(_Mat)
				_MatP = _Mat
			Endif

			_MatP = Iif(Empty(_MatP), CrSigCdPam.Ouros, _MatP)

			Select csCompOps
			Select * from csCompOps Where Nenvs = _nEnvs And Nops = _nOps Into Cursor csResCpOs ReadWrite

			Select csResCpOs
			_Peso = csResCpOs.Pesos
			_PesGrava = _Peso - _PesAnt

			If Reccount()=0
				Select csCompOps
				Select * from csCompOps Where Empty(Nenvs) And Empty(Nops) Into Cursor csResCpOs ReadWrite
				Select csResCpOs
				_Peso = csResCpOs.Pesos
				_PesGrava = _Peso
			EndIf
			
			If _PesGrava <> 0 
				
				Select xMFas
				Insert Into xNensI (Numps, CMats, PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Qtds, Rateio, TPOPS, FlagIncs, Nenvs, Nops) ;
					Values (TmpNens.Numps, _MatP, _PesGrava, _PesGrava, _PesGrava, 2, _Tpop,.T., _nEnvs, _nOps)
					
			EndIf 		

		Else
		
			If Not Empty(_Mat)
				_MatP = _Mat
				Exit
			Endif
		EndIf 
	Endscan
	
	If Not _Servico
		_MatP = Iif(Empty(_MatP), CrSigCdPam.Ouros, _MatP)

		_PesGrava = _TotPeso - _TotGrava

		Insert Into xNensI (Nenvs, Nops, Numps, CMats, PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Qtds, Rateio, TPOPS, FlagIncs) ;
			Values (Nenvs, Nops, TmpNens.Numps, _MatP, _PesGrava, _PesGrava, _PesGrava, 2, _Tpop,.T.)
			
	EndIf 
Endif

***** Se năo aceita retrabalho, verifica se é retrabalho e faz estorno (gera registro de estorno no cursor) ****
*!*	Select * From xNensi Where 0 = 1 Into Cursor LocalNensI ReadWrite
*!*	Select xNensI
*!*	GO TOP
*!*	Scan For Qtds <> 0 Or Pesos <> 0 Or Peso2s <> 0 Or CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1
*!*		IF xNensi.retrab = 0 and servicos
*!*			lcSql = [Select * From SigCdNei Where cmats = '] + xNensi.cmats+[' and tpops = '] + xNensi.tpOps + [']
*!*			ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalNei')
*!*			SELECT LocalNei
*!*			DELETE all for nops<>xNensi.nOps and not servicos
*!*			Index On Str(estorno,1) Tag Esto
*!*			If Not Seek("1",'LocalNei','Esto')
*!*				GO top
*!*				SCAN
*!*				** gera estorno se ainda nao houver **
*!*				IF nops = xNensi.nOps and servicos and estorno = 0
*!*					SCATTER memvar memo
*!*					m.estorno = 1
*!*					Insert Into LocalNensI from memvar
*!*				ENDIF
*!*				ENDSCAN
*!*			ELSE
*!*				SCATTER memvar memo
*!*				Insert Into LocalNensI from memvar
*!*			ENDIF
*!*		ENDIF
*!*	ENDSCAN
*!*	SELECT XNensi
*!*	Append From Dbf('LocalNensI')
*******************************************************

&&Select * From CrSigCdNei Where 0 = 1 Into Cursor LocalNensI ReadWrite
Select * From xNensI Where 0 = 1 Into Cursor LocalNensI Readwrite
Select LocalNensI
Index On Str(Nenvs,10) + Str(Nops,10) + Str(nLotes,10) + CMats + Cats + TPOPS + CodCors + CodTams + Str(estorno) Tag Gravar

Select xNensI
Go Top
Scan For Qtds <> 0 Or Pesos <> 0 Or Peso2s <> 0 Or CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1
	Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'LocalPro', 'CPros', xNensI.CMats, 'CGrus, Varias, Dpros, MoeCusfs, CustoFs, pVens, Moevs ')
	Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'LocalGru', 'CGrus', LocalPro.Cgrus, 'CEstoqs,TipoEstos,pvCompos,Semiacabs')
	Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpOpt', 'LocalOpt', 'Cods',  xNensI.TPOPS, 'AnaEsGrps')

	_pCor = xNensI.CodCors
	_pTam = xNensI.CodTams

	lnNop = xNensI.Nops
	If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4) And xNensI.Nops = 0
		lnNop = xNensI.Nenvs
	Endif

	lcBusca = Str(xNensI.Nenvs,10)+Str(lnNop,10)+Str(xNensI.nLotes,10)+xNensI.CMats+xNensI.Cats+xNensI.TPOPS+;
		xNensI.CodCors+xNensI.CodTams+Str(estorno)

	If Not Seek(lcBusca,'LocalNensI','Gravar')
		Insert Into LocalNensI (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, Nenvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, TPOPS, Cats, Obss, ;
			FlagIncs, Fators, Moedas, Servicos, GrupoFins, CodCors, CodTams, ;
			nLotes, PesoFixs, cIdChaves, EmpDNPs, Pvens, estorno) ;
			Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, lnNop, xNensI.Nenvs, xNensI.CMats, ;
			LocalPro.Dpros, xNensI.CUnis, xNensI.TPOPS, xNensI.Cats, xNensI.Obss, ;
			xNensI.FlagIncs, xNensI.Fators, xNensI.Moedas, xNensI.Servicos, xNensI.GrupoFins, ;
			xNensI.CodCors, xNensI.CodTams, xNensI.nLotes, xNensI.PesoFixs, fUniqueIds(), ;
			TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10), xNensI.Pvens, xNensI.estorno)

		If (CrSigCdOpd.PesoFixs = 1) And (LocalPro.Varias = 1)
			Replace PesoFixs With 1 In LocalNensI
		Endif

		If LocalGru.pvCompos = 2
			Replace CustoFs  With LocalPro.Pvens,;
				MoeCusfs With LocalPro.Moevs In LocalNensI
		Else
			Replace CustoFs  With LocalPro.CustoFs,;
				MoeCusfs With LocalPro.MoeCusfs In LocalNensI
		Endif

	Endif
	Replace Peso2s With Peso2s + xNensI.Peso2s,;
		AQtds  With AQtds  + xNensI.AQtds ,;
		Qtds   With Qtds   + xNensI.Qtds  ,;
		Pesos  With Pesos  + xNensI.Pesos In LocalNensI
	If LocalNensI.Servicos And LocalNensI.Nops = 0 And LocalNensI.Nenvs > 0
		Replace Nops With Nenvs In LocalNensI
	Endif

	If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs, 1, 2) And (CrSigCdOpd.BxOEsts = 2) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1 And LocalGru.Semiacabs <> 1) && Tiago - 13/10/2015 - Quando for semiacabado năo dá saída na origem pois só movimenta a composiçăo
		_Oper = Iif(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs = 1, 'E', 'S')

		xOper = _Oper
		*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
		*!*			If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests,1,2)
		*!*				xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
		*!*			Endif

		llOk = .T.
		If ( LocalOpt.AnaEsGrps # ' ' And LocalOpt.AnaEsGrps # _Oper )
			llOk = .F.
		Endif
		If llOk
			lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999') + Thisform.sigkey
			pSeq  = fGerUniqueKey('HISTBAR')
			
			Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Empos, Qtds, Grupos, ;
				Estos, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, DtAlts, OriDopNums, Seqs, Pesos, ;
				CodCors, CodTams, Obs ) ;
				Values (Usuar, Datetime(), Thisform.pEmps, _Oper, TmpNens.Dopps, xNensI.Numps, TmpNens.DataS, ;
				xNensI.CMats, Thisform.pEmps, xNensI.Qtds, TmpNens.GrupoOs, TmpNens.Contaos, lcIds, ;
				ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(xNensI.Numps, 6), ;
				ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.GrupoOs + TmpNens.Contaos, ;
				Datetime(), Thisform.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps,6), pSeq, ;
				Iif(xNensI.CMats='CONSERTO',_TotGrava,xNensI.Peso2s), _pCor, _pTam, TmpNens.Obss)  &&_TotGrava, _pCor, _pTam, TmpNens.Obss) && 
			=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
			=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )
		Endif
	Endif

	If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests, 1, 2) And (CrSigCdOpd.BxDEsts = 2) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1 And LocalGru.Semiacabs <> 1) && Tiago - 13/10/2015 - Quando for semiacabado năo dá entrada no destino pois só movimenta a composiçăo
		_Oper = Iif(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests = 1, 'E', 'S')

		xOper = _Oper
		*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
		*!*			If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs,1,2)
		*!*				xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
		*!*			Endif

		llOk = .T.
		If ( LocalOpt.AnaEsGrps # ' ' And LocalOpt.AnaEsGrps # _Oper )
			llOk = .F.
		Endif
		If llOk
			lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey
			pSeq  = fGerUniqueKey('HISTBAR')

			Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Empos, Qtds, Grupos, ;
				Estos, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, DtAlts, OriDopNums, Seqs, Pesos, ;
				CodCors, CodTams, Obs ) ;
				Values (Usuar, Datetime(), Thisform.pEmps, _Oper, TmpNens.Dopps, xNensI.Numps, TmpNens.DataS, ;
				xNensI.CMats, Thisform.pEmps, xNensI.Qtds, TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, lcIds, ;
				ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(xNensI.Numps, 6), ;
				ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.Grupods + TmpNens.Contads, ;
