				Datetime(), Thisform.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(xNensI.Numps, 6), pSeq, ;
				xNensI.Peso2s, _pCor, _pTam, TmpNens.Obss)

			=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
			=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )
		Endif
	Endif

	*** Tiago - 24/04/2013 - Comentei para quando for separaçăo de pedras checar através do campo NENVS, pois ao incluir um item avulso năo é gravado o NOPS
	*!*		Select xMFas
	*!*		If Not Empty(xNensi.Nops) And Seek(xNensi.Nops) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1)
	*!*			Replace Pesos With xMFas.Pesos + xNensi.Pesos In xMFas
	*!*		EndIf

	Select xMFas
	If (Not Empty(xNensI.Nops) And Seek(xNensI.Nops) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1)) Or (Not Empty(xNensI.Nenvs) And Seek(xNensI.Nenvs) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1)) And LocalGru.Semiacabs <> 1 && Tiago - 13/10/2015 - Quando for semiacabado năo agrega pois agrega os componentes dele
		Replace Pesos With xMFas.Pesos + xNensI.Pesos In xMFas
	Endif

	** Grava pagamento de serviço **
	If (LocalGru.CEstoqs <> 1) And xNensI.Servicos And (xNensI.Qtds <> 0) And ((!TmpNens.Retrabs And xNensI.Fators <> 0) Or (TmpNens.Retrabs And xNensI.Coefs <> 0))
		*!*		If (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1) And xNensi.Servicos And (xNensi.Qtds <> 0) And (xNensi.Fators <> 0) Tiago - 25/08/11 - Comentei
		pDat = Thisform.Pagina.Dados.cntDados.Dt_Data.Value

		lcQuery = [Select Top 1 Datas, Horas, Valos ] + ;
			[From SigCdCot ] + ;
			[Where CMoes = '] + xNensI.Moedas + [' And ] + ;
			[Datas <= ?pDat ] + ;
			[Order By Datas Desc, Horas Desc, Valos Asc]

		If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalCot') < 1)
			=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalCot)')
			Return .F.
		Endif
		Select LocalCot
		Go Top

		_Cota = 1
		If Not Eof('LocalCot') And (LocalCot.Valos <> 0)
			_Cota = LocalCot.Valos
		Endif

		_Grupo = TmpNens.GrupoOs
		_Conta = TmpNens.Contaos

		If (CrSigCdOpd.PagServs = 1)
			_Grupo = TmpNens.Grupods
			_Conta = TmpNens.Contads
		Endif

		*** Tiago - 04/09/11 - Valor do serviço a ser lançado varia de acordo com o percentual do cargo do funcionário. Se estiver sem cargo năo lança pagamento
		lcQuery = [Select a.comis from SigCdCrg a inner join SigCdCli b on a.CCargs = b.CCargs where Iclis = '] + _Conta + [']
		If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalCar') < 1)
			=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalCar)')
			Return .F.
		Endif
		Select LocalCar
		Go Top
		If Eof()
			Messagebox([Funcionário năo possui cargo. Năo será lançado pagamento de serviços.],48,[Aviso])
			Loop
		Endif
		***

		Select crSigMvCcr
		_Noper = fGerUniqueKey('SigMvCcr')

		****	retirado em 17/03/2011 **** Tiago - 25/08/11 - Descomentei
		If TmpNens.Retrabs And xNensI.Coefs # 0
			_Valor = Round(xNensI.Coefs * xNensI.Qtds, 2) &&Round((xNensi.Coefs * xNensi.Qtds * LocalCar.Comis) / 100, 2)
			_Fator = xNensI.Coefs &&(xNensi.Coefs * LocalCar.Comis) / 100
		Else
			_Valor = Round(xNensI.Fators * xNensI.Qtds, 2) &&Round((xNensi.Fators * xNensi.Qtds * LocalCar.Comis) / 100, 2)
			_Fator = xNensI.Fators &&(xNensi.Fators * LocalCar.Comis) / 100
		Endif

		*** Tiago - 25/08/11 - Comentei
		*!*			_Valor = xNensi.pvens*xNensi.qtds*xNensi.fators/100	&& calcula valor do pagamento
		*!*			_Fator = xNensi.Fators

		If _Valor = 0
			Loop
		Endif

		If Empty(CrSigCdOpd.Hists)
			_Hist = Alltrim(xNensI.CMats) + ' - ' + ;
				Alltrim(Transform(xNensI.Qtds, '9,999.99')) + ;
				' x ' + Alltrim(Transform(_Fator, '999.99')) + xNensI.Moedas
			*!*						Iif(Not Empty(xNensi.Nenvs),'E:'+Alltrim(str(xNensi.Nenvs)),'')
		Else
			_Hist = Alltrim(CrSigCdOpd.Hists)
		Endif
		_Hist2 = Iif(TmpNens.Retrabs,'(RT)','') + Alltrim(xNensI.Dopps) + Alltrim(Str(xNensI.Numps))

		xOper  = 'C'
		xSoper = 'D'

		If _Valor < 0
			xOper  = 'D'
			xSoper = 'C'
			_Valor = Abs(_Valor)
		Endif

		If xNensI.estorno = 1		&& troca a operacao caso seja estorno
			xOper  = 'D'
			xSoper = 'C'
			_Hist = 'Estorno:' + Alltrim(xNensI.CMats) + ' - ' + Alltrim(Transform(xNensI.Pvens, '999,999.99')) + ;
				' x ' + Alltrim(Transform(xNensI.Qtds, '999,999.99')) + ;
				' x ' + Alltrim(Transform(_Fator, '9,999.9999')) + '% ' + xNensI.Moedas
		Endif

		lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) + Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey
		_numcs = fGerUniqueKey(lcDopcs) &&xNensi.dopcs)		&& cria id par contas a pagar

		Insert Into crSigMvCcr (NOpers, Emps, DataS, UsuAlts, DatAlts, Vencs, Hists, Autos, Dopes, Numes, Tipos, ;
			ContaPgs, Opers, Grupos, Contas, Moedas, Cotacaos, Valors, SOpers, SGrupos, SContas, ;
			SMoedas, SCotacaos, SValors, cIdChaves, GruConMoes, EmpDopNums, EmpDopNcs, Pagos, Hist2s,;
			dopcs, numcs) ;
			Values (_Noper, Thisform.pEmps, TmpNens.DataS, Usuar, Datetime(), TmpNens.DataS, _Hist, .T., ;
			TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, 'X', 0, xOper, _Grupo, _Conta, xNensI.Moedas, _Cota, ;
			_Valor, xSoper, xNensI.GrupoFins, _Conta, xNensI.Moedas, _Cota, _Valor, lcIds, ;
			_Grupo + _Conta + xNensI.Moedas, Thisform.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), ;
			ThisForm.pEmps + lcDopcs + Str(_numcs, 6), Iif(_Valor = 0, '0', '1'), _Hist2, ;
			lcDopcs, _numcs)

		=fRecalculaS( crSigMvCcr.Grupos, crSigMvCcr.Contas, crSigMvCcr.DataS, crSigMvCcr.Moedas, Thisform.poDataMgr)

		lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) + Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey

		Insert Into crSigMvCcr (NOpers, Emps, DataS, UsuAlts, DatAlts, Vencs, Hists, Autos, Dopes, Numes, Tipos, ;
			ContaPgs, SOpers, SGrupos, SContas, SMoedas, SCotacaos, SValors, Opers, Grupos, ;
			Contas, Moedas, Cotacaos, Valors, cIdChaves, GruConMoes, EmpDopNums, EmpDopNcs, Pagos, ;
			Hist2s, dopcs, numcs ) ;
			Values (_Noper, Thisform.pEmps, TmpNens.DataS, Usuar, Datetime(), TmpNens.DataS, _Hist, .T., ;
			TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, 'X', 0, xOper, _Grupo, _Conta, xNensI.Moedas, _Cota, ;
			_Valor, xSoper, xNensI.GrupoFins, _Conta, xNensI.Moedas, _Cota, _Valor, lcIds, ;
			xNensI.GrupoFins + _Conta + xNensI.Moedas, Thisform.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), ;
			ThisForm.pEmps + lcDopcs + Str(_numcs, 6), Iif(_Valor = 0, '0', '1'), ;
			_Hist2, lcDopcs, _numcs)

		=fRecalculaS( crSigMvCcr.Grupos, crSigMvCcr.Contas, crSigMvCcr.DataS, crSigMvCcr.Moedas, Thisform.poDataMgr)
	Endif

	Select xNensI
Endscan

Select CrSigCdNei
Append From Dbf('LocalNensI')

*!*	If (Not InList(crSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4))
If CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 4 &&& Tiago - 28/03/2012 - Vianna - Antes năo gerava histórico de fase quando era separaçăo de pedra; mudei para năo gerar quando for devoluçăo
	Select xMFas
	Scan
		If (CrSigCdOpd.Seqs = 1) And (CrSigCdOpd.GrOdns <> 2)
			lcQuery = [Select Ordems, Grupos ] + ;
				[From SigCdPrf ] + ;
				[Where Produtos = '] + xMFas.codpds + [' And ] + ;
				[Ordems = ] + Alltrim(Str(xMFas.Ordems + 1)) + [ ] + ;
				[Order By Ordems, Grupos]

			If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalProF') < 1)
				=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalProF)')
				Return .F.
			Endif

			Select LocalProf
			Go Top
			If (LocalProf.Grupos = TmpNens.Grupods)
				_Ordem = xMFas.Ordems + 1
			Else
				lcQuery = [Select Grupos, Ordems ] + ;
					[From SigCdPrf ] + ;
					[Where Produtos = '] + xMFas.codpds + [' And ] + ;
					[Grupos = '] + TmpNens.Grupods + [' And ] + ;
					[Ordems = ] + Alltrim(Str(xMFas.Ordems + 1)) + [ ] + ;
					[Order By Grupos, Ordems]

				If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalProF') < 1)
					=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalProF)')
					Return .F.
				Endif

				Select LocalProf
				Go Top
				If (LocalProf.Grupos = TmpNens.Grupods)
					_Ordem = LocalProf.Ordems
				Else
					If Not Bof()
						Skip - 1
					Endif
					If (LocalProf.Grupos = TmpNens.Grupods)
						_Ordem = LocalProf.Ordems
					Else
						lcQuery = [Select Grupos, Ordems ] + ;
							[From SigCdPrf ] + ;
							[Where Produtos = '] + xMFas.codpds + [' And ] + ;
							[Grupos = '] + TmpNens.Grupods + [' ] + ;
							[Order By Grupos, Ordems]

						If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalProF') < 1)
							=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalProF)')
							Return .F.
						Endif

						Select LocalProf
						Go Top
						If (LocalProf.Grupos = TmpNens.Grupods)
							_Ordem = LocalProf.Ordems
						Else
							_Ordem = 1
						Endif
					Endif
				Endif
			Endif
		Else
			_Ordem = xMFas.Ordems
		Endif

		If CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1
			If CrSigCdOpd.Seqs = 1
				_Ordem = xMFas.Ordems
			Else
				_Ordem = 1
			Endif
		Endif

		Select xMFas
		If (Pesos = 0) And CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops <> 1
			Replace Pesos With PesoAntigo
		Endif

		Insert Into crSigPdMvf (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datars, DataS, Usuars, Opers, GrupoOs, Contaos, Grupods,;
			Contads, Nops, Nenvs, Dopes, Numes, Dataps, Dataes, Obss, codpds, Unids, ;
			Pesos, Qtds, Obsps, Inicios, Finals, Ordems, cRetrabs, cIdChaves, EmpDNPs, ;
			EmpDopNums, TmpMins, OrdemOs  ) ;
			Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, Datetime(), TmpNens.DataS, Usuar, ;
			xMFas.Opers, TmpNens.GrupoOs, TmpNens.Contaos, TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, ;
			xMFas.Nops, xMFas.Nenvs, xMFas.Dopes, xMFas.Numes, TmpNens.DataS, xMFas.Dataes, ;
			xMFas.Obss, xMFas.codpds, xMFas.Unids, xMFas.Pesos, xMFas.Qtds, xMFas.Obsps, ;
			xMFas.Inicios, xMFas.Finals, _Ordem, Iif(TmpNens.Retrabs, xMFas.cRetrabs, ''), ;
			Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)+Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)),"@L 999999")+Thisform.sigkey , ;
			TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10), ;
			TmpNens.Emps + xMFas.Dopes +Str(xMFas.Numes, 6), xMFas.TmpMins, ;
			xMFas.Ordems )
	Endscan
Endif

Select xNensiS  &&Serviços
Scan
	If Empty(ContaFs)
		Loop
	Endif
	Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'LocalPro', 'CPros', xNensiS.CMats, 'CGrus, Varias, MoeCusfs, CustoFs, pvens, Moevs ')
	Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'LocalGru', 'CGrus', LocalPro.Cgrus, 'CEstoqs, pvCompos')

	Insert Into CrSigCdNei (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, Nenvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, TPOPS, Cats, Obss, AQtds, ;
		Qtds, Pesos, FlagIncs, Fators, Moedas, Servicos, GrupoFins, Obss, nLotes, PesoFixs, ;
		cIdChaves, EmpDNPs, GrupoFs, ContaFs, cRetrabs, CoefInfs, Coefs, Pvens ) ;
		Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xNensiS.Nops, xNensiS.Nenvs, xNensiS.CMats, ;
		xNensiS.CDescs, xNensiS.CUnis, xNensiS.TPOPS, xNensiS.Cats, xNensiS.Obss, xNensiS.AQtds, ;
		xNensiS.Qtds, xNensiS.Pesos, xNensiS.FlagIncs, xNensiS.Fators, xNensiS.Moedas, ;
		xNensiS.Servicos, xNensiS.GrupoFins, xNensiS.Obss, xNensiS.nLotes, xNensiS.PesoFixs, ;
		fUniqueIds(), TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10), xNensiS.GrupoFs,;
		xNensiS.ContaFs, xNensiS.cRetrabs, xNensiS.CoefInfs, xNensiS.Coefs, xNensiS.Pvens)

	If LocalGru.pvCompos = 2
		Replace CustoFs  With LocalPro.Pvens,;
			MoeCusfs With LocalPro.Moevs In LocalNensI
	Else
		Replace CustoFs  With LocalPro.CustoFs,;
			MoeCusfs With LocalPro.MoeCusfs In LocalNensI
	Endif

Endscan

Select xNensiJ &&Justificativas
Scan
	If Empty(Cods)
		Loop
	Endif
	Insert Into CrSigPrJus (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, Nenvs, cIdChaves, EmpDNPs, cRetrabs, Cods ) ;
		Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xNensiJ.Nops, xNensiJ.Nenvs, ;
		fUniqueIds(), TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10), ;
		xNensiJ.cRetrabs, xNensiJ.Cods )
Endscan

If (CrSigCdOpd.ExclSubns = 1)
	Select xMFas
	Scan
		lcQuery = [Select CidChaves From SigPdMvf ] + ;
			[Where Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(xMFas.Nops)) + [ And ] + ;
			[Emps = '] + TmpNens.Emps + [' And ] + ;
			[Dopps = '] + TmpNens.Dopps + [' And ] + ;
			[Numps <> ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.Numps))
		If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmpMfad') < 1)
			=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Delete 1- SigPdMvf)')
			Return .F.
		Endif

		Select TmpMfad
		Scan
			lcQuery = [Delete From SigPdMvf Where CidChaves = ']+TmpMfad.cIdChaves+[']
			If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Delete 2 - SigPdMvf)')
				Return .F.
			Endif
		Endscan
	Endscan
Endif

*** Tiago - 27/09/2012 - Se existir o cursor xTotPed é porque tem pedidos que foram finalizados totalmente. Essa rotina grava a data de fechamento do pedido
*!*	If Used('xTotPed')
*!*	Select xTotPed
*!*	Scan
*!*		lcChv = xTotPed.Emps + xTotPed.Dopes + Str(xTotPed.Numes, 6)

*!*	*!*		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalMvCab', 'EmpDopNums', lcChv, 'cIdChaves, DtFechas')

*!*		lcQuery = [Update SigMvCab ] + ;
*!*					 [Set DtFechas = ?xTotPed.DtFechas ] + ;
*!*				   [Where EmpDopNums = ?lcChv] &&'] + LocalEest.cIdChaves + [']

*!*		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
*!*			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Update - SigMvCab)')
*!*			Return .f.
*!*		EndIf
*!*	Endscan
*!*	Endif

*** Tiago - 27/09/2012 - Processando os Pedidos Baixados Por Completo.  Essa rotina grava a data de fechamento do pedido
If CrSigCdOpd.BxAutos = 1 And (Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4) Or CrSigCdOpd.Pccs)
	Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Processando Pedidos Baixados Por Completo... ' Nowait

	Create Cursor xTotPed (Emps c(3), Dopes c(20), Numes N(6)) &&, MascNum c(6), NConta c(50), Repres c(50), Flag n(1), DtFechas d )
	Index On Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes, 6) Tag EmpDopNum

	Select xMFas
	Scan
		_Aberto = .F.
		Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpPic', 'LocalOpi', 'Nops', xMFas.Nops, 'Emps, Dopes, Numes, EmpDs, Dopps, Nops')
		Select LocalOpi
		Scan
			lcEmp = Iif(Empty(LocalOpi.EmpDs), LocalOpi.Emps, LocalOpi.EmpDs)
			lcEdn = lcEmp + LocalOpi.Dopes + Str(LocalOpi.Numes, 6)

			If Not Seek(lcEdn, 'xTotPed')
				Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalEest', 'EmpDopNums', lcEdn, 'ContaOs, ContaDs, Vends')

				Insert Into xTotPed (Emps, Dopes, Numes) ;
					Values (lcEmp, LocalOpi.Dopes, LocalOpi.Numes)
			Endif
		Endscan
	Endscan

	Select xTotPed
	Scan
		lcChave = Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes, 6)
		_Aberto = .F.

		Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigOpPic', 'LocalOpi', 'EmpDopNums', lcChave, 'Emps, Dopps, Nops')
		Select LocalOpi
		Scan
			lcChaveP = Emps + Dopps + Str(Nops, 10)

			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdNec', 'LocalNens', 'EmpDNPs', lcChaveP, 'ChkSubn')
			If Not LocalNens.ChkSubn
				_Aberto = .T.
				Exit
			Endif
		Endscan

		If Not _Aberto
			lcChv = xTotPed.Emps + xTotPed.Dopes + Str(xTotPed.Numes, 6)

			*!*		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigMvCab', 'LocalMvCab', 'EmpDopNums', lcChv, 'cIdChaves, DtFechas')

			lcQuery = [Update SigMvCab ] + ;
				[Set DtFechas = ?TmpNens.Datas ] + ;
				[Where EmpDopNums = ?lcChv] &&'] + LocalEest.cIdChaves + [']

			If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Update - SigMvCab)')
				Return .F.
			Endif
		Endif
	Endscan
Endif
***

If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4) Or (CrSigCdOpd.BxOEsts = 1) Or (CrSigCdOpd.BxDEsts = 1)
	If Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs,1,3,4)
		_TotPeso = 0

		Select Nenvs, Sum(Qtds) As Qtds ;
			From xPesa ;
			Group By Nenvs ;
			Into Cursor TPesa

		Select a.Nenvs, Sum(a.Pesos) As Pesos, b.Qtds ;
			From xNensI a, TPesa b ;
			Where Not a.Visivel And ;
			a.Rateio = 3 And ;
			a.Nenvs = b.Nenvs ;
			Group By a.Nenvs, b.Qtds ;
			Into Cursor xRateio

		Select xRateio
		Index On Nenvs Tag Nenvs
		Select xPesa
		Scan
			_Nenv = Nenvs
			_Pesagem = Peso
			Select xRateio
			If Seek(_Nenv) And (xRateio.Pesos <> 0) And (CrSigCdOpd.PesMatPs)
				xRat = ((xRateio.Pesos / xRateio.Qtds) * xPesa.Qtds)
				Select xPesa
				Replace Peso2 With xPesa.Peso - xRat In xPesa
			Else
				Select xPesa
				Replace Peso2 With xPesa.Peso In xPesa
			Endif
		Endscan
	Endif

	Select xPesa
	Scan
		lcsql = [Select a.Cgrus, b.cestoqs, c.Etiqs, b.TipoEstos, c.CEstos, a.CUnis, a.CUnips From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b, SigCdUni c Where a.Cpros = ']+xPesa.CPros+[' ]+;
			[And a.Cgrus = b.cgrus And a.Cunis = c.CUnis ]
		=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

		_pCor = xPesa.Cors
		_pTam = xPesa.Tams

		xQtde  = xPesa.Qtds

		Do While xQtde > 0
			Select xPesa
			If xPesa.Divs
				If xQtde - 1 > 0
					xQtde  = xQtde - 1
					QtdGrv = 1
					Ps2Grv = Round(xPesa.Peso2 / xPesa.Qtds,3)
					PesGrv = Round(xPesa.Peso  / xPesa.Qtds,3)
				Else
					QtdGrv = xQtde
					Ps2Grv = xPesa.Peso2 - ( ( xPesa.Qtds - xQtde ) * Round(xPesa.Peso2 / xPesa.Qtds,3) )
					PesGrv = xPesa.Peso  - ( ( xPesa.Qtds - xQtde ) * Round(xPesa.Peso  / xPesa.Qtds,3) )
					xQtde  = 0
				Endif
			Else
				xQtde  = 0
				QtdGrv = xPesa.Qtds
				Ps2Grv = xPesa.Peso2
				PesGrv = xPesa.Peso
			Endif

			*** Tiago - 22/11/2011 - Vianna - Se o produto estiver para controlar QTD e PESO, ai checa através das unidades qual é o campo que está configurado para calcular o peso através do fator
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni', 'CUnis', LocalPro.CUnis, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cEstos')
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'LocalUni2', 'CUnis', LocalPro.CUniPs, 'Fators,QtEqualPs,cEstos')
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'CrTmpGru', 'CGrus', LocalPro.Cgrus, 'TpMovs')

			If ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
				*** Mantem o cálculo normal de GR
			Else
				If LocalUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(LocalPro.CUniPs) And ( ( CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni2.Fators <> 1 ) Or ( LocalUni2.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
					Ps2Grv = Ps2Grv / LocalUni2.Fators
					PesGrv = PesGrv / LocalUni2.Fators
				Endif
			Endif
			***
			
			*-- Rafael - 05/09/2016 - Peso do Conserto
			_Servico = .F.
			lcSql = [Select Globalizas, servicos From SigCdOpe Where Dopes = ']+xPesa.Dopes+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'crConserto')
			
			If Not _Servico
				_Servico = (crConserto.Servicos = 1)
				*-- Rafael - 05/09/2016 - Se tem essa variavel preenchida é um CONSERTO
				If _Servico 
					*-- Rafael - 05/09/2016 - Nessa Variável está o peso que deve ser usado na etiqueta, como sendo o peso atual da peça
					Ps2Grv = xPesa.Peso &&- xPesa.Peso2 
				EndIf
			EndIf

			Select xPesa
			llChkUni = Iif(CrSigCdOpd.ChkUnis <> 1,.T.,Iif(LocalPro.Etiqs = [S],.T.,.F.) )
			
			If (Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs,1,4) And llChkUni ) And LocalPro.CEstoqs <> 2 And ( CrSigCdOpd.BxOEsts = 1 Or CrSigCdOpd.BxDEsts = 1 )
				If (xPesa.Cbars > 0) And Not xPesa.Divs And CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 1
					CodBarra = xPesa.Cbars
					CodCor   = xPesa.Cors
					CodTam   = xPesa.Tams

					Replace Cbars With CodBarra In xPesa

					Insert Into crSigOpEtq (Cbars, CPros, Pesos, Qtds, Emps, Dopes, Numes, DataS, Empos, Grupos, Contas, ;
						DopeOs, NumeOs, Nops, ObsEtiqs, CodCors, CodTams, DtMovs, Usados, Peso2s, EmpDopNums, ;
						DtIncs, Pesoms, usuLibs, CustoFs ) ;
						Values (CodBarra, xPesa.CPros, Ps2Grv, QtdGrv, TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, ;
						TmpNens.Numps, TmpNens.DataS, xPesa.Emps, TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, ;
						xPesa.Dopes, xPesa.Numes, xPesa.Nops, xPesa.Obs, xPesa.Cors, xPesa.Tams, Datetime(), .T., PesGrv - Ps2Grv, ;
						TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), ;
						Datetime(), xPesa.Pesoms, xPesa.usuLibs, xPesa.CustoFs )
				Else
					Cbar  = Transform(fGerUniqueKey('SigOpEtq'), '@L 9999999999999')
					Cbar1 = fDigVerificador(Cbar)
					Cbar2 = Cbar + Transform(Cbar1, '@L 9')
					Set Decimals To 0
					CodBarra = Val(Cbar2)
					CodCor   = xPesa.Cors
					CodTam   = xPesa.Tams
					Set Decimals To 2
					Replace Cbars With CodBarra In xPesa

					Insert Into crSigOpEtq (Cbars, CPros, Pesos, Qtds, Emps, Dopes, Numes, DataS, Empos, Grupos, Contas, ;
						DopeOs, NumeOs, Nops, ObsEtiqs, CodCors, CodTams, DtMovs, Peso2s, ;
						EmpDopNums, DtIncs, Pesoms, usuLibs, CustoFs ) ;
						Values (CodBarra, xPesa.CPros, Ps2Grv, QtdGrv, TmpNens.Emps, ;
						TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, TmpNens.DataS, xPesa.Emps, TmpNens.Grupods, ;
						TmpNens.Contads, xPesa.Dopes, xPesa.Numes, xPesa.Nops, xPesa.Obs, xPesa.Cors, ;
						xPesa.Tams, Datetime(), PesGrv - Ps2Grv, ;
						TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6),;
						Datetime(), xPesa.Pesoms, xPesa.usuLibs, xPesa.CustoFs )
				Endif
				*** Tiago - 17/11/2010 - Atualiza codbarras em SigOpPic, para buscar o item certo na hora da venda com substituiçăo
				lcQuery = [Update SigOpPic ] + ;
					[Set codbarras = ?xPesa.cbars ] + ;
					[Where nOps = ?xPesa.nOps and citens = ?xPesa.citens]

				If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Update - SigOpPic)')
					Return .F.
				Endif
			Else
				CodBarra = 0
				CodCor   = xPesa.Cors
				CodTam   = xPesa.Tams
				If (CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 3 Or (CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 1 And Not llChkUni) ) And ( CrSigCdOpd.BxOEsts = 1 Or CrSigCdOpd.BxDEsts = 1 )
					Insert Into crSigEtPos (Cbars, CPros, Pesos, Qtds, Emps, Dopes, Numes, DataS, Empos, Grupos, Contas, ;
						DopeOs, NumeOs, Nops, ObsEtiqs, CodCors, CodTams, DtMovs, Peso2s, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves) ;
						Values (xPesa.Cbars, xPesa.CPros, Ps2Grv, QtdGrv, TmpNens.Emps, ;
						TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, TmpNens.DataS, xPesa.Emps, TmpNens.Grupods, ;
						TmpNens.Contads, xPesa.Dopes, xPesa.Numes, xPesa.Nops, xPesa.Obs, ;
						xPesa.Cors, xPesa.Tams, Datetime(), PesGrv - Ps2Grv, ;
						TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), fUniqueIds())
				Endif
			Endif

			If LocalPro.CEstoqs <> 2 And Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs, 1, 2) And (CrSigCdOpd.BxOEsts = 1)
				_Oper = Iif(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs = 1, 'E', 'S')

				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif

				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey
				pSeq  = fGerUniqueKey('HISTBAR')

				Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Empos, Qtds, ;
					Grupos, Estos, CodBarras, CodCors, CodTams, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, ;
					EmpGruEsts, DtAlts, OriDopNums, Seqs, Pesos, Obs ) ;
					Values (Usuar, Datetime(), xPesa.Emps, _Oper, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, ;
					TmpNens.DataS, xPesa.CPros, Thisform.pEmps, ;
					QtdGrv * Iif( LocalPro.cEstos == '2', Ps2Grv, 1 ), TmpNens.GrupoOs, ;
					TmpNens.Contaos, CodBarra, _pCor, _pTam, lcIds, ;
					xPesa.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), ;
					xPesa.Emps + TmpNens.GrupoOs + TmpNens.Contaos, Datetime(), ;
					ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), pSeq, Ps2Grv, TmpNens.Obss)

				=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )
			Endif

			If LocalPro.CEstoqs <> 2 And Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests, 1, 2) And (CrSigCdOpd.BxDEsts = 1)
				_Oper = Iif(CrSigCdOpd.EstDests = 1, 'E', 'S')

				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif
				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey
				pSeq  = fGerUniqueKey('HISTBAR')

				Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Empos, Qtds, ;
					Grupos, Estos, CodBarras, CodCors, CodTams, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, ;
					EmpGruEsts, DtAlts, OriDopNums, Seqs, Pesos, Obs ) ;
					Values (Usuar, Datetime(), xPesa.Emps, _Oper, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, ;
					TmpNens.DataS, xPesa.CPros, Thisform.pEmps, ;
					QtdGrv * Iif( LocalPro.cEstos == '2', Ps2Grv, 1 ), TmpNens.Grupods, ;
					TmpNens.Contads, CodBarra, _pCor, _pTam, lcIds, ;
					xPesa.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), ;
					xPesa.Emps + TmpNens.Grupods + TmpNens.Contads, Datetime(),;
					ThisForm.pEmps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 6), pSeq, Ps2Grv, TmpNens.Obss)

				=SqlCalcP2(xPesa.Emps, TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, xPesa.CPros, TmpNens.DataS, CodCor, CodTam, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(xPesa.Emps, xPesa.CPros, TmpNens.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )


				Thisform.BaixarCompos(xPesa.CPros)
			Endif
		Enddo

		_TotPeso = _TotPeso + xPesa.Peso
		
		*--Numero do OP/OS para gravar nas movimentaçőes de subnivel
		lnNop = xPesa.Nops
		
		lcEdn = xPesa.Emps + xPesa.Dopes + Str(xPesa.Numes, 6)
		lcsql = [Select Cpros, cItens, QtProds, QtBxProds, cidchaves From SigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEdn+[' ]+;
			[And Cpros = ']+xPesa.CPros+[']

		If Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalEestI') < 1
			=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - LocalEestI )')
			Return .F.
		Endif

		Select LocalEestI
		Go Top
		_Baixa = xPesa.Qtds
		Scan While (_Baixa > 0)
			_Chave = lcEdn + Str(LocalEestI.CItens, 4)
			_Pendente = (QtProds - QtBxProds)
			If (_Pendente) <> 0
				Select LocalEestI
				If (_Pendente > _Baixa)
					pQtd = QtBxProds + _Baixa
					_Baixa = 0
				Else
					pQtd = QtBxProds + _Pendente
					_Baixa = _Baixa - _Pendente
				Endif

				pDat = Datetime()

				lcQuery = [Update SigMvItn ] + ;
					[Set DtAlts = ?pDat, ] + ;
					[QtBxProds = ?pQtd ] + ;
					[Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEestI.cIdChaves + [']

				If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Update - SigMvItn 1)')
					Return .F.
				Endif

				lcQuery = [Select QtProds, QtBxProds, cIdChaves ] + ;
					[From SigMvIts ] + ;
					[Where EmpDopNums = '] + lcEdn + [' And ] + ;
					[CItens = ] + Str(LocalEestI.CItens, 4)

				If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalEstI2') < 1)
					=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalEstI2 - 2)')
					Return .F.
				Endif
				Select LocalEstI2
				Go Top
				Scan While (_Baixa > 0)
					_Pendente = (QtProds - QtBxProds)
					If (_Pendente <> 0)
						If (_Pendente > _Baixa)
							pQt2 = LocalEstI2.QtBxProds + _Baixa
							_Baixa = 0
						Else
							pQt2 = LocalEstI2.QtBxProds + _Pendente
							_Baixa = _Baixa - _Pendente
						Endif

						pDat = Datetime()

						lcQuery = [Update SigMvIts ] + ;
							[Set QtBxProds = ?pQt2 ] + ;
							[Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalEstI2.cIdChaves + [']

						If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
							=Messagebox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (mSv_Inserir - Update - SigMvIts)')
							Return .F.
						Endif
					Endif
				Endscan
			Endif
		Endscan
	Endscan

	If Not Empty(CrSigCdPam.TransfEncs) And Inlist(CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs,3,4)
		Set Step On 
		_Dope       = CrSigCdPam.TransfEncs
		lcsql = [Select * From SigCdOpe Where dopes = ']+_Dope+[']
		=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'CrSigCdOpe')

		_ChaveNens  = TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps,6)

		Go Top In crSigEtPos
		Go Top In crSigOpEtq

		If CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 3
			Select *, Space(10) As Grupods, Space(10) As Contads, Space(10) As GrupoOs, Space(10) As Contaos ;
				From crSigEtPos Into Cursor Localpeti Order By cIdChaves Readwrite
		Else
			Select *, Space(10) As Grupods, Space(10) As Contads, Space(10) As GrupoOs, Space(10) As Contaos ;
				From crSigOpEtq Into Cursor Localpeti Order By Cbars Readwrite
		Endif

		Select Localpeti
		Go Top
		Scan
			lcChv = Localpeti.Empos + Localpeti.DopeOs + Str(Localpeti.NumeOs, 6)

			lcsql = [Select GrupoOs, ContaOs, GrupoDs, ContaDs From SigMvCab ]+;
				[Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcChv+[']
			Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalEest')

			Replace Grupods With LocalEest.Grupods,;
				Contads With LocalEest.Contads,;
				GrupoOs With LocalEest.GrupoOs,;
				Contaos With LocalEest.Contaos In Localpeti
		Endscan

		*** Tiago - 09/09/11 - Cursor totalizando qtds e peso por OP, para ratear nos barras gerados da OP
		*!*			Select Count(1) as qtds , Sum(pesos + peso2s) as pesos, nOps from LocalpEti group by Nops into cursor crTotEti readwrite
		Select Sum(Qtds) As Qtds , Sum(Pesos + Peso2s) As Pesos, Nops From Localpeti Group By Nops Into Cursor crTotEti Readwrite

		Select Localpeti
		Index On Grupods + Contads + GrupoOs + Contaos + CPros Tag CPros

		_Chave = Space(40)
		_Nume  = 0
		lnItem = 0
		lnItem2 = 0

		Scan

			_GrupoOs = Localpeti.Grupods
			_ContaOs = Localpeti.Contads
			_GrupoDs = Localpeti.GrupoOs
			_ContaDs = Localpeti.Contaos
			_Empd    = ' '

			If _Chave <> _GrupoDs + _ContaDs + _GrupoOs + _ContaOs

				_Chave   = _GrupoDs + _ContaDs + _GrupoOs + _ContaOs
				_Nume    = fGerUniqueKey(Alltrim(_Dope)+TmpNens.Emps)

				Insert Into crSigMvCab (Emps, EmpDs, Dopes, Numes, MascNum, DataS, Datars, Usuars, GrupoOs, Contaos, ;
					Grupods, Contads, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts, EmpDnCrds, Utilizados ) ;
					Values (Localpeti.Emps, _Empd, _Dope, _Nume, Alltrim(fGerMascara(_Nume)), ;
					Datetime(), Datetime(), Usuar, _GrupoOs, _ContaOs, _GrupoDs, _ContaDs, ;
					Localpeti.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime(), _ChaveNens, 1)
				lnItem = 0
				lnItem2 = 0
			Endif

			lnItem = lnItem + 1
			Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'LocalPro', 'CPros', Localpeti.CPros, 'CUnis, DPros')

			Insert Into crSigMvItn (CItens, Emps, Dopes, Numes, CPros, Qtds, Pesos, CUnis, Dpros, ;
				Opers, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts, CodBarras) ;
				Values (lnItem, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, _Nume, Localpeti.CPros, Localpeti.Qtds, ;
				Localpeti.Pesos + Localpeti.Peso2s, LocalPro.CUnis, LocalPro.Dpros, ;
				'S', TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime(), Localpeti.Cbars)

			*** Tiago - 12/09/11 - Grava cor e tamanho
			If !Empty(Localpeti.CodCors) Or !Empty(Localpeti.CodTams)
				Insert Into crSigMvIts ( CItens, CPros, Emps, Dopes, Numes, Qtds, QtdEmbs, Pesos, CodCors, CodTams, CodEmbs, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts ) ;
					Values ( lnItem, Localpeti.CPros, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, _Nume, Localpeti.Qtds, Localpeti.Qtds, ;
					0 , Localpeti.CodCors, Localpeti.CodTams, '', TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime() )
			Endif

			If CrSigCdOpd.Etiqs = 4
				Select crSigOpEtq
				Go Top
				Locate For Cbars = Localpeti.Cbars
				If !Eof()
					Replace Grupos With _GrupoDs ,;
						Contas With _ContaDs In crSigOpEtq
				Endif
			Endif

			*** Tiago - 09/09/11 - Grava o material baixado de cada OP na tabela de composiçăo substituida, para depois ser usada na INVOICE
			Select crTotEti
			Go Top
			Locate For Nops = Localpeti.Nops
			If !Eof()
				_Nenv = crTotEti.Nops
				Select xPesa
				Go Top
				Locate For Cbars = Localpeti.Cbars
				_MatP = xPesa.MatPs && CrSigCdPam.Ouros
				Select xNensI
				Set Order To Nops &&Nenvs
				llTemOuro = .F.
				If Seek(_Nenv)
					Scan While Nops = _Nenv
						If CMats = _MatP
							llTemOuro = .T.
							Exit
						Endif
					Endscan
				Endif

				*** Tiago - 24/09/2013
				Select * From xPesa Where Nops = _Nenv Into Cursor crRatCompo

				Select xNensI
				lnQtds = 0
				lnPesos = 0
				lnSomaEtq = 0
				Scan For Nops = _Nenv &&Nenvs = _Nenv
					If Empty(xNensI.CMats) Or xNensI.Servicos
						Loop
					Endif
					lnItem2 = lnItem2 + 1

					lnQtRat = 0 &&crTotEti.Qtds
					*** Tiago - 23/09/2013 - Busca se o componente faz parte de alguma substituiçăo de componente para gravar no barra correspondente e năo rateando para todos os produtos iguais
					If xNensI.CMats <> _MatP
						lcsql = [Select a.Mats, a.Qtds, a.cats, a.grupos, a.ordems, a.cunis as unicompos, a.Pesos, a.units as pcompos, a.moevs as moeds ]+;
							[From SigSubMv a ]+;
							[Where a.empdopnums = '] + xPesa.Emps + xPesa.Dopes + Str(xPesa.Numes, 6) + [' and a.Cpros = ']+Localpeti.CPros+[' and a.citem2 = ] + Alltrim(Str(xPesa.CItens))
						=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
						Select LocalCompo
						llCompoSub = !Eof('LocalCompo')
						llItemSub = !Eof('LocalCompo')
						If !Eof('LocalCompo')
							Go Top
							Locate For Mats = xNensI.CMats
							llItemSub = !Eof('LocalCompo')
						Endif

						lcsql = [Select Mats, Qtds, Cats, Grupos, Ordems, UniCompos, Pesos, pCompos, Moeds  From SigPrCpo Where Cpros = ']+Localpeti.CPros+[' ] +;
							[ And Mats = '] + xNensI.CMats + [']
						Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
						llCompoOri = !Eof('LocalCompo')

						If (llCompoSub And !llItemSub)
							Loop
						Endif

						Select crRatCompo
						Scan
							lcsql = [Select a.Mats, a.Qtds, a.cats, a.grupos, a.ordems, a.cunis as unicompos, a.Pesos, a.units as pcompos, a.moevs as moeds ]+;
								[From SigSubMv a ]+;
								[Where a.empdopnums = '] + crRatCompo.Emps + crRatCompo.Dopes + Str(crRatCompo.Numes, 6) + [' and a.Cpros = ']+Localpeti.CPros+[' and a.citem2 = ] + Alltrim(Str(crRatCompo.CItens))
							*!*										[ And a.Mats = '] + xNensI.CMats + [']
							=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
							Select LocalCompo
							If !Eof('LocalCompo')
								Go Top
								Locate For Mats = xNensI.CMats
								If !Eof()
									lnQtRat = lnQtRat + crRatCompo.Qtds
								Endif
							Else
								*!*									If Reccount('LocalCompo') = 0
								*!*										lcsql = [Select Mats, Qtds, Cats, Grupos, Ordems, UniCompos, Pesos, pCompos, Moeds  From SigPrCpo Where Cpros = ']+LocalPEti.Cpros+[' ] +;
								*!*												[ And Mats = '] + xNensI.CMats + [']
								*!*										ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
								*!*										If !Eof('LocalCompo')
								If llCompoOri Or (!llCompoSub And !llItemSub And !llCompoOri)
									lnQtRat = lnQtRat + crRatCompo.Qtds
								Endif
								*!*										Endif
								*!*									Endif
							Endif
						Endscan
						If (!llCompoSub And !llCompoOri And lnQtRat <> crTotEti.Qtds)
							Loop
						Endif
					Endif
					*!*						If lnQtRat = 0
					*!*							lnQtRat = crTotEti.Qtds
					*!*						Endif
					Select xNensI
					***

					If llTemOuro And xNensI.CMats <> _MatP
						*!*							lnPesos = lnPesos  + Iif(crTotEti.Qtds > 1,(xNensi.Pesos / crTotEti.Qtds),xNensi.Pesos)
						lnPesos = lnPesos  + Iif(lnQtRat > 1,(xNensI.Pesos / lnQtRat ),xNensI.Pesos)

						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'CrTmpPro', 'CPros', xNensI.CMats, 'Cgrus')
						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'CrTmpGru', 'CGrus', CrTmpPro.Cgrus, 'CfgGerGprs')
						If Int(Val(Substr(CrTmpGru.CfgGerGprs, 14, 1))) = 1 && Tiago - 18/02/2014 - Incluído para checar se no grupo do componente está configurado para năo salvar no peso de pedras
							lnSomaEtq = lnSomaEtq + Iif(lnQtRat > 1,(xNensI.Pesos / lnQtRat ),xNensI.Pesos)
						Endif
					Endif

					*!*						Insert Into crSigSubMv (CItens, Emps, Dopes, Numes, CPros, Qtds, Pesos, Cunis, CuniPs, DPros, ;
					*!*												Opers, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts, Mats, Citem2, CodBarras) ;
					*!*										Values (lnItem2, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, _Nume, LocalPEti.CPros, Iif(crTotEti.Qtds > 1,(xNensi.Qtds / crTotEti.Qtds),xNensi.Qtds), ;
					*!*												Iif(crTotEti.Qtds > 1,(xNensi.Peso2s / crTotEti.Qtds), xNensi.Peso2s), xNensi.Cunis, xNensi.CuniPs, xNensi.cDescs, ;
					*!*												'S', TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime(), xNensi.cMats, lnItem, LocalpEti.Cbars)
					* LocalpEti.Cbars adicionado por Richard em 24/07/2012
					*!*						Insert Into crSigSubMv (CItens, Emps, Dopes, Numes, CPros, Qtds, Pesos, Cunis, CuniPs, DPros, ;
					*!*												Opers, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts, Mats, Citem2, CodBarras) ;
					*!*										Values (lnItem2, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, _Nume, LocalPEti.CPros, Iif(crTotEti.Qtds > 1,(xNensi.Qtds / crTotEti.Qtds) * LocalPEti.Qtds,xNensi.Qtds), ;
					*!*												Iif(crTotEti.Qtds > 1,(xNensi.Peso2s / crTotEti.Qtds) * LocalPEti.Qtds, xNensi.Peso2s), xNensi.Cunis, xNensi.CuniPs, xNensi.cDescs, ;
					*!*												'S', TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime(), xNensi.cMats, lnItem, LocalpEti.Cbars)

					Insert Into crSigSubMv (CItens, Emps, Dopes, Numes, CPros, Qtds, Pesos, CUnis, CUniPs, Dpros, ;
						Opers, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts, Mats, Citem2, CodBarras) ;
						Values (lnItem2, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, _Nume, Localpeti.CPros, Iif(lnQtRat > 1,(xNensI.Qtds / lnQtRat) * Localpeti.Qtds,xNensI.Qtds), ;
						Iif(lnQtRat > 1,(xNensI.Peso2s / lnQtRat) * Localpeti.Qtds, xNensI.Peso2s), xNensI.CUnis, xNensI.CUniPs, xNensI.CDescs, ;
						'S', TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime(), xNensI.CMats, lnItem, Localpeti.Cbars)
				Endscan
				*!*					replace qtds with (LocalPEti.Pesos + LocalPEti.Peso2s) - lnPesos, ;
				*!*							pesos with (LocalPEti.Pesos + LocalPEti.Peso2s) - lnPesos for EmpDopNums = TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6) And mats = _MatP and cItem2 = lnItem in crSigSubMv
				Replace Qtds With (Localpeti.Pesos + Localpeti.Peso2s) - (lnPesos * Localpeti.Qtds), ;
					Pesos With (Localpeti.Pesos + Localpeti.Peso2s) - (lnPesos * Localpeti.Qtds) For EmpDopNums = TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(_Nume, 6) And Mats = _MatP And Citem2 = lnItem In crSigSubMv
				*** Tiago - 25/04/2013 - Ícaro - Estava gravando LocalPEti.Pesos - lnPesos, mas quando está configurado para a etiqueta ficar separado o peso de metal e outros componentes, estava subtraindo peso a mais

				If CrSigCdOpd.PesMatPs And lnSomaEtq > 0 && Tiago - 18/02/2014 - Incluído para checar se no grupo do componente está configurado para năo salvar no peso de pedras
					Select crSigOpEtq
					Go Top
					Locate For Cbars = Localpeti.Cbars
					If !Eof()
						Replace Pesos With Pesos + (lnSomaEtq * Localpeti.Qtds), Peso2s With Peso2s - (lnSomaEtq * Localpeti.Qtds)
					Endif
				Endif
			Endif
			***

			=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro','CrTmpPro','Cpros',crSigMvItn.CPros, [Cgrus, cUnis])
			=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp','CrTmpGru','Cgrus',CrTmpPro.Cgrus, [cEstoqs, MoeCusts])
			=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni','CrTmpUni','Cunis',CrTmpPro.CUnis)

			If crSigCdOpe.estoqs # 1 Or CrTmpGru.CEstoqs = 2
				Loop
			Endif

			If Inlist( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs, 1, 2 ) Or ( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs = 4 And crSigMvItn.Opers = "S" )
				_Oper = Iif( crSigCdOpe.Opers = 3, crSigMvItn.Opers, Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs = 1, "E", "S" ) )
				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpe.EstDests,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif
				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey

				*5
				Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, ;
					units, Moedas, totas, Empos, Qtds, Grupos, Estos, ;
					cIdChaves, Pesos, EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, OriDopNums, Obs, CodBarras, CodCors, CodTams ) ;
					values (Usuar, Datetime(), TmpNens.Emps, _Oper, _Dope, crSigMvItn.Numes, ;
					TmpNens.DataS, crSigMvItn.CPros, crSigMvItn.units, CrTmpGru.MoeCusts, crSigMvItn.totas,	;
					TmpNens.Emps, crSigMvItn.Qtds, ;
					_GrupoOs, _ContaOs, lcIds, ;
					crSigMvItn.Pesos, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6),;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+_GrupoOs+_ContaOs,;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), TmpNens.Obss, ;
					Localpeti.Cbars, Localpeti.CodCors, Localpeti.CodTams )

				=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )

			Endif

			If Inlist( crSigCdOpe.EstDests, 1, 2 ) Or ( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 4 And crSigMvItn.Opers = "E" )
				_Oper = Iif( crSigCdOpe.Opers = 3, Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 4, crSigMvItn.Opers, ;
					Iif( crSigMvItn.Opers = 'E', 'S', 'E' ) ), ;
					Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 1, "E", "S" ) )

				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif

				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey

				*6

				Insert Into crSigMvHst ( Usuars, Datars, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Qtds, ;
					units, Moedas, totas, Empos, Emps, Grupos, Estos, ;
					Pesos, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, OriDopNums, Obs, CodBarras, CodCors, CodTams ) ;
					values (Usuar, Datetime(), _Oper, crSigMvCab.Dopes, crSigMvCab.Numes, crSigMvCab.DataS,;
					crSigMvItn.CPros, crSigMvItn.Qtds, ;
					crSigMvItn.units, CrTmpGru.MoeCusts, crSigMvItn.totas, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps, crSigMvCab.Emps, _GrupoDs, _ContaDs, ;
					crSigMvItn.Pesos, lcIds, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6),;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+_GrupoDs+_ContaDs,;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), TmpNens.Obss, ;
					Localpeti.Cbars, Localpeti.CodCors, Localpeti.CodTams )

				=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )
			Endif
		Endscan

		*-- Rafael - 06/12/2016 - Marca a Operaçăo Inicial com o Status de Finalizado Produçăo
		lcPStatus = []
		=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select Top 1 Cods from SigStats Order By Cods Desc],[CrTmpStats])
		
		Select CrTmpStats
		If Reccount([CrTmpStats])>0
			lcPStatus = CrTmpStats.Cods
			
			Select xNensi 
			Select Distinct Nops From xNensi where Not Empty(Nops) Into Cursor csTmpNops ReadWrite 
			
			Select csTmpNops
			Go Top
			Scan 
			
				lcQuery = [Select EmpDopNums From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(csTmpNops.Nops,10)
				=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrTmpOpPic')
				
				Select CrTmpOpPic
				lcEdnOp = CrTmpOpPic.EmpDopNums 
				
				lcQuery = [Select distinct c.empdopnums, d.nemps, right(a.codigos,6) as codigos ] + ;
						[from sigmvpec a ] + ;
						[join sigcdemp d on a.empsubns = d.cemps ] + ;
						[join sigmvcab c on a.empsubns = c.emps and right(a.codigos,6)=c.numes ] + ;
						[Join (select a.Dopes from sigcdope a ] + ;
							[join sigmvpec b on a.ndopes = left(b.Codigos,len(b.codigos)-6) where b.empdopnums = ']+lcEdnOp+[' ) b on c.dopes = b.dopes ] + ;
						[where a.empdopnums = ']+lcEdnOp+[' ]
				=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrTmpProdu')
				
				Select CrTmpProdu
				Select a.EmpDopNums from CrTmpProdu a ;
					Join xNensi b on a.Codigos = Right(Str(b.Nops,10),6) ;
					And Alltrim(Str(a.Nemps,3)) = Left(Str(b.Nops,10),Len('b.Nops')-7) ;
					Into Cursor crAtStatus ReadWrite 
					
				Select crAtStatus
				Go Top
				Scan
					lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set PStatus = ']+lcPStatus+[' Where EmpDopNums = ']+crAtStatus.EmpDopNums+[' ]
					=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate)
					Select crAtStatus
				EndScan  
				
				*--Atualiza a movimentaçăo com o Numero da Op/Os da Movimentaçăo anterior
				lcUpdate = [Update SigMvCab Set Nops = ]+Str(lnNop,10)+[ Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEdnOp+[' ]
				=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpdate)
				
				Select csTmpNops
			Endscan 
		EndIf 
		
		*--Movimentaçăo financeira
		_Dope       = CrSigCdPam.TransfEncs
		lcsql = [Select * From sigopfin Where dopes = ']+_Dope+[' and codigos <> space(10)]
		=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'CrSigOpFin')
		
		=fSigOpFin_Lancs(ThisForm.poDataMgr, crSigMvCab.Dopes, [crSigMvCab], [crSigMvItn], [], [], [], .T.)
		* Fim: - Gravar Lançamentos da Configuraçăo Financeira da Movimentaçăo
		
		* Richard em 31/07/2012 - Lançamento Financeiro Se o Movimento de Finalizaçăo Tiver essa configuraçăo - Vianna
		If (crSigCdOpe.EdComis = 5) And Not Empty(crSigCdOpe.Grupos) And Not Empty(crSigCdOpe.Contas)
			&& Tipo 5 = Lança CC dos Produtos Colocado Para Possibilitar Configuraçăo Sem Criar Novos Parâmetros
			Select crSigMvCab
			Scan
				&& Richard em 25/07/2012 para Vianna. O EdComis foi colocado pra evitar erros em outros clientes com uma
				&& eventual configuraçăo incorreta uma vez que o certo seria o Precops estar como 4 com essa configuraçăo
				&& Nota: hoje está pegando o custo do cadastro dos produtos, porém o ideal é usar o custo médio (Tipo 8).
				If fCalcCusto(Thisform.poDataMgr, crSigMvCab.Dopes, CrSigCdPam.MoedaPs, crSigMvCab.DataS, [crSigMvItn], ;
						[crSigSubMv], crSigMvCab.EmpDopNums)
					Select Moedas, Sum(totas) As totas From crSigMvItn Where EmpDopNums = crSigMvCab.EmpDopNums Group By 1 Into Cursor crSoma
					Go Top In crSoma
					Replace Valos With crSoma.totas In crSigMvCab
				Endif

				Select crSigMvCcr
				_Noper = fGerUniqueKey([SigMvCcr])
				_VOper = crSigMvCab.Emps + _TipoE + Alltrim(Str(_Noper, 9))
				_Valor = crSigMvCab.Valos
				_Hist  = Iif(Empty(crSigCdOpe.Hists), Alltrim(_Dope) + [ ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nume, 6)), Alltrim(crSigCdOpe.Hists))
				_Hist2 = Alltrim(Alltrim(crSigCdOpe.Hist2s) + [ ] + crSigMvCab.EmpDnCrds)
				xOper  = Iif(crSigCdOpe.COpers=2, [C], [D])
				xSope  = Iif(crSigCdOpe.COpers=2, [D], [C])
				lcMoe  = Iif(Empty(crSigCdOpe.Cmoes), CrSigCdPam.MoedaPs, crSigCdOpe.Cmoes)

				For lnCont = 1 To 2
					_numcs = fGerUniqueKey(lcDopcs)
					lcodc  = Iif(lnCont=1,xOper,xSope)
					lcSdc  = Iif(lnCont=1,xSope,xOper)
					lcIds  = Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS) + Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS)), [@L 999999]) + Thisform.sigkey
					lcGOri = Iif(lnCont=1, crSigCdOpe.Grupos,  crSigMvCab.Grupods)
					lcCOri = Iif(lnCont=1, crSigCdOpe.Contas,  crSigMvCab.Contads)
					lcGDes = Iif(lnCont=1, crSigMvCab.Grupods, crSigCdOpe.Grupos)
					lcCDes = Iif(lnCont=1, crSigMvCab.Contads, crSigCdOpe.Contas)

					Insert Into crSigMvCcr (NOpers, VOpers, Emps, DataS, UsuAlts, DatAlts, Vencs, Hists, Opers, SOpers, Moedas, ;
						Cotacaos, Valors, Autos, Grupos, Contas, SGrupos, SContas, SMoedas, SCotacaos, SValors, ;
						Dopes, Numes, ValPags, ValLiqs, DtEmis, Hist2s, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, Tipos) ;
						Values (_Noper, _VOper, crSigMvCab.Emps, crSigMvCab.DataS, Usuar, Datetime(), crSigMvCab.DataS, ;
						_Hist, lcodc, lcSdc, lcMoe, 1, _Valor, .T., lcGOri, lcCOri, lcGDes, lcCDes, lcMoe, ;
						1, _Valor, crSigMvCab.Dopes, crSigMvCab.Numes, _Valor, _Valor, crSigMvCab.DtEmis, _Hist2, ;
						lcIds, crSigMvCab.Emps + crSigMvCab.Dopes + Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), [P])

					Replace GruConMoes With crSigMvCcr.Grupos + crSigMvCcr.Contas + crSigMvCcr.Moedas, ;
						EmpDopNcs  With crSigMvCcr.Emps + crSigMvCcr.dopcs + Str(crSigMvCcr.numcs,6), ;
						Pagos      With Iif(crSigMvCcr.Valors = crSigMvCcr.ValPags, [0], [1]), ;
						DopoTps    With crSigMvCcr.dopcs + crSigMvCcr.Opers + crSigMvCcr.Tipos + crSigMvCcr.Pagos In crSigMvCcr

					=fRecalculaS( crSigMvCcr.Grupos, crSigMvCcr.Contas, crSigMvCcr.DataS, crSigMvCcr.Moedas, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				Next

				=fCalcCCPro(Thisform.poDataMgr, [crSigMvItn],.F.,CrSigCdOpd.GruCcus,CrSigCdOpd.ContaCcus)

				Select TmpComiss
				Go Top In TmpComiss
				If Not Eof([TmpComiss])
					Scan
						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigOpOpe], [crDope], [Dopes], crSigCdOpe.dopcs, [RealPrevs,Opers])
						GrupoTran = Iif(crDOpe.Opers = [CR], CrSigCdPam.GrupoPags, CrSigCdPam.GrupoRecs)
						ContaTran = Iif(crDOpe.Opers = [CR], CrSigCdPam.ContaPags, CrSigCdPam.ContaRecs)

						_Noper = fGerUniqueKey([SigMvCcr])
						_VOper = crSigMvCab.Emps + _TipoE + Alltrim(Str(_Noper, 9))
						_Valor = TmpComiss.Comissaos

						For lnCont = 1 To 2
							_numcs = fGerUniqueKey(lcDopcs)
							lcodc  = Iif(lnCont=1,xOper,xSope)
							lcSdc  = Iif(lnCont=1,xSope,xOper)
							lcIds  = Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS) + Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS)), [@L 999999]) + Thisform.sigkey
							lcGOri = Iif(lnCont=1,GrupoTran,TmpComiss.Grupos)
							lcCOri = Iif(lnCont=1,ContaTran,TmpComiss.Contas)
							lcGDes = Iif(lnCont=1,TmpComiss.Grupos,GrupoTran)
							lcCDes = Iif(lnCont=1,TmpComiss.Contas,ContaTran)
							_Hist2 = [CUSTOS DE PRODUTOS]
							lcIds  = Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS) + Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(crSigMvCab.DataS)), [@L 999999]) + Thisform.sigkey

							Insert Into crSigMvCcr (NOpers, VOpers, Emps, DataS, UsuAlts, DatAlts, Vencs, Hists, Opers, SOpers, Moedas, ;
								Cotacaos, Valors, Autos, Grupos, Contas, SGrupos, SContas, SMoedas, SCotacaos, SValors, ;
								Dopes, Numes, ValPags, ValLiqs, DtEmis, Hist2s, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, Tipos) ;
								Values (_Noper, _VOper, crSigMvCab.Emps, crSigMvCab.DataS, Usuar, Datetime(), crSigMvCab.DataS, ;
								_Hist, lcodc, lcSdc, lcMoe, 1, _Valor, .T., lcGOri, lcCOri, lcGDes, lcCDes, ;
								lcMoe, 1, _Valor, crSigMvCab.Dopes, crSigMvCab.Numes, _Valor, _Valor, crSigMvCab.DtEmis, ;
								_Hist2, lcIds, crSigMvCab.Emps + crSigMvCab.Dopes + Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), [P])

							Replace GruConMoes With crSigMvCcr.Grupos + crSigMvCcr.Contas + crSigMvCcr.Moedas, ;
								EmpDopNcs  With crSigMvCcr.Emps + crSigMvCcr.dopcs + Str(crSigMvCcr.numcs,6), ;
								Pagos      With Iif(crSigMvCcr.Valors = crSigMvCcr.ValPags, [0], [1]), ;
								DopoTps    With crSigMvCcr.dopcs + crSigMvCcr.Opers + crSigMvCcr.Tipos + crSigMvCcr.Pagos In crSigMvCcr

							=fRecalculaS( crSigMvCcr.Grupos, crSigMvCcr.Contas, crSigMvCcr.DataS, crSigMvCcr.Moedas, Thisform.poDataMgr)
						Next
					Endscan
				Endif
			Endscan
		Endif
	Endif
Endif

If Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs)
	Select * From crSigMvItn Into Cursor xEesti Where 0=1 Readwrite
	Go Top In CrSigCdNei

	Select Nenvs, Nops, CMats, Qtds, Pesos, Peso2s,cIdChaves  From CrSigCdNei ;
		Into Cursor TmpNensi Where Nops <> 0 Order By Nops,CMats Readwrite

	Select crSigMvCab
	Index On Dopes+GrupoOs+Contaos+Grupods+Contads Tag Grupos

	_citem = 1

	Select TmpNensi
	Scan
		lnEnv = Iif(Empty(Nenvs),Nops,Nenvs)
		lcPro = TmpNensi.CMats
		lcsql = [Select Cpros From SigOpPic where Nops = ]+Str(TmpNensi.Nops)
		Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')

		lnOp = Val(Left(Str(TmpNensi.Nops,10),6))
		lcsql = [Select a.emps,a.Numes,a.GrupoOs,a.ContaOs,a.GrupoDs,a.ContaDs,]+;
			[b.Cpros,b.Qtds,b.QtBaixas,b.CidChaves,b.citens ]+;
			[from SigMvCab a, SigMvItn b Where a.Nops = ]+Str(lnOp)+[ ]+;
			[And a.Dopes = ']+CrSigCdPam.DopEmphs+[' And a.empDopNums = b.EmpDopNums  And ]+;
			[b.Cpros = ']+TmpNensi.CMats+[' And b.cpro2s = ']+LocalOpi.CPros+[']
		lnErro = Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'CrTmpEesti')
		If lnErro < 1
			Messagebox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo')
			Wait Clear
			Return .F.
		Endif

		_QtBaixar = TmpNensi.Qtds

		Select CrTmpEesti
		Scan
			If _QtBaixar <= 0
				Exit
			Endif

			If CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas + _QtBaixar <= CrTmpEesti.Qtds
				Replace CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas With CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas + _QtBaixar
				_QtBaixado = _QtBaixar
				_QtBaixar = 0
			Else
				_QtBaixar = _QtBaixar - ( Qtds - QtBaixas )
				_QtBaixado = CrTmpEesti.Qtds - CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas
				Replace QtBaixas With Qtds In CrTmpEesti
			Endif
			llBaixa = Iif(CrTmpEesti.Qtds = CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas,.T.,.F.)
			lcUpDate = [UpDate SigMvItn Set QtBaixas = ]+Str(CrTmpEesti.QtBaixas,12,3)+[, ChkSubn = ?llBaixa ]+;
				[Where CidChaves = ']+CrTmpEesti.cIdChaves+[']

			lnErro = Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcUpDate,'')
			If lnErro < 1
				Messagebox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo')
				Wait Clear
				Return .F.
			Endif

			lcsql = [Select cpros,dpros,cunis from SigCdPro where cpros = ']+lcPro+[']
			If Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalPro') < 1
				Messagebox('Favor reinicializar o processo.',16,'Falha na Conexăo')
				Wait Clear
				Return .F.
			Endif

			Select crSigMvCab
			If Not Seek(CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs+CrTmpEesti.GrupoOs+CrTmpEesti.Contaos+CrTmpEesti.Grupods+CrTmpEesti.Contads)
				lnNume = fGerUniqueKey(Alltrim(CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs)+Thisform.pEmps)
				lcMasc = Alltrim( fGerMascara( lnNume ) )

				Insert Into crSigMvCab (MascNum,DataS,Datars,Dopes,Emps,Numes,GrupoOs,Contaos,Grupods,Contads,;
					cIdChaves,EmpDopNums,EmpDnCrds) Values ;
					(lcMasc,TmpNens.DataS,Datetime(),CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs,TmpNens.Emps,;
					lnNume,CrTmpEesti.GrupoOs,CrTmpEesti.Contaos,CrTmpEesti.Grupods,CrTmpEesti.Contads,;
					fUniqueIds(),TmpNens.Emps+CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs+Str(lnNume,6),;
					TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps,6))
			Endif

			Select crSigMvItn
			Insert Into crSigMvItn (CItens,CPros,CUnis,Dopes,Dpros,Emps,Numes,Opers,Qtds,;
				cIdChaves,EmpDopNums,cpro2s,AQtds) Values ;
				(_citem,lcPro,LocalPro.CUnis,CrSigCdOpd.DopEmphs,LocalPro.Dpros,;
				crSigMvCab.Emps,crSigMvCab.Numes,'S',_QtBaixado,fUniqueIds(),;
				crSigMvCab.EmpDopNums,LocalOpi.CPros,TmpNensi.Qtds)

			_citem = _citem + 1

			Insert Into crSigBxEst ( Emps, Dopes, Numes, CItens, CPros, Qtdes, ;
				Datas, Empbs, Dopebs, Numebs, EmpDopNums, EmpdopNumb, cIdChaves ) ;
				Values ( crSigMvCab.Emps, crSigMvCab.Dopes, crSigMvCab.Numes, ;
				CrTmpEesti.CItens, crSigMvItn.CPros, _QtBaixado,;
				crSigMvCab.DataS, CrTmpEesti.Emps, CrSigCdPam.DopEmphs , ;
				CrTmpEesti.Numes, crSigMvCab.EmpDopNums,;
				CrTmpEesti.Emps + CrSigCdPam.DopEmphs + Str(CrTmpEesti.Numes,6), fUniqueIds() )
		Endscan

	Endscan

Endif

Select xMFas
Set Order To Nops

Select xNensiN  &&năo conformidades
Set Order To
Scan
	If Empty(Cods)
		Loop
	Endif
	=Seek(xNensiN.Nops,'xMfas')
	Insert Into crSigOpInc (Nops, Cods, CPros, Nenvs, Qtds, EmpDNPs, DataS, cIdChaves, Grupos, Contas, Descs, Conta2s ) Values ;
		(xNensiN.Nops, xNensiN.Cods, xMFas.codpds, xMFas.Nenvs, xNensiN.Qtds, ;
		TmpNens.Emps+TmpNens.Dopps+Str(TmpNens.Numps,10), TmpNens.DataS, ;
		fUniqueIds(), TmpNens.Grupods, TmpNens.Contads, xNensiN.Descs, xNensiN.Conta2s )

	Replace TmpNens.nConforms With .T. In TmpNens

Endscan

Select xNensiNC  &&Autorizaçőes
Set Order To
Scan
	If Empty(Cods)
		Loop
	Endif
	Insert Into crSigOpInc (Cods, Nenvs, Qtds, AQtds, EmpDNPs, DataS, cIdChaves, Grupos, Contas, Descs, Usuars ) Values ;
		(xNensiNC.Cods, xNensiNC.Nenvs, xNensiNC.Qtds, xNensiNC.AQtds, ;
		TmpNens.Emps+TmpNens.Dopps+Str(TmpNens.Numps,10), TmpNens.DataS, ;
		fUniqueIds(), TmpNens.GrupoOs, TmpNens.Contaos, xNensiNC.Descs, xNensiNC.Usuars )
Endscan

Select TmpNens
Go Top
Replace TotPesos With _TotPeso In TmpNens

*** Tiago - Gera movimentaçăo automática de transformaçăo dos itens semiacabados
If !Empty(CrSigCdOpd.DopSemis)
	Select * From xNensI Where CarCompos And Visivel Order By Nenvs, Amarracao Into Cursor crTmpSacb Readwrite
	If !Eof()
		_Dope = CrSigCdOpd.DopSemis
		lcsql = [Select * From SigCdOpe Where Dopes = '] + _Dope + [']
		=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'crSigCdOpe')

		Select crSigMvCab
		lnNume = fGerUniqueKey(Alltrim(_Dope)+Thisform.pEmps)
		lcMasc = Alltrim( fGerMascara( lnNume ) )

		Insert Into crSigMvCab (MascNum,DataS,Datars,Dopes,Emps,Numes,GrupoOs,Contaos,Grupods,Contads,cIdChaves,EmpDopNums,EmpDnCrds,Usuars) Values ;
			(lcMasc,TmpNens.DataS,Datetime(),_Dope,TmpNens.Emps, lnNume,TmpNens.GrupoOs,TmpNens.Contaos,TmpNens.GrupoOs,TmpNens.Contaos,;
			fUniqueIds(),TmpNens.Emps+_Dope+Str(lnNume,6),TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps,6), Usuar)

		lnItem = 0
		Select crTmpSacb
		Scan
			*!*				=ThisForm.podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdPro','CrTmpPro','Cpros',CrSigMvItn.cpros, [Cgrus, cUnis])
			=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp','CrTmpGru','Cgrus',crTmpSacb.Cgrus, [cEstoqs, MoeCusts, SemiAcabs])
			*!*				=ThisForm.podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdUni','CrTmpUni','Cunis',CrTmpPro.cunis)
			lcOper = Iif(CrTmpGru.Semiacabs = 1,'S','E')

			lnItem = lnItem + 1
			Insert Into crSigMvItn (CItens, Emps, Dopes, Numes, CPros, Qtds, CUnis, Pesos, CUniPs, Dpros, ;
				Opers, EmpDopNums, cIdChaves, DtAlts) ;
				Values (lnItem, TmpNens.Emps, _Dope, lnNume, crTmpSacb.CMats, crTmpSacb.Qtds, ;
				crTmpSacb.CUnis, crTmpSacb.Peso2s, crTmpSacb.CUniPs, crTmpSacb.Descs, ;
				lcOper, TmpNens.Emps + _Dope + Str(lnNume, 6), fUniqueIds(), Datetime())

			If crSigCdOpe.estoqs # 1 Or CrTmpGru.CEstoqs = 2
				Loop
			Endif

			If Inlist( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs, 1, 2 ) Or ( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs = 4 And crSigMvItn.Opers = "S" )
				_Oper = Iif( crSigCdOpe.Opers = 3, crSigMvItn.Opers, Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstOrigs = 1, "E", "S" ) )
				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpe.EstDests,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif
				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey

				Insert Into crSigMvHst (Usuars, Datars, Emps, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, units, Moedas, ;
					totas, Empos, Qtds, Grupos, Estos, cIdChaves, Pesos, ;
					EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, OriDopNums, Obs ) ;
					values (Usuar, Datetime(), TmpNens.Emps, _Oper, _Dope, crSigMvItn.Numes, TmpNens.DataS, crSigMvItn.CPros, crSigMvItn.units, ;
					CrTmpGru.MoeCusts, crSigMvItn.totas, TmpNens.Emps, crSigMvItn.Qtds, TmpNens.GrupoOs,TmpNens.Contaos, lcIds, crSigMvItn.Pesos, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), crSigMvCab.Emps+TmpNens.GrupoOs+TmpNens.Contaos,;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), TmpNens.Obss)

				=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr)
			Endif

			If Inlist( crSigCdOpe.EstDests, 1, 2 ) Or ( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 4 And crSigMvItn.Opers = "E" )
				_Oper = Iif( crSigCdOpe.Opers = 3, Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 4, crSigMvItn.Opers, ;
					Iif( crSigMvItn.Opers = 'E', 'S', 'E' ) ), ;
					Iif( crSigCdOpe.EstDests = 1, "E", "S" ) )

				xOper = _Oper
				*** Tiago - 23/10/2015 - Definido com o Richard que vamos gravar no cidchaves a mesma letra da movimentaçăo para padronizar, assim a ordem do histórico fica correta
				*!*					If InList(CrSigCdOpd.EstOrigs,1,2)
				*!*						xOper = Iif(_Oper=[E],[H],[K])
				*!*					Endif

				lcIds = Dtos(TmpNens.DataS) +xOper+ Transform(fGerUniqueKey(Dtos(TmpNens.DataS)), '@L 999999')+Thisform.sigkey

				Insert Into crSigMvHst ( Usuars, Datars, Opers, Dopes, Numes, DataS, CPros, Qtds, units, Moedas, ;
					totas, Empos, Emps, Grupos, Estos, ;
					Pesos, cIdChaves, EmpDopNums, EmpGruEsts, OriDopNums, Obs ) ;
					values (Usuar, Datetime(), _Oper, crSigMvCab.Dopes, crSigMvCab.Numes, crSigMvCab.DataS,	crSigMvItn.CPros, crSigMvItn.Qtds, ;
					crSigMvItn.units, CrTmpGru.MoeCusts, crSigMvItn.totas, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps, crSigMvCab.Emps, TmpNens.GrupoOs, TmpNens.Contaos, ;
					crSigMvItn.Pesos, lcIds, ;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6),;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+TmpNens.GrupoOs+TmpNens.Contaos,;
					crSigMvCab.Emps+crSigMvCab.Dopes+Str(crSigMvCab.Numes,6), TmpNens.Obss)

				=SqlCalcP2(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.Grupos, crSigMvHst.Estos, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, crSigMvHst.CodCors, crSigMvHst.CodTams, Thisform.poDataMgr)
				=fRecalculaC(crSigMvHst.Emps, crSigMvHst.CPros, crSigMvHst.DataS, Thisform.poDataMgr )
			Endif
		Endscan
	Endif
Endif

Return .T.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_procurar
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_procurar
If Used('TmpProcurar')
	USE in TmpProcurar
Endif
ThisForm.LocRegister = CrSigCdNec.Numps
Do Case
	Case !Empty( TmpNens.Numps )
		lcEdn = Thisform.pEmps + ThisForm._dopp  + Str( TmpNens.Numps, 10 )
		lcSql = [Select * from SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcEdn+[']
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpProcurar')
		ThisForm.LocRegister = TmpNens.Numps
		Select TmpProcurar
		Scan
			Scatter Memvar Memo
			If Not Seek(TmpProcurar.Numps,'CrProcurar','numps')
				Insert into crProcurar From memvar
			EndIf
		endscan

	Case !Empty( TmpNens.Docus )
		lcDocu = Padl(Alltrim(TmpNens.Docus),10)
		lcSql = [Select * from SigCdNec Where Docus = ']+lcDocu+[']
		=ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpProcurar')
		ThisForm.LocRegister = TmpProcurar.Numps
		Select TmpProcurar
		Scan
			Scatter Memvar Memo
			If Not Seek(TmpProcurar.Numps,'CrProcurar','numps')
				Insert into crProcurar From memvar
			EndIf
		endscan
EndCase

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE Release
ThisForm.Podatamgr.Release
ThisForm.Podatamgr4.Release
DoDefault()
ENDPROC
