================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Lista.cmdfechalote
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 22
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local llOk

llOk = .t.
lcSql = [Select * From SigPdNlt Where nLotes = ]+Str(crSigCdNec.nLotes)
If Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'LocalNlt') < 1
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo - SigPdNlt ')
	llOk = .f.
Else
	Select LocalNlt
	Go Top
	If ChkSubn = 0
		MessageBox('Operaçăo Sem Fechamento de Lote!',0+16,'Controle de lote')
		llOk = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf

If llOk And MessageBox('Confirma cancelamento do Fechamento de Lote?',4+32+256,'Controle de lote') = 6
	lcSql = [Update SigPdNlt Set chksubn =  0 Where nLotes = ]+Str(crSigCdNec.nLotes)
	If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'') < 1
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.rollback()
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo - Update SigPdNlt ')
	Else
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.Commit()
	EndIf
EndIf
Thisform.Pagina.Lista.Grade.SetFocus

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.cntDados.Get_Lote
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 25
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If !Empty(This.Value) && Tiago - 29/06/2015 - Real Gold - Alterei para năo buscar os lotes abertos quando năo informar nada
	If Seek(TmpNens.GrupoOs,'TmpGccr','balcodigo') and InList(TmpGccr.CtrLotes,1,3)
		lcsql = [Select nlotes, Datas From SigPdNlt Where EmpGruEsts = ']+TmpNens.Emps+TmpNens.GrupoOs+TmpNens.ContaOs+[' ]+;
				[And Chksubn = 0 ]
		Thisform.Podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpNlt')
		Select TmpNlt
		Index on nLotes tag nLotes
		If Not Seek(This.Value)
			loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'TmpNlt', 'nLotes', This.Value, 'Cadastro de Lotes ')
			loBrowse.AddColuna('nLotes', '9999999999', 'Código')
			loBrowse.AddColuna('Datas',  '99/99/9999', 'Data')
			loBrowse.Show()
			If Lastkey() = 27
				This.Value = 0
			Else 	
				This.Value = TmpNlt.nLotes
			Endif
		Endif
	Else
		If Seek(TmpNens.GrupoDs,'TmpGccr','balcodigo') and InList(TmpGccr.CtrLotes,1,3)
			lcsql = [Select nlotes, Datas From SigPdNlt Where EmpGruEsts = ']+TmpNens.Emps+TmpNens.GrupoDs+TmpNens.ContaDs+[' ]+;
					[And Chksubn = 0 ]
			Thisform.Podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpNlt')
			Select TmpNlt
			Index on nLotes tag nLotes
			If Not Seek(This.Value)
				loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'TmpNlt', 'nLotes', This.Value, 'Cadastro de Lotes ')
				loBrowse.AddColuna('nLotes', '9999999999', 'Código')
				loBrowse.AddColuna('Datas',  '99/99/9999', 'Data')
				loBrowse.Show()
				If Lastkey() = 27
					This.Value = 0
				Else 				
					This.Value = TmpNlt.nLotes
				Endif
			Endif
		Else
			This.Value = 0
		EndIf
	EndIf
Endif
This.Refresh()
*!*	Return .t.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return (Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And CrSigCdOpd.CtrLotes = 1)

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.cntDados.Dt_data
* Classe: fweditdata (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 26
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
If ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'INSERIR' And (crSigCdOpd.Numeras = 1) and (Reccount('tmpoperacao') = 1 and Empty(TmpOperacao.Codigos))
	thisform.pagina.dADOS.gradeOperaçăo.column1.SetFocus()
Endif
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If (fVerificaBloqueio(This.Value, ThisForm.Podatamgr) <> 0)
	=Messagebox('Periodo Bloqueado!!!', 0+48, '')
	Return 0
EndIf

If (fBloqueioPorPeriodo(This.Value, ThisForm.Podatamgr) <> 0)
	=Messagebox('Periodo Bloqueado!!!', 0+48, '')
	Return 0
EndIf
If (crSigCdOpd.Origems = 1)
	lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Datas ] + ;
			    [From SigCdFcx ] + ;
			   [Where Emps = '] + ThisForm.pEmps + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Grupos = '] + TmpNens.GrupoOs + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Contas = '] + TmpNens.ContaOs + [' ] + ;
			   [Order By Codigos Desc]			    

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalFecha') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalFecha)')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	Select LocalFecha
	Go Top
	If Reccount() > 0 And Dtos(TmpNens.Datas) < dtos(Ttod(LocalFecha.Datas)+CrSigCdPac.ndFechas)
		Use In LocalFecha
		=Messagebox('Período Bloqueado Para a Conta de Origem!!!', 32, '')
		This.Value = This.Tag
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Use In LocalFecha
EndIf

If (crSigCdOpd.Destinos = 1)
	lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Datas ] + ;
			    [From SigCdFcx ] + ;
			   [Where Emps = '] + ThisForm.pEmps + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Grupos = '] + TmpNens.GrupoDs + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Contas = '] + TmpNens.ContaDs + [' ] + ;
			   [Order By Codigos Desc]			    

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalFecha') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalFecha)')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	Select LocalFecha
	Go Top
	If RECCOUNT() > 0 AND (dtos(TmpNens.Datas) < dtos(Ttod(LocalFecha.Datas)+CrSigCdPac.ndFechas) )
		Use In LocalFecha
		=Messagebox('Período Bloqueado Para a Conta de Origem!!!', 32, '')
		This.Value = This.Tag
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Use In LocalFecha
EndIf
pdData = TTOD(ThisForm.PodataMgr.GetDatetime())
IF (TTOD(This.Value) < pdData And INLIST(Thisform.pcescolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR') )
	If Messagebox('Lançamento com Data Retroativa!!! Continua?',4+16+256,'') = 7
		Return 0
	Endif
Endif

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
If Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') 
	Select TmpOperacao
	Count to _LnCont For Codigos > 0
	If _lnCont > 0
		MessageBox('A Data só pode ser alterada antes de Informar Envelopes/Ops',0+16,'')
		Return .f.
	Else
		Return .t.
	Endif
Else
	Return .f.
Endif
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.cntDados.getTotPeso
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 27
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Select xNensi
Set Order To NopMatCat
lccMats = Iif(Empty(crSigCdOpd.MatPads), crSigCdPam.Ouros, crSigCdOpd.MatPads)
If Not Seek(Str(0, 10) + lccMats)
	Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Visivel, Rateio, FlagIncs, TpOps, NChkSep) ;
				Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, .t., 5, .t., CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos, .t.)
EndIf

lnPesos = This.Value
lnQtds  = This.Value

=Thisform.podatamgr.SqlExecute([Select CPros, DPros, CUnis, cUniPs, Cgrus From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+lccMats+[' ],[crTmpPro])

Select xNensi
Replace Cmats  With crTmpPro.CPros, ;
			CDescs With crTmpPro.DPros, ;
			CUnis  With crTmpPro.CUnis, ;
			cUniPs With crTmpPro.cUniPs, ;
			Cgrus  With crTmpPro.Cgrus ,;
			Qtds   With lnQtds ,;
			Pesos  With lnPesoS In xNensi

* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return (Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR'))
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_grupo
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 40
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
This.Parent.Get_conta.Setfocus
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid

If Not Empty(This.Value)

	If Not Empty(This.Value) And Not Seek(This.Value, 'TmpGccr', 'BalCodigo')
		loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'TmpGccr', 'BalCodigo', This.Value, 'Cadastro de Grupos')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Codigos', '', 'Código',    .t., 'BalCodigo')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Descrs',  '', 'Descriçăo', .t., 'BalDescrs')
		loBrowse.Show
		This.Value = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpGccr.Codigos)
	EndIf

	If Not fAcessoContab(Usuar, 'C', This.Value, '', '', This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
		=Messagebox('Acesso Negado!!!', 48, '')
		This.Value = ''
	EndIf

	If Not fRestritos(This.Parent.Parent.Origem.Get_grupo.Value, This.Value, ThisForm.poDataMgr)
		=Messagebox('Movimentaçăo Năo Permitida!!! Setor Com Restriçăo!!!', 48, '')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	If (crSigCdOpd.Grodns = 2) And (This.Value <> crSigCdPam.GrTrans) And Not Empty(crSigCdPam.GrTrans)
		=Messagebox('Grupo Transitório Obrigatório no Destino!!!', 48, '')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	If (crSigCdOpd.Grodns = 1) And (This.Value = crSigCdPam.GrTrans) And Not Empty(crSigCdPam.GrTrans)
		=Messagebox('Permitido Grupo Transitório Somente na Origem!!!', 48, '')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	
	If Not Empty(This.Parent.Get_conta.Value)
		lcSql = [Select Fases From SigClStp Where Iclis = ']+This.Parent.Get_conta.Value+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalSetP') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalSetP)')
			Return 0
		EndIf
		If Reccount('LocalSetP') > 0
			Select LocalSetP
			Locate For Fases = This.Value
			If Eof()
				MessageBox('Setor Năo definido para esta Conta!!!',0+16,' ')
				Return .f.
			EndIf
		Endif
	Endif
Endif
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops # 1
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_conta
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 41
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not Empty(This.Value)
	If !Empty(CrSigCdOpd.MascDs)
		This.Value = SUBSTR(This.Value,1,LEN(ALLTRIM(CrSigCdOpd.Mascds)))
		Clear Typeahead
		This.Refresh
	EndIf
	If Not Seek(This.Value, 'TmpCli', 'BalCodigo')
		loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'TmpCli', 'BalCodigo', This.Value, 'Cadastro de Contas')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('IClis',  '', 'Código',    .t., 'BalCodigo')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('RClis',  '', 'Descriçăo', .t., 'BalNome')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Grupos', '', 'Grupo',     .t., 'BalGrupo' )
		loBrowse.gridProc.SetAll('DynamicForeColor', [Iif(TmpCli.Inativas == 1, Rgb(255, 0, 0), Rgb(0,0,0))], 'Column')
		loBrowse.Show
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.IClis)
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.RClis)
	Else
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = TmpCli.RClis
	EndIf
	
	lcSql = [Select Fases From SigClStp Where Iclis = ']+TmpCli.Iclis+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalSetP') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalSetP)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	If Reccount('LocalSetP') > 0
		Select LocalSetP
		Locate For Fases = This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value
		If Eof()
			MessageBox('Setor Năo definido para esta Conta!!!',0+16,' ')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Else
		If Not fAcessoContas(Usuar, This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value, 'C', This.Value, '', '', '', '', ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			=Messagebox('Acesso Negado!!!', 48, '')
			This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
			This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		EndIf
	Endif

	If not fChecarInativas( TmpCli.IClis, ThisForm.poDataMgr )
		MessageBox('Conta Inativa ...',32,'' )
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		Return .f.
	Endif
	If Empty(This.Parent.get_grupo.Value)
		This.Parent.get_grupo.Value = TmpCli.Grupos
	EndIf
	This.Parent.get_conta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_dconta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_grupo.Refresh

	If (crSigCdOpd.Destinos = 1)
		lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Datas ] + ;
				    [From SigCdFcx ] + ;
				   [Where Emps = '] + ThisForm.pEmps + [' And ] + ;
				   		 [Grupos = '] + TmpNens.GrupoDs + [' And ] + ;
				   		 [Contas = '] + TmpNens.ContaDs + [' ] + ;
				   [Order By Codigos Desc]			    

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalFecha') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalFecha)')
			Return 0
		EndIf

		Select LocalFecha
		Go Top
		If RECCOUNT() > 0 AND (dtos(TmpNens.Datas) < dtos(Ttod(LocalFecha.Datas)+CrSigCdPac.ndFechas))
			Use In LocalFecha
			=Messagebox('Período Bloqueado Para a Conta de Origem!!!', 32, '')
			This.Value = This.Tag
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Use In LocalFecha
	EndIf
Else
	This.Parent.Get_DConta.Value = ''
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.get_buscaop
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 45
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If ThisForm._OldCodigo <> This.Value
	=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
	=Seek(crSigCdOpd.Nivels, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

	_Nivel    = crSigCdOpd.Dopps
	_NivelOp  = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
	_NumNivel = crSigCdOpd.NDopps

	lnop = this.Value
	lnOpi = lnOp * 10000
	lnOpf = (lnOp + 1) * 10000

	_ChaveI = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str(lnOpi,10)
	_ChaveF = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str(lnOpf,10)

	lcsql = [Select numps, cIdChaves From SigCdNec Where EmpDnps BetWeen ?_chaveI and ?_chaveF]
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'BuscaNens')
	Select BuscaNens
	Scan
		Set Decimals to 0
		_Operacao  = Right(Str(BuscaNens.numps, 12), 10)
		_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)

		_Operacao = (_NumNivel * 10000000000 ) + _nOperacao

	*!*		Insert Into TmpOperacao (Codigos) Values (BuscaNens.numps)
		replace codigos with BuscaNens.numps in tmpOperacao
		thisform.pagina.dados.gradeOperaçăo.column1.text1.Value = BuscaNens.numps
		thisform.pagina.dados.gradeOperaçăo.Refresh()

		thisform.pagina.dados.gradeOperaçăo.column1.text1.Valid()
	EndScan
EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
ThisForm._OldCodigo = This.Value
DoDefault()
ENDPROC

		loBrowse.AddColuna('RClis',  '', 'Descriçăo', .t., 'BalNome')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Grupos', '', 'Grupo',     .t., 'BalGrupo' )
		loBrowse.gridProc.SetAll('DynamicForeColor', [Iif(TmpCli.Inativas == 1, Rgb(255, 0, 0), Rgb(0,0,0))], 'Column')
		loBrowse.Show
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.IClis)
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.RClis)
	Else
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = TmpCli.RClis
	EndIf

	lcSql = [Select Fases From SigClStp Where Iclis = ']+TmpCli.Iclis+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalSetP') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalSetP)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	If Reccount('LocalSetP') > 0
		Select LocalSetP
		Locate For Fases = This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value
		If Eof()
			MessageBox('Setor Năo definido para esta Conta!!!',0+16,' ')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Else
		If Not fAcessoContas(Usuar, This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value, 'C', This.Value, '', '', '', '', ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			=Messagebox('Acesso Negado!!!', 48, '')
			This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
			This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		EndIf
	Endif
	If not fChecarInativas( TmpCli.IClis, ThisForm.poDataMgr )
		MessageBox('Conta Inativa ...',32,'' )
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		Return .f.
	Endif

	If Empty(This.Parent.get_grupo.Value)
		This.Parent.get_grupo.Value = TmpCli.Grupos
	EndIf
	This.Parent.get_conta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_dconta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_grupo.Refresh

	If (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'INSERIR')
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados
			If (crSigCdOpd.cRepls = 1) And Empty(.Destino.Get_Conta.Value)
				.Destino.Get_Conta.Value = This.Value
			EndIf
		EndWith
	EndIf
	
	lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Datas ] + ;
			    [From SigCdFcx ] + ;
			   [Where Emps = '] + ThisForm.pEmps + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Grupos = '] + TmpNens.GrupoOs + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Contas = '] + TmpNens.ContaOs + [' ] + ;
			   [Order By Codigos Desc]			    

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalFecha') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalFecha)')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	Select LocalFecha
	Go Top
	If RECCOUNT() > 0 AND (dtos(TmpNens.Datas) < dtos(Ttod(LocalFecha.Datas)+CrSigCdPac.ndFechas) )
		Use In LocalFecha
		=Messagebox('Período Bloqueado Para a Conta de Origem!!!', 32, '')
		This.Value = This.Tag
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Use In LocalFecha
Else
	This.Parent.Get_DConta.Value = ''
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
This.Tag = This.Value
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And Not Empty(This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value) And ThisForm.EditaOrigem
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_dconta
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 64
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not Empty(This.Value)
	If Not Seek(This.Value, 'TmpCli', 'BalNome')
		loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'TmpCli', 'BalNome', This.Value, 'Cadastro de Contas')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('RClis',  '', 'Descriçăo', .t., 'BalNome')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Iclis',  '', 'Código',    .t., 'BalCodigo')
		loBrowse.AddColuna('Grupos', '', 'Grupo',    .t., 'BalGrupo')		
		loBrowse.gridProc.SetAll('DynamicForeColor', [Iif(TmpCli.Inativas == 1, Rgb(255, 0, 0), Rgb(0,0,0))], 'Column')
		loBrowse.Show
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.IClis)
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = Iif(Lastkey()=27, '', TmpCli.RClis)
	Else
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value = TmpCli.IClis
	EndIf

	lcSql = [Select Fases From SigClStp Where Iclis = ']+TmpCli.Iclis+[']
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalSetP') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalSetP)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	If Reccount('LocalSetP') > 0
		Select LocalSetP
		Locate For Fases = This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value
		If Eof()
			MessageBox('Setor Năo definido para esta Conta!!!',0+16,' ')
			Return .f.
		Endif
	Else
		If Not fAcessoContas(Usuar, This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value, 'C', This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value, '', '', '', '', ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			=Messagebox('Acesso Negado!!!', 48, '')
			This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
			This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		EndIf
	Endif
	If not fChecarInativas( TmpCli.IClis, ThisForm.poDataMgr )
		MessageBox('Conta Inativa ...',32,'' )
		This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.Get_dConta.Value = ''
		Return .f.
	Endif

	If Empty(This.Parent.get_grupo.Value)
		This.Parent.get_grupo.Value = TmpCli.Grupos
	EndIf
	This.Parent.get_conta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_dconta.Refresh
	This.Parent.get_grupo.Refresh

	If (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'INSERIR')
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados
			If (crSigCdOpd.CRepls = 1) And Empty(.Destino.Get_Conta.Value)
				.Destino.Get_Conta.Value = .Origem.Get_Conta.Value
			EndIf
		EndWith
	EndIf

	lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Datas ] + ;
			    [From SigCdFcx ] + ;
			   [Where Emps = '] + ThisForm.pEmps + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Grupos = '] + TmpNens.GrupoOs + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [Contas = '] + TmpNens.ContaOs + [' ] + ;
			   [Order By Codigos Desc]			    

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalFecha') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalFecha)')
		Return 0
	EndIf

	Select LocalFecha
	Go Top
	If RECCOUNT() > 0 AND (dtos(TmpNens.Datas) < dtos(Ttod(LocalFecha.Datas)+CrSigCdPac.ndFechas))
		Use In LocalFecha
		=Messagebox('Período Bloqueado Para a Conta de Origem!!!', 32, '')
		This.Value = This.Tag
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Use In LocalFecha
Else
	This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value = ''
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
This.Tag = This.Value
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And Not Empty(This.Parent.Get_Grupo.Value) And ;
	   Empty(This.Parent.Get_Conta.Value) And ThisForm.EditaOrigem
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 67

PROCEDURE When
Return (Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') Or ;
		( ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'PROCURAR' And ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.cntDados.get_codigo.Value = 0 ) )

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Bot_Pendentes
* Classe: commandbutton (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 68
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'INSERIR')
	If Empty(TmpNens.ContaOs)
		=MessageBox('Informe a Conta de Origem!!!', 48, '')
		Return 0
	Else
		Select TmpOperacao
		Go Top
		Count To lnBot For Not Empty(Codigos)
		If (lnBot = 0) And Reccount('xNensi') = 0
			ThisForm.Enabled = .f.
			Do Form SigOpMpn With ThisForm, ThisForm.DataSessionId
		EndIf
	EndIf
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return (ThisForm.pcEscolha <> 'PROCURAR')
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.GradeOperaçăo.Column1.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 72
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
If Empty(This.Value) And (LastKey()=13)
	Set Confirm Off
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.SetFocus
	=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

	Do Case
		Case CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1
			Thisform.Pagina.Dados.Componentes.SetFocus

		Case Not crSigCdOpd.FixGOrigs And ThisForm.EditaOrigem
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_Grupo.SetFocus

		Case Not crSigCdOpd.FixCOrigs And ThisForm.EditaOrigem And Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_Conta.Value)
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_Conta.SetFocus

		Case Not crSigCdOpd.FixGDests
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Grupo.SetFocus

		Case Not crSigCdOpd.FixCDests
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Conta.SetFocus

		Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Responsavel.Visible 
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Responsavel.Get_Grupo.SetFocus

		Case (crSigCdOpd.GrProds = 1)
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Operacao.SetFocus

		Case (crSigCdOpd.GrComps = 1)
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Componentes.SetFocus

		Otherwise
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Componentes.SetFocus
	EndCase
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pNot, pTru
Local NDopp, Nume, CodConf, OpeAtu, _RecnoAnt, _OldCodigo, _TpOpPadrao, _CompAgru, _AgSep

=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
=Seek(crSigCdOpd.Nivels, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

pNot = .f.
pTru = .t.

_Nivel    = crSigCdOpd.Dopps
_NivelOp  = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
_NumNivel = crSigCdOpd.NDopps

=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

_Posicao       = TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10)
_Sequencia     = (crSigCdOpd.Seqs = 1)
_NaoAgrega     = (crSigCdOpd.Agregas = 2)
_PuxaOrigem    = crSigCdOpd.ConOSubs
_PuxaDestino   = crSigCdOpd.ConDSubs
_OldCodigo     = ThisForm._OldCodigo
_BaixaSubnivel = (crSigCdOpd.BxAutos = 1)
_ExclSubn      = (crSigCdOpd.ExclSubns = 1)
_SepPedra      = (InList(crSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4))
_BuscaEnv      = (CrSigCdOpd.BuscaEnvs = 1)
_TrfPesag      = (CrSigCdOpd.TrfPesas )
_Chavei        = ' '
_ChaveF        = ' '
_TpOpPadrao    = ' '
_CompAgru      = ( CrSigCdOpd.CompAgrus )
_AgSep         = ( CrSigCdOpd.AgSeps = 1 )

If (This.Value <> 0) And (This.Value <> _OldCodigo)

	_Operacao  = Right(Str(This.Value, 12), 10)
	_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)

	If _BuscaEnv And Not Empty(crSigCdPam.DopEnvels)
	
		_Encontrou = .f.
		_nVezes = 1

		For _nVezes = 1 to 10
		
			_xOperacao = Val(Str(_nVezes - 1,1)+Transform(_nOperacao,'@l 999999') )

			_Chave = TmpNens.Emps + CrSigCdPam.DopEnvels + Str(_xoperacao,10)
			
			lcSql = [Select CidChaves, ChkSubn From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+_Chave+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
			Select LocalNens

			If ( Not Eof() And LocalNens.ChkSubn ) Or Eof()

			Else
				This.Value = Val(Transform(_xoperacao,'@l 9999999999'))
				Exit
			EndIf
		Next
	Endif

	lnRec = Recno('TmpOperacao')

	LnNivel = (_NumNivel * 10000000000 ) + _nOperacao

	Select Codigos ;
	  From TmpOperacao ;
	 Where (Codigos = This.Value Or Codigos=lnNivel) And ;
	 	   Not Recno() = lnRec ;
	  Into Cursor csTmp

	If (Reccount('csTmp') > 0)
		=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + ' Já Digitad' + ThisForm.Artigo + '!!!', 48, '')
		This.Value = _OldCodigo
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	Use In csTmp
EndIf

If Not Empty(_OldCodigo) And (This.Value <> _OldCodigo)
	Set Decimals to 0
	_Operacao  = Right(Str(_OldCodigo, 12), 10)
	_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)
	_Chave     = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str(_nOperacao,10)

	If (_CompAgru = 1)
		_AgrupaOper = Str(0, 10)
	Else
		_AgrupaOper = _Operacao
	EndIf

	Select TmpOperacao
	Set Order To EmpDnPs
	lcEDPs = EmpDnPs
	If Not Empty(lcEdps)
		Seek lcEdps
	Endif
	Scan While EmpDnPs = lcEDPS
	
		Select CrSigInAop
		Set Order To 
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao
	
		Select xMFas
		Set Order to
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao

		Select xOpi
		Set Order to
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao

		Select xPesa
		Set Order to
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao

		If CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
			Select * from xNensi Where Nenvs = _nOperacao Into Cursor DelxNensi
			Select DelxNensi
			Scan
				If Seek( Str(0,10) + DelxNensi.cMats, 'xNensi', 'NopCmat')
					Replace Qtds      With Qtds - DelxNensi.Qtds ,;
							Pesos     With Pesos - DelxNensi.Pesos ,;
							QtFaseAnt With QtFaseAnt + DelxNensi.QtFaseAnt, ;
							PsFaseAnt With PsFaseAnt + Delxnensi.PsFaseAnt in xNensi
					Select xNensi
					If Qtds <= 0 Or Pesos<= 0
						Delete
					Endif
				EndIf
			EndScan
		Endif

		Select xNensi
		Set Order to
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao
		
		Select xNensiS
		Set Order To 
		Delete All For Nenvs = _nOperacao
		
		Select xnensiR
		Set Order To 
		Delete All For Nenvs = _Noperacao
		
		Select xNensiP
		Set Order to
		Delete All for Nenvs = _nOperacao

		Select CsContas
		Set Order To
		Delete All For Nenvs = _nOperacao
		
		Select xMaterial
		Set Order to
		Delete All For Nenvs = _nOperacao
		
		If Empty(lcedps)
			lcEdn = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + _Operacao
		Else
			lcEdn = lcEDPs
		EndIf
		
		lcSql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcEdn+[']
		ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
		Select LocalNens

		lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
					 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot, nAceites = 0 ] + ;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text)')
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Set Decimals to 2

		If _BaixaSubNivel
			lcSql = [Select Nops, cIdChaves From SigPdMvf Where EmpDnPs = ']+_Chave+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas')
			Select LocalMFas
			Scan
				_Nops       = Nops
				_CheckBaixa = crSigCdOpd.Nivels

				lcEdn = ThisForm.pEmps + _CheckBaixa + Str(_Noperacao, 10)

				lcSql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcEdn+[']
				ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
				Select LocalNens
				Scan
					lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
								 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot ] + ;
							   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 2)')
						Return 0
					EndIf
				Endscan

				lcEdn = ThisForm.pEmps + _NivelOp + Str(_Nops, 10)
				lcSql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcEdn+[']
				ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
				Select LocalNens

				lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
							 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot ] + ;
						   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 2)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
			EndScan
		EndIf
		
		If Empty(lcEDPs)
			Exit
		EndIf
		
		Select TmpOperacao
		Delete
	
	EndScan
	
	Select TmpOperacao
	Set Order To Codigos
	=Seek(This.Value)
	Set Order To
	_RecnoAnt = Recno()
	Go Top
	ThisForm.EditaOrigem = .t.
	Scan For Not Empty(Codigos) And Not _SepPedra
		ThisForm.EditaOrigem = .f.
		Exit
	EndScan
	Locate For Recno() = _RecnoAnt

	If (CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 1 And ThisForm.tiposubnivel = 'OP') Or ;
		(CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 2 And ThisForm.Tiposubnivel = 'ENV')
	Else
		Skip
		If Eof()
			Insert Into TmpOperacao (Codigos) Values (0)
		EndIf
	Endif
EndIf

Ok = .t.

If Not Empty(This.Value) And (This.Value <> _OldCodigo)

	If CrSigCdOpd.Grodns = 1

		=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
		
		_NivelOs = CrSigCdOpd.Nivels
	
		Set Decimals to 0
		_Operacao  = Right(Str(This.Value, 12), 10)
		_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)

		This.Value = (_NumNivel * 10000000000 ) + _nOperacao

		lcQuery = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datas, ContaDs From SigPdMvf ]+;
				[Where Nenvs = ]+Str(_nOperacao)+[ And Dopps = ']+_NivelOs+[' And Emps = ']+TmpNens.Emps+[' ]+;
				[ Order By CidChaves Desc]

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalEnve') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalEnve)')
			Return 0
		EndIf

		Select LocalEnve
		Go Top
		If Reccount() = 0 Or ContaDs # TmpNens.ContaOs
			=MessageBox('Os em Outra Fase Ou năo Encontrado!!!', 0+48 )
			Return 0
		EndIf
		
		=Seek(LocalEnve.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

		_ChaveNens = LocalEnve.Emps + LocalEnve.Dopps + Str(LocalEnve.Numps, 10)

		lcSql = [Select CidChaves, Retrabs, Chksubn From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+_ChaveNens+[']
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')

		If (LocalNens.ChkSubn)
			=Messagebox('Movimentaçăo Năo Pendente Para Aceite!!!', 48, '')
			This.Value = 0
			Return 0
		EndIf

		lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
					 [Set NAceites = ] + Alltrim(Str(TmpNens.Numps, 10)) + [ ] + ;
					 Iif(_BaixaSubnivel,[, ChkSubn = ?pTru ],[])+;
				   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (OK - Update - SigCdNec)')
			Return 0
		EndIf

		If LocalNens.Retrabs
			Replace Retrabs With .t. In TmpNens
		Else
			Replace Retrabs With .f. In TmpNens
		EndIf

		lcSql = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datars, Datas, Usuars, Opers, ]+;
				[Grupoos, Contaos, Grupods, Contads, Nops, Nenvs, ]+;
				[Dopes, Numes, Dataps, Dataes, Obss, Codpds, Unids, ]+;
				[Pesos, Qtds, Obsps, Ordems, cRetrabs From SigPdMvf Where EmpDnPs = ']+_ChaveNens+[']
				
		ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalMfas')

		Select LocalMFas
		Scan
			_Nops   = LocalMfas.Nops
			lcQuery = [Select a.Nops, a.Datas, a.cidChaves From SigPdMvf a ] + ;
					   [Where a.Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops)) + [ And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ] + ;
					   [Order By a.Nops Desc, a.cIdChaves Desc]
			
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas2') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalMFas2)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Select LocalMFas2
			Go Top

			If (Dtos(LocalMFas2.Datas) > Dtos(TmpNens.datas) )
				=Messagebox('Data inconsistente. Último lançamento com data de '+Dtoc(LocalMfas2.datas), 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			EndIf

			Insert Into xMFas (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datars, Datas, Usuars, Opers, Grupoos, Contaos, Grupods, ;
							   Contads, NOps, NEnvs, Dopes, Numes, Dataps, Dataes, Obss, Codpds, Unids, Pesos, ;
							   Qtds, Obsps, Ordems, cRetrabs, TmpMins  ) ;
					   Values (LocalMFas.Emps, LocalMFas.Dopps, LocalMFas.Numps, LocalMFas.Datars, LocalMFas.Datas, ;
					   		   LocalMFas.Usuars, LocalMFas.Opers, LocalMFas.Grupoos, LocalMFas.Contaos, ;
					   		   LocalMFas.Grupods, LocalMFas.Contads, LocalMFas.Nops, LocalMFas.Nenvs, ;
					   		   LocalMFas.Dopes, LocalMFas.Numes, LocalMFas.Dataps, LocalMFas.Dataes, ;
					   		   LocalMFas.Obss, LocalMFas.Codpds, LocalMFas.Unids, LocalMFas.Pesos, ;
					   		   LocalMFas.Qtds, LocalMFas.Obsps, LocalMFas.Ordems, LocalMFas.cRetrabs, TmpOperacao.TmpMins)

			If Not Seek((_NumNivel * 10000000000 ) + xMFas.NEnvs, 'TmpOperacao', 'Codigos')
				Insert Into TmpOperacao (Codigos) Values ((_NumNivel * 10000000000) + xMFas.NEnvs)
			EndIf
			Replace EmpDnPs With _ChaveNens,;
					Autos   With .t. In TmpOperacao
			
			lcSql = [Select Emps, Dopes, Numes, Qtds, CodCors, CodTams, Empds, CodTgops, citens From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(LocalMfas.Nops)
			Thisform.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')

			Select LocalOpi
			Scan
				If (LocalOpi.Qtds <> 0)
					lcEmp = Iif(Empty(LocalOpi.EmpDs), LocalOpi.Emps, LocalOpi.EmpDs)
					lcEdn = LocalOpi.Emps + LocalOpi.Dopes + Str(LocalOpi.Numes, 6)
					
					lcSql = [Select ContaOs, ContaDs From SigMvCab Where EmpDopNums = ']+lcEdn+[']
					ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalEest')
					
					lcSql = [Select Globalizas, servicos From SigCdOpe Where Dopes = ']+LocalOpi.Dopes+[']
					ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpe')

					lcSql = [Select dopes, EncPesMs From SigOpCdc Where Dopes = ']+LocalOpi.Dopes+[']
					ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalDcOpe')

					If (LocalOpe.Globalizas = 1) Or (LocalOpe.Servicos = 1)
						lcContaOs = LocalEest.ContaOs
					Else
						lcContaOs = LocalEest.ContaDs
					EndIf

					Insert Into xOpi (Nops, Oper, Qtds, CPros, Indiv, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, ;
									  Conta, Empds, CodCors, CodTams, Obrigs, divs, citens ) ;
							  Values (LocalMFas.NOps, Alltrim(LocalOpi.Dopes ) + '/' + Alltrim(Str(LocalOpi.Numes)), ;
							  		  LocalOpi.Qtds, LocalMFas.CodPds, (crSigCdPam.TpPesas = 1 And LocalDcOpe.EncPesms <> 1), ;
							  		  LocalMFas.Nenvs, LocalOpi.Emps, LocalOpi.Dopes, LocalOpi.Numes, lcContaOs, ;
							  		  lcEmp, LocalOpi.CodCors, LocalOpi.CodTams, LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs = 1, LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs = 1, LocalOpi.citens )
				EndIf
			EndScan
		EndScan

		lcSql = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, ]+;
				[Qtds, Pesos, TpOps, Cats, FlagIncs, CUnis, Obss, Servicos, Peso2s, CodCors, CodTams ]+; 
				[From SigCdNei Where EmpDnPs = ']+_chaveNens+[']
	
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNensi')

		Select LocalNensi
		Scan
			_NEnv     = LocalNensi.NEnvs
			_TotalNop = 0
			_RecNensi = Recno()

			Scan While (NEnvs = _NEnv)
			
				lcsql = [Select CGrus, Varias, Dpros, Cunis, cUnips From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+LocalNensi.cmats+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

				*** Tiago - 22/12/2011 - Martinelli - Voltei a checagem da flag CrSigCdOpd.AcEnvs = 1 que o Richard havia retirado; 
				*** sem ela o aceite de envelope com mais de uma OP năo carrega o peso dos componentes agregados corretamente
				lnRateio  = 5
				llVisivel = .t.		
				If CrSigCdOpd.AcEnvs = 1
				****
					If (LocalNensi.Nops = 0)
						lnRateio  = 5
						llVisivel = .t.
					Else
						lnRateio  = Iif(LocalPro.Varias = 1, 2, 3)
						llVisivel = .f.
					Endif
				Endif

				_Servico = LocalNensi.Servicos

				If Not _Servico And Not Empty(LocalNensi.CMats) And Empty(LocalNensi.Cats)
					Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs,  QtFaseAnt, Qtds, PsFaseAnt, ;
										Pesos, Visivel, Rateio, TpOps, Cats, FlagIncs, CUnis, CGrus, Obss, cUniPs, ;
										Peso2s, Ps2FaseAnt, CodCors, codTams) ;
								Values (LocalNensi.Emps, LocalNensi.Dopps, LocalNensi.Numps, LocalNensi.Nops, ;
										LocalNensi.NEnvs, LocalNensi.CMats, LocalNensi.CDescs, LocalNensi.Qtds, ;
										LocalNensi.Qtds, LocalNensi.Pesos, LocalNensi.Pesos, llVisivel, lnRateio, ;
										LocalNensi.TpOps, LocalNensi.Cats, LocalNensi.FlagIncs, LocalNensi.CUnis, ;
										LocalPro.CGrus, LocalNensi.Obss, LocalPro.cuniPs, LocalNensi.Peso2s,;
										LocalNensi.Peso2s, LocalNensi.CodCors, LocalNensi.codTams)

					*** Tiago - 22/12/2011 - Martinelli - Voltei a checagem da flag CrSigCdOpd.AcEnvs = 1 que o Richard havia retirado; 
					*** sem ela o aceite de envelope com mais de uma OP năo carrega o peso dos componentes agregados corretamente
					If CrSigCdOpd.AcEnvs = 1
					****
						If LocalNensi.FlagIncs
							_BMat   = LocalNensi.CMats
							_DMat   = LocalPro.DPros
							_CMat   = LocalPro.CUnis
							_GMat   = LocalPro.CGrus
							_CatMat = LocalNensi.Cats
						Else
							_BMat   = Space(10)
							_DMat   = ''
							_CMat   = ''
							_GMat   = ''
							_CatMat = '   '
						EndIf
						_TMat = LocalNensi.TpOps

						If (_CompAgru = 1)
							_Nenv = 0
						EndIf

						If (lnRateio <> 5)
							If Not Seek(Str(_Nenv, 10) + _BMat + _TMat, 'xNensi', 'NEnvTpops')
								Insert Into xNensi (Nops, Nenvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, Visivel, Rateio, Cats, TpOps, Servicos) ;
											Values (_NEnv, _NEnv, _BMat, _DMat, _CMat, _GMat, .t., 1, _CatMat, _TMat, _Servico)
							Else
								If (xNensi.Rateio <> 1)
									Replace Rateio With 1 In xNensi
								EndIf
							EndIf

							Select xNensi
							Replace QtFaseAnt With xNensi.QtFaseAnt + LocalNensi.Qtds, ;
									PsFaseAnt With xNensi.PsFaseAnt + LocalNensi.Pesos, ;
									Ps2FaseAnt With xNensi.Ps2FaseAnt + LocalNensi.Peso2s, ;
									Qtds 	  With xNensi.Qtds  + LocalNensi.Qtds, ;
									Pesos 	  With xNensi.Pesos + LocalNensi.Pesos In xNensi
						Endif
					Endif
				EndIf
			EndScan
			Select LocalNensi
			Skip - 1
		EndScan
		
		=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
		
		If (CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 1 And ThisForm.tiposubnivel = 'OP') Or ;
			(CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 2 And ThisForm.Tiposubnivel = 'ENV')
		Else
			Select TmpOperacao
			Delete For Codigos = 0
			Set Order To Codigos
			Seek 0
			If Eof()
				Insert Into TmpOperacao (Codigos) Values (0)
			EndIf
			Set Order To
			Go Bott
			Keyboard '{PGDN}'
			
			Thisform.Pagina.Dados.GradeOperaçăo.Refresh
		Endif
	Else
		Set Decimals To 0
		_Operacao  = Str(Val(Right(Str(This.Value, 12), 10)), 10)
		_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)
		_Chave     = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + _Operacao
		If CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
			_ChaveI    = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str((_nOperacao*10000)+1,10)
			_ChaveF    = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str((_nOperacao*10000)+9999,10)
		Endif
		If (_CompAgru = 1)
			_AgrupaOper  = Str(0, 10)
			_nAgrupaOper = 0
		Else
			_AgrupaOper  = _Operacao
			_nAgrupaOper = _nOperacao
		EndIf
		Set Decimals to 2

		lcQuery = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends, ChkSubn From SigCdNec Where EmpDnps = ']+_chave+[']
		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalNens]) < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalNens)])
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Go Top In LocalNens
		If Eof('LocalNens') And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras # 4
			=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + ' Năo Localizad' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' !!!', 0+48, '')
			This.Value = 0
			Select TmpNens
			Ok = .f.
			Return 0
		EndIf

		If LocalNens.ChkSubn And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras # 4
			=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + ' Já Foi Encerrad' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' !!!', 0+48, '')
			This.Value = 0
			Select TmpNens
			Ok = .f.
			Return 0
		EndIf
		
		If ThisForm.TipoSubnivel = 'OP' And CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 1 And Not InList(CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4)
			Select dopps From CrSigCdOpd Where ChkDests = 1 Into Cursor TmpOppE
			If Reccount('TmpOppE') > 0 And CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 10 And CrSigCdPac.MovOpEvs = 1
				lcSql = [Select Numps From SigPdMvf Where Nops = ]+Str(_Noperacao,10)+[ And dopps = ']+TmpOppE.Dopps+[']
				If ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpMfEnv') > 0 And Reccount('TmpMfEnv') > 0
					MessageBox('Movimentaçăo năo Permitida. Op com Envelopagem '+Alltrim(Str(TmpMfEnv.Numps,10)),0+48,'')
					This.Value = 0
					Return .f.
				EndIf
			EndIf
		Endif
		
		lcsql = [Select CodPds From SigPdMvf Where EmpDnps = ']+_chave+[']
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas')
		Select LocalMFas
		Scan
			lcsql = [Select MatPrincs,Cgrus From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+LocalMfas.codpds+[']
			ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')
			
			lcsql = [Select Mercs From SigCdGrp Where Cgrus = ']+LocalPro.Cgrus+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalGru')
			
			lcsql = [Select MatPrincs From SigCdGpr Where Codigos = ']+LocalGru.Mercs+[']
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalGgrp')
			
			_MatP = IIF(!EMPTY(LocalPro.MatPrincs),LocalPro.MatPrincs,IIF(!EMPTY(LocalGgrp.Matprincs),LocalGgrp.MatPrincs,CrSigCdPam.Ouros))

			Select xMaterial
			Append Blank
			Replace Nenvs With _nOperacao, ;
					Cpros With LocalMfas.CodPds, ;
					MatPs With _MatP
		EndScan

		Select Distinct MatPs ;
		  From xMaterial ;
		 Into Cursor csResultado
		
		*-- Rafael - 26/09/2016 - Permite Material Principal diferente na mesma OP 
		If CrSigCdOpd.MatPrncDif = 1 Or CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4
			*-- Nao faz validaçăo do material principal
		Else
			If (Reccount('csResultado') > 1) And CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras # 4
				=Messagebox('Lançar Somente Produtos Com Mesmo Material Principal!!!', 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			EndIf
		EndIf 
		
		Select csResultado
		Go Top

		If (crSigCdOpd.Chkfunds = 1)
			lcsql = [Select Codigos, Tubos From SigCdFud Where Nops = ]+Str(This.Value)
			ThisForm.PodataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalIfund')
			Select LocalIfund
			If Not Eof('LocalIfund')
				_Tubo = LocalIfund.Tubos
				_Cod  = LocalIfund.Codigos

				lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
						    [From SigCdFud ] + ;
						   [Where Codigos = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Cod)) + [ And ] + ;
						   		 [Tubos = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Tubo))

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalIfund') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalIfund)')
					Return 0
				EndIf

				_Libera = .f.

				Select LocalIfund
				Scan
					If Not Empty(nNumes)
						_Libera = .t.
						Exit
					EndIf
				EndScan

				If Not _Libera
					=Messagebox('Fundiçăo : ' + Alltrim(Str(_Cod, 6)) + ' - ' + ;
								'Tubo : ' + Str(_Tubo, 2) + ' Sem Transformaçőes Informadas!!!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpNens
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndIf

		If CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests = 3 && Se operaçăo for de Encerramento e se a OP teve reposiçăo de pedras, checa se teve a devoluçăo das pedras trocadas
			lcSql = [Select Cods From SigOpOpt Where ChkDevs = 'S' ]
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'TmpOPt') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalNoo)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Select TmpOpt
			If Reccount() > 0
				lnEnv = VAL(RIGHT(STR(This.Value,12),10))
				*** Tiago - 05/04/2012 - Vianna - Checagem era só B.SEPPEDRAS = 1, mudei para checar = 4 pois a OP tinha que ter o material agregado para sair no histórico
				lcSql = [Select a.Cmats, a.Qtds, a.TpOps From SigCdNei a, SigCdOpd b, SigOpOpt c ]+;
						[Where a.Nenvs = ]+Str(lnEnv,10)+[ And a.Dopps = b.Dopps And b.SepPedras in (1,4) ]+;
						[And b.ChkDests = 6 And a.TpOps = c.Cods And c.chkDevs = 'S' And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ]+;
						[union all ]+;
						[Select a.Cmats, (a.Qtds*-1) as Qtds, a.TpOps From SigCdNei a, SigCdOpd b ]+;
						[Where a.Nenvs = ]+Str(lnEnv,10)+[ And a.Dopps = b.Dopps ]+;
						[And b.ChkDests = 4 And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ]+;
						[Order by a.Cmats ]
				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalNoo') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalNoo)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
				
				Select cmats, Sum(qtds) as Qtds From LocalNoo Group by cmats Into Cursor Selecao
				Select Selecao
				Scan
					If Qtds > 0
						=Messagebox('A Devoluçăo de Pedra Ainda năo foi lançada!!!', 0+48, '')
						DO Form SigPdM13 With ThisForm,This.Value
						This.Value = 0
						Select TmpNens
						Ok = .f.
						Return 0
					EndIf
				EndScan
			Endif
		EndIf

		Create Cursor Destino (GrupoOs c(10), ContaOs c(10))
		Append Blank

		lcsql = [Select a.Nops, a.Nenvs, a.Dopps, a.NumPs, b.CodTgOps From SigPdMvf a, SigOpPic b ]+;
				[Where a.EmpDnPs = ']+_chave+[' And a.Nops = b.Nops ]
		Thisform.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas')
		Select LocalMFas
		Scan While Not _SepPedra
			=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
			_Nops      = Nops
			_Nenvs     = Nenvs
			_DoppMf    = Dopps
			_Numpp     = Numps
			_RecnoMFas = Recno()

			If ( Not Empty(crSigCdOpd.CodTgOps) And LocalMFas.CodTgOps <> crSigCdOpd.CodTgOps )
				=Messagebox('Op do Tipo '+LocalMfas.CodTgOps+' Nao Permitido Nesta Operacao!!!', 48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Return 0
			EndIf
			
			lcQuery = [Select a.Nops, a.Datas, a.Dopps, a.GrupoOs, a.ContaOs, a.GrupoDs, a.ContaDs, a.CodPds, a.Ordems, a.cIdChaves, a.Qtds, b.ChkDests ] + ;
					    [From SigPdMvf a, SigCdOpd b ] + ;
					   [Where a.Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops)) + [ And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' And a.Dopps = b.Dopps ] + ;
					   [Order By a.Nops Desc, a.cIdChaves Desc]
			
			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas2') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalMFas2)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Select LocalMFas2
			Go Top

			If Not Empty(TmpNens.Grupoos) And (LocalMFas2.Grupods <> TmpNens.Grupoos)
				=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Em Outra Fase (' + LocalMFas2.Grupods + ')!', 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			Else
				If Empty(TmpNens.GrupoOs) And Not Empty(Destino.GrupoOs) And (LocalMFas2.Grupods <> Destino.GrupoOs)
					=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Em Outra Fase (' + LocalMFas2.Grupods + ')!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpNens
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				Endif
			EndIf

			If Not Empty(TmpNens.Contaos) And (LocalMFas2.Contads <> TmpNens.Contaos)
				=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Com Outro Funcionário!!!', 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			Else
				If Empty(TmpNens.Contaos) And Not Empty(Destino.ContaOs) And (LocalMFas2.Contads <> Destino.ContaOs)
					=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Com Outro Funcionário!!!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpNens
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				Endif
			EndIf
			Replace GrupoOs With LocalMfas2.GrupoDs,;
					ContaOs With LocalMfas2.ContaDs In Destino

			If (crSigCdOpd.Grodns <> 1) And (LocalMFas2.Grupods = crSigCdPam.GrTrans) And Not Empty(crSigCdPam.GrTrans)
				=Messagebox('Movimentaçăo Sem Aceite!!!', 48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Return 0
			EndIf

			If (crSigCdOpd.Grodns = 1) And (LocalMFas2.Grupods <> crSigCdPam.GrTrans) And Not Empty(crSigCdPam.GrTrans)
				=Messagebox('Movimentaçăo Năo Pendente Para Aceite!!!', 48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Return 0
			EndIf

			If (Dtos(LocalMFas2.Datas) > Dtos(TmpNens.datas) )
				=Messagebox('Data inconsistente. Ultimo lançamento com data de '+Dtoc(LocalMfas2.datas), 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			EndIf
			If LocalMfas2.ChkDests = 10
				Replace GrupoO With LocalMfas2.GrupoOs,;
						ContaO With LocalMfas2.ContaOs in TmpOperacao
			Endif

			_CheckBaixa = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
			If Not Empty(crSigCdOpd.Nivels) And Seek(LocalMFas2.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps') And Not Empty(crSigCdOpd.Nivels)
				_CheckBaixa = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
				=Seek(_CheckBaixa,'CrSigCdOpd','Dopps')
				If Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.Nivels)
					If CrSigCdOpd.Nivels <> CrSigCdPam.DoppPads And CrSigCdOpd.Nivels <> CrSigCdPam.DoppServs 
						_CheckBaixa = CrSigCdOpd.Nivels
					Endif
				Endif
			EndIf

			=Seek(LocalMFas2.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps') 
			_Nopp = _Nops
			If CrSigCdOpd.Nivels <> CrSigCdPam.DoppPads And CrSigCdOpd.Nivels <> CrSigCdPam.DoppServs 
				_Nopp =  _Nenvs
				If _Nopp = _Nenvs
					_Nopp = _Numpp
				Endif
			EndIf

			lcEdn = ThisForm.pEmps + _CheckBaixa + Str(_Nopp, 10)
			lcsql = [Select ChkSubn, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where EmpDnPs = ']+lcedn+[']
			ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
			Select LocalNens
			If ChkSubn
				=Messagebox(Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Já Foi Finalizada!!!', 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			EndIf

			=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

			lcsql = [Select Obss From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(_Nops)
			ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')
			Select LocalOpi
			Scan
				If Not isEmpty(LocalOpi.Obss)
					lcSql = [Select CidChaves From SigCdMsg Where EmpCpros = ']+ ThisForm.Pemps + Padr('OBSOP',10)+[']
					ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'CrTmpMens')
					Select CrTmpMens
					If Reccount() > 0
						DO Form SigPdMen With CrTmpMens.CidChaves, 'Op '+Transf( _Nops, '@L 9999999999' ) + ' Com Observaçăo!!!'+Chr(13),Alltrim(LocalOpi.Obss)
						Exit
					EndIf
				EndIf
			EndScan

			If _Sequencia
				lcsql = [Select CidChaves From SigCdPrf Where Produtos = ']+LocalMFas2.CodPds+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalProf')
				If Not Eof('LocalProf')
					lcQuery = [Select Produtos, Ordems, Grupos, Ordem2 ] + ;
							    [From SigCdPrf ] + ;
							   [Where Produtos = '] + LocalMFas2.CodPds + [' And ] + ;
							   		 [Ordems = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalMFas2.Ordems + 1)) + [ ] + ;
							   [Order By Produtos, Ordems, ordem2, Grupos]

					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalProF') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalProF)')
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Select LocalProF
					Go Top
					If Not Eof('LocalProF') And Not Empty(TmpNens.Grupoos)
						If (TmpNens.Grupoos <> LocalProf.Grupos)
							Scan While Grupos <> TmpNens.Grupoos
							EndScan
						EndIf
						If Not Eof()
							Skip
						EndIf
						If Not Eof() And Produtos = LocalMFas2.CodPds
							If (Not Empty(TmpNens.Grupods) And (TmpNens.Grupods <> LocalProf.Grupos) And (crSigCdOpd.InibMens <> 1))
								lcMensagem = ThisForm.Titulo + ' ' + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' ' + ;
											'Fora da Seqüęncia de Produçăo...' + Chr(13) + Chr(13) + ;
											'Fase Selecionada : ' + Alltrim(TmpNens.Grupods) + Chr(13) + Chr(13) + ;
											'Fase Correta : ' + Alltrim(LocalProf.Grupos)

								Select TmpOperacao
								lnRecnoConta = Recno()
								Count to lnConta 
								If (lnConta > 1)
									=Messagebox(lcMensagem + Chr(13) + Chr(13) + ThisForm.Titulo + ' ' + ;
												'Deve Ser Movimentad' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' Separadamente!!!', 32, '')
									This.Value = 0
									Select TmpNens
									Ok = .f.
									Return 0
								Else
									lnResp = Messagebox(lcMensagem + Chr(13) + Chr(13) + ;
													    'Deseja Fazer ' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' ' + ThisForm.Titulo + ' ' + ;
													    'Entrar Na Seqüęncia Novamente ?', 3+32, '')
									If (lnResp = 2) Or (lnResp = 7) && Cancel
										This.Value = 0
										Select TmpNens
										Ok = .f.
										Return 0
									EndIf
								EndIf
							EndIf
						EndIf
					EndIf
				Else
					=Messagebox('O Produto ' + Alltrim(LocalMFas2.CodPds ) + ' Năo Possui Cadastro de Processo...' + Chr(13) + ;
								'Năo Será Possível Checar Se a Seqüęncia de Produçăo Está Correta!!!', 32, '')
				EndIf
			EndIf

			lcQuery = [Update SigPdMvf ] + ;
						 [Set cidchaves = cidchaves ] + ;
					   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMFas2.cIdChaves + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
				=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Em Uso Por Outra Movimentaçăo!!!', 0+48, '')
				This.Value = 0
				Select TmpNens
				Ok = .f.
				Return 0
			EndIf

			If _ExclSubn
				lcSql = [Select Emps, Dopps, Numps From SigPdMvf Where Nops = ]+Str(_Noperacao)+[ And emps = ']+_Empr+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas3')
				Select LocalMFas3
				Scan
					If (Emps + Dopps = TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps) And (Numps = TmpNens.Numps)
						=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + ' Já Foi Envelopado!!!', 0+48, '')
						This.Value = 0
						Select TmpNens
						Ok = .f.
						Return 0
					EndIf
				EndScan
			EndIf
			Select LocalMfas
			Locate for Recno() = _RecnoMFas
		Endscan

		If _SepPedra And CrSigCdOpd.ChkCtDes = 1 And Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.GruDests) And Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.ConDests)
			Select LocalMFas
			Scan
				=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
				_Nops      = Nops
				_Nenvs     = Nenvs
				_DoppMf    = Dopps
				_Numpp     = Numps
				_RecnoMFas = Recno()
			
				lcQuery = [Select Nops, Datas, Dopps, GrupoOs, ContaOs, GrupoDs, ContaDs, CodPds, Ordems, cIdChaves, Qtds ] + ;
						    [From SigPdMvf ] + ;
						   [Where Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops)) + [ And Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ] + ;
						   [Order By Nops Desc, cIdChaves Desc]
			
				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas2') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalMFas2)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
				Select LocalMFas2
				Go Top

				If (CrSigCdOpd.GruDests + CrSigCdOpd.ConDests) <> (LocalMFas2.Grupods + LocalMfas2.ContaDs)
					=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Năo está na Fase Destino!!!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpNens
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				Endif

				*** Tiago - 23/06/2015 - Vianna - Inclui para travar o registro quando for separaçăo de pedra, pois estavam movimentando a OP ao mesmo tempo em movimentaçăo diferentes
				lcQuery = [Update SigPdMvf ] + ;
							 [Set cidchaves = cidchaves ] + ;
						   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalMFas2.cIdChaves + [']

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Em Uso Por Outra Movimentaçăo!!!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpNens
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				Endif							
			EndScan
		Endif

		If Ok
			Select crSigCdOpd
			Seek TmpNens.Dopps
			Select xMFas
			If Not Empty(_OldCodigo)
				Select xMFas
				Delete All For Nenvs = Val(Right(Str(_OldCodigo, 12), 10))

				Select xOpi
				Delete All For Nenvs = Val(Right(Str(_OldCodigo, 12), 10))

				Select xPesa
				Delete All For Nenvs = Val(Right(Str(_OldCodigo, 12), 10))

				lcEdn = TmpNens.Emps + _Nivel + Str(Val(Right(Str(_OldCodigo, 12), 10)), 10)
				lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where EmpDNPs = ']+lcedn+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
				Select LocalNens

				lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
							 [Set ChkSubn = ?pNot ] + ;
						   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 3)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
				Set Decimals to 2
			EndIf

			Select xNensi
			Set Order to 
			If Not Empty(_OldCodigo)
				Delete All For Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10) = _Chave
			EndIf

			Delete All For Empty(CMats) And Empty(Nops) And Empty(Qtds) And Empty(PsFaseAnt)

			If Not _SepPedra
				ThisForm.EditaOrigem = .f.
			EndIf
			
			Go Top

			If CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4 And Reccount('LocalNens') = 0
				lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends, ChkSubn From SigCdNec Where EmpDnps BetWeen ]+;
						[']+_chavei+[' And ']+_ChaveF+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
				If Eof('LocalNens')
					=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + ' Năo Localizad' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' !!!', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpOperacao
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				EndIf
				
				Select Codigos From TmpOperacao ;
				Where Codigos > 0 Into Cursor csTmp
				
				lcsql = [Select Nops, CodPds, Ordems, Nenvs, Datars, Datas, Opers, Unids, Pesos, Obsps, Obss, Qtds ]+;
						[From SigPdMvf Where Empdnps Between ']+_chavei+[' And ']+_ChaveF+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas')
				
				ThisForm.InformouOp = .t.

			Else
				
				If ThisForm.InformouOp
					=Messagebox('Operaçăo Invalida!!!, Informe somente OPs ', 0+48, '')
					This.Value = 0
					Select TmpOperacao
					Ok = .f.
					Return 0
				Else
					lcsql = [Select Nops, CodPds, Ordems, Nenvs, Datars, Datas, Opers, Unids, Pesos, Obsps, Obss, Qtds ]+;
							[From SigPdMvf Where Empdnps = ']+_chave+[']
					ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalMfas')
				Endif
			Endif

			Select LocalMFas
			INDEX ON Nops TAG Nops
			Scan
				_Nops 	   = Nops
				_RecnoMFas = Recno()
	
				lcQuery = [Select a.Nops, a.Datas, a.GrupoOs, a.ContaOs, a.GrupoDs, a.ContaDs, a.cIdChaves, a.CodPds, ]+;
						  [a.Nenvs, a.Datars, a.Opers, a.Unids, a.Pesos, a.Obsps, a.ordems, a.Obss, a.Dopps, a.Numps, b.CravCers ] + ;
						  [From SigPdMvf a, SigCdPro b ] + ;
						  [Where a.Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops)) + [ And a.CodPds = b.Cpros And a.emps = ']+_Empr+[' ] + ;
						  [Order By a.Nops Desc, a.cIdChaves Desc]

				If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalNops') < 1)
					=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalNops)')
					Return 0
				EndIf
				Select LocalNops
				Go Top
				
				If CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras = 4 And CrSigCdOpd.CravCers = 1 And LocalNops.CravCers <> 1
					Loop
				Endif

				If Inlist(_PuxaOrigem, 1, 2)
					If Empty(TmpNens.GrupoOs) Or (Empty(TmpNens.ContaOs) And Not crSigCdOpd.FixGOrigs)
						ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_Grupo.Value = Iif(_PuxaOrigem=1, LocalNops.Grupoos, LocalNops.Grupods)
					EndIf
					If Empty(TmpNens.ContaOs) 
						ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Origem.Get_Conta.Value = Iif(_PuxaOrigem=1, LocalNops.Contaos, LocalNops.Contads)
					EndIf
				EndIf
				
				If InList(_PuxaDestino, 1, 2)
					If Empty(TmpNens.Grupods )
						ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Grupo.Value = Iif(_PuxaDestino=1, LocalNops.Grupoos, LocalNops.Grupods)
					EndIf
					If Empty(TmpNens.Contads)
						ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Conta.Value = Iif(_PuxaDestino=1, LocalNops.Contaos, LocalNops.Contads)
					EndIf
				EndIf
				=Seek(TmpNens.GrupoOs,'TmpGccr','BalCodigo')
				If _TrfPesag = 7
					_TrfPesag = Iif(TmpGccr.TrfPesas=2,5,Iif(TmpGccr.TrfPesas=4,0,Iif(TmpGccr.TrfPesas=5,9,TmpGccr.TrfPesas)))
				EndIf
				If InList(TmpGccr.CompAgrus,1,3)
					_CompAgru = TmpGccr.CompAgrus
					Set Decimals To 0
					If (_CompAgru = 1)
						_AgrupaOper  = Str(0, 10)
						_nAgrupaOper = 0
					Else
						_AgrupaOper  = _Operacao
						_nAgrupaOper = _nOperacao
					EndIf
					Set Decimals to 2
				Endif
				
				_TpOpPadrao = Thisform.RetTpOp()

				If Not IsEmpty(CrSigCdPac.contaRs) And TmpNens.ContaOs = CrSigCdPac.ContaRs And CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 7
					Select Dopps From crSigCdOpd Where ChkDests = 6 Into Cursor TmpRepo
					If Reccount('TmpRepo') > 0 
						lcSql = [Select a.Cmats, a.Qtds From SigCdNei a, SigCdOpd b ]+;
								[Where a.Nenvs = ]+Str(This.Value,10)+[ And a.Dopps = b.Dopps And b.ChkDests = 6 ]+;
								[Order by a.Cmats ]
						If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'LocalNoo') < 1)
							=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalNoo)')
							Return 0
						EndIf
						
						Select LocalNoo
						If Reccount() = 0
							=Messagebox('A Reposiçăo Desta OS Ainda năo foi lançada!!!', 0+48, '')
							This.Value = 0
							Select TmpNens
							Ok = .f.
							Return 0
						EndIf
					EndIf
				EndIf

				If _BaixaSubNivel
					_CheckBaixa = crSigCdOpd.Nivels
					llPcc = crSigCdOpd.Pccs					
					
					lcChv = ThisForm.pEmps + _CheckBaixa + Str(_Noperacao, 10)
					lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where empdnps = ']+lcchv+[']
					ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
					Select LocalNens
					Scan
						lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
									 [Set ChkSubn = ?pTru, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
								   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

						If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
							=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 4)')
							Return 0
						EndIf
					EndScan

					lcChv = ThisForm.pEmps + _Nivelop + Str(_Nops, 10)
					lcsql = [Select cIdChaves, Vends, GrVends From SigCdNec Where empdnps = ']+lcchv+[']
					ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalNens')
					Select LocalNens
					If Not Eof()
						lcQuery = [Update SigCdNec ] + ;
									 [Set ChkSubn = ?pTru, Lccs = ?llPcc ] + ;
								   [Where cIdChaves = '] + LocalNens.cIdChaves + [']

						If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, '') < 1)
							=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Update - SigCdNec - Text 5)')
							Return 0
						EndIf
					EndIf
				EndIf
				
				If _Sequencia
					lcQuery = [Select Produtos, Ordems, Grupos, Ordem2 ] + ;
							    [From SigCdPrf ] + ;
							   [Where Produtos = '] + LocalNOPS.CodPds + [' And ] + ;
							   		 [Ordems >= ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalNOPS.Ordems)) + [ ] + ;
							   [Order By Produtos, Ordems, ordem2, Grupos ]

					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalProF') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalProF 2)')
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Select LocalProF
					Go Top
					If Not Eof()
						DO while Ordems = LocalNops.Ordems
							Skip
						EndDo
						If Not Eof() And (Produtos = Localnops.CodPds) And (LocalProF.Ordems = Localnops.Ordems + 1)
							If Empty(TmpNens.Grupods)
								ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Grupo.Value = LocalProF.Grupos
							EndIf
						EndIf
						If (Eof() Or Produtos <> LocaLNops.CodPds) And (crSigCdOpd.InibMens <> 1)
							=Messagebox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' ' + ;
										'Chegou ao Fim da Seqüęncia de Produçăo!!!', 32, '')
						EndIf
					Else
						If (crSigCdOpd.InibMens <> 1)
							=MessageBox(ThisForm.Titulo + Transform(_Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' ' + ;
										'Chegou ao Fim da Seqüęncia de Produçăo!!!', 32, '')
						EndIf
					EndIf
				EndIf

				If (crSigCdOpd.ChkFases = 1)
					lcQuery = [Select GrupoDs ] + ;
							    [From SigPdMvf ] + ;
							   [Where Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops))+[ And Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ]

					If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas2') < 1)
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalMFas2 2)')
						Return 0
					EndIf

					Select LocalMFas2
					Scan
						If (LocalMFas2.Grupods = TmpNens.Grupods) Or (LocalMFas2.Grupods = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Destino.Get_Grupo.Value)
							=Messagebox('Atençăo...' + Chr(13) + Chr(13) + 'Est' + ThisForm.Artigo + ' ' + ThisForm.Titulo + ' ' + ;
										'Já Passou Por Esta Fase ao Menos Uma Vez!!!', 32)
							Exit
						EndIf
					EndScan
				EndIf
				
				If CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests = 9
					lcQuery = [Select a.emps, a.Dopps, a.Numps, a.Cmats, a.Pesofixs, a.qtds, a.pesos, b.Datas, a.peso2s, ]+;
								[a.CodCors, a.CodTams, a.Servicos ]+;
								[From SigCdNei a, SigCdNec b ]+;
							  [Where a.Nops = ]+Str(LocalNops.Nops)+[ And a.Empdnps = b.EmpDnps Order by b.CidChaves Desc]

					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'LocalNensi')
					Select LocalNensi
					Scan
						=Seek(LocalNensi.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
						If (Not InList(crSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4) And crSigCdOpd.GrComps = 1 )
							Exit
						EndIf
					EndScan
					=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
					_ChaveOrig = LocalNensi.Emps + LocalNensi.Dopps + Str(LocalNensi.Numps, 10)
					_Bloquear = .f.
					Scan While Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10) = _ChaveOrig And Not _SepPedra
						If ( Pesos = 0 And Qtds = 0 ) Or InList(_TrfPesag,2,4) Or Servicos
							Loop
						EndIf
						_Bloquear = .t.
					EndScan
					If _Bloquear
						=Messagebox(Transform(LocalNops.Nops, '@L 9999999999') + ' Com Material Agregado!!!'+Chr(13)+;
								'mudança de Fase năo permitida!!!', 0+48, 'Atençăo...')
						This.Value = 0
						Select TmpNens
						Ok = .f.
						Return 0
					EndIf
				Endif

				If InList(crSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4)
					
					lcsql = [Select Emps, EmpDs, Dopes, Numes, Qtds, CodCors, CodTams, CodBarras, Nops, CodTgOps, citens ]+;
							[From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(LocalNops.Nops)
					ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')
					Select LocalOpi
					Scan
						If (LocalOpi.Qtds = 0)
							Loop
						EndIf

						ThisForm.Amarra = ThisForm.Amarra + 1
						lcEmp = Iif(Empty(LocalOpi.EmpDs), LocalOpi.Emps, LocalOpi.EmpDs)

						lcChv = lcEmp + LocalOpi.Dopes + Str(LocalOpi.Numes, 6)
						
						lcsql = [Select Contaos, contaDs From SigMvCab Where empdopnums = ']+lcchv+[']
						ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalEest')
						
						lcsql = [Select Globalizas, Servicos, CadProds, Pesos From SigCdOpe Where dopes = ']+LocalOpi.Dopes+[']
						Thisform.podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalOpe')
						
						lcSql = [Select dopes, EncPesMs From SigOpCdc Where Dopes = ']+LocalOpi.Dopes+[']
						ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalDcOpe')

						lcsql = [Select MatPrincs, Cgrus, Pesoms from SigCdPro where cpros = ']+LocalNops.CodPds+[']
						ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

						lcsql = [Select Mercs from SigCdGrp where cgrus = ']+localpro.cgrus+[']
						ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalGru')
						
						lcsql = [Select MatPrincs,cpqtds From SigCdGpr Where codigos = ']+localgru.mercs+[']
						ThisForm.PodataMgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'Localggrp')

						_MatP = IIF(!EMPTY(LocalPro.MatPrincs),LocalPro.MatPrincs,IIF(!EMPTY(LocalGgrp.Matprincs),LocalGgrp.MatPrincs,CrSigCdPam.Ouros))

						If (LocalOpe.Globalizas = 1) Or (LocalOpe.Servicos = 1)
							lcContaOs = LocalEest.ContaOs
						Else
							lcContaOs = LocalEest.ContaDs
						EndIf

						Insert Into xOpi (Nops, Oper, Qtds, CPros, Indiv, Amarra, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, Conta, ;
										  Empds, CodCors, CodTams, Cbars, Obrigs, citens ) ;
								  Values (LocalNops.NOps, Alltrim(LocalOpi.Dopes ) + '/' + Alltrim(Str(LocalOpi.Numes)), ;
										  LocalOpi.Qtds, LocalNops.CodPds, (crSigCdPam.TpPesas = 1 And LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs <> 1), ;
										  ThisForm.Amarra, LocalNops.Nenvs, LocalOpi.Emps, LocalOpi.Dopes, ;
										  LocalOpi.Numes, lcContaOs, lcEmp, LocalOpi.CodCors, LocalOpi.CodTams, ;
										  LocalOpi.CodBarras, (LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs = 1), LocalOpi.citens )

						m.Especial = Iif(InList(LocalOpe.CadProds,3,5) Or LocalOpe.Pesos = 1 ,.t.,.f.)
						
						Select ChkDests,ReiNops From CrSigCdOpd Where Dopps = LocalNops.Dopps Into Cursor TmpDopp
						Select TmpDopp
						If ChkDests = 1 And ReiNops <> 1
							_nEnvelope = LocalNops.Numps
						Else
							_nEnvelope = LocalNops.Nenvs
						Endif

						If ( crSigCdPam.TpPesas = 1 And LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs <> 1 And LocalOpi.CodBarras = 0 )
							_Cont = Int(xOpi.Qtds)
							_Qtde = 0
							Do While _Qtde < _Cont
								_Qtde = _Qtde + 1
								Insert Into xPesa (Oper, CPros, Qtds, Peso, Amarra, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, ;
												   Nops, Conta, Cors, Tams, MatPs, Pesoms, Especial, citens ) ;
										   Values (xOpi.Oper, xOpi.CPros, 1, IIF(LocalGgrp.cpQtds=1,1,0), ;
										   			ThisForm.Amarra, _nEnvelope,lcEmp, LocalOpi.Dopes, ;
										   			LocalOpi.Numes, LocalNops.Nops, lcContaos, LocalOpi.CodCors,;
										   			LocalOpi.CodTams, _MatP, LocalPro.Pesoms, m.Especial, LocalOpi.citens )
							EndDo

							If (xOpi.Qtds > _Qtde)
								Insert Into xPesa (Oper, CPros, Qtds, Peso, Amarra, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, ;
												   Nops, Conta, Cors, Tams, MatPs, Pesoms, Especial, citens ) ;
										   Values (xOpi.Oper, xOpi.CPros, xOpi.Qtds - _Qtde, ;
										   		IIF(LocalGgrp.cpQtds=1,xopi.qtds-_qtde,0), ThisForm.Amarra, ;
										   		   _nEnvelope, lcEmp, LocalOpi.Dopes, LocalOpi.Numes, ;
										   		   LocalNops.Nops, lcContaos, LocalOpi.CodCors, LocalOpi.CodTams, ;
										   		   _MatP, (LocalPro.Pesoms * (xOpi.Qtds - _Qtde)), m.Especial, LocalOpi.citens )
							EndIf
						Else
							If (crSigCdPam.Altpesas = 1)
								Insert Into xPesa (cBars, Oper, CPros, Qtds, Peso, Amarra, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, ;
												   Nops, Conta, Cors, Tams, Matps, Pesoms, Especial, Divs, citens ) ;
										   Values (LocalOpi.CodBarras, xOpi.Oper, xOpi.CPros, xOpi.Qtds, ;
										   		   Iif(LocalGgrp.cpQtds=1,xOpi.qtds,0), ThisForm.Amarra, ;
										   		   _nEnvelope, lcEmp, LocalOpi.Dopes, LocalOpi.Numes,;
										   		   LocalNOps.Nops, lcContaos, LocalOpi.CodCors, LocalOpi.CodTams, ;
										   		   _Matp, (LocalPro.Pesoms * xOpi.Qtds), m.Especial, (LocalDcOpe.EncPesMs = 1 ), LocalOpi.citens )
							Else
								Select xPesa
								Set Order To Nops
								Seek LocalOpi.Nops
								If Eof()
									Insert Into xPesa (cBars, Oper, CPros, Qtds, Peso, Amarra, Nenvs, Emps, Dopes, Numes, ;
													   Nops, Conta, Cors, Tams, Matps, Pesoms, Especial, citens ) ;
											   Values (LocalOpi.CodBarras, xOpi.Oper, xOpi.CPros, xOpi.Qtds, IIF(LocalGgrp.cpQtds=1,xopi.qtds,0), ;
											   		   ThisForm.Amarra, _nEnvelope, lcEmp, LocalOpi.Dopes, ;
											   		   LocalOpi.Numes, LocalNops.Nops, lcContaos, LocalOpi.CodCors, ;
											   		   LocalOpi.CodTams, _MatP, (LocalPro.Pesoms * xOpi.Qtds), m.Especial, LocalOpi.citens )
								Else
									Replace Qtds With Qtds + xOpi.Qtds
									IF LocalGgrp.CpQtds = 1
										Replace Peso WITH Qtds
									ENDIF
								EndIf
								Set Order To Amarra
							EndIf
						EndIf
					EndScan
				EndIf

				If Empty(TmpNens.GrVends)
					ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Responsavel.Get_Grupo.Value = LocalNens.GrVends
				EndIf
				If Empty(TmpNens.Vends) And (TmpNens.GrVends = LocalNens.GrVends)
					ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Responsavel.Get_Conta.Value = LocalNens.Vends
				EndIf

				=Seek(ThisForm._Dopp, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
				
				lcsql = [Select Emps, EmpDs, Dopes, Numes, Qtds, CodCors, CodTams, CodBarras, CodTgOps, citens ]+;
						[From SigOpPic where Nops = ]+Str(LocalNops.Nops)
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')	

				Select LocalOpi
				Sum Qtds To lnQtdMfas

				Insert Into xMFas (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Datars, Datas, Usuars, Opers, Grupoos, Contaos, Grupods, ;
								   Contads, NOps, NEnvs, Codpds, Unids, Pesos, Qtds, Obsps, Ordems, Obss) ;
						   Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, LocalNops.Datars, LocalNops.Datas, ;
						   		   Usuar, LocalNops.Opers, TmpNens.Grupoos, TmpNens.Contaos, TmpNens.Grupods, ;
						   		   TmpNens.Contads, LocalNops.Nops, _nOperacao, LocalNops.Codpds, LocalNops.Unids, ;
						   		   LocalNops.Pesos, lnQtdMfas, LocalNops.Obsps, LocalNops.Ordems, LocalNops.Obss)

				If InList(CrSigCdOpd.Apontas,1,2)
					lcSql = [Select * From SigInAop Where Grupos = ']+TmpNens.GrupoOs+[' And Contas = ']+TmpNens.ContaOs+[' ]+;
							[And Nops = ]+Str(LocalNops.Nops)+[ And EmpDnPs=' ' And Not DataFins is null ]
					Thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpAope')
					lcEDN = TmpNens.Emps + TmpNens.Dopps + Str(TmpNens.Numps,10)
					Tempo = 0
					Select TmpAope
					Scan
						Tempo = ( Tempo + ( DataFins - DataInis ) )
						Scatter Memvar
						m.EmpDnPs = lcEDN
						m.Nenvs   = This.Value
						Insert Into CrSigInAop From Memvar
					EndScan
					Replace xMfas.TmpMins With Fstom(Tempo) ,;
							xMfas.Autos   with 1 in xMfas
					If Tempo > 0

					Endif

				*** Carrega os componentes da OP agregados na fases anterios, menos os que foram agregados numa operaçăo de separaçăo de pedras
				lcQuery = [Select a.emps, a.Dopps, a.Numps, a.Cmats, a.Pesofixs, a.qtds, a.pesos, b.Datas, a.peso2s, ]+;
							[a.CodCors, a.CodTams, a.Servicos, a.TpOps, b.CidChaves From SigCdNei a, SigCdNec b ]+;
						  [Where a.Nops = ]+Str(xMfas.Nops)+[ And a.Empdnps = b.EmpDnps Order by b.CidChaves Desc]

				ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'LocalNensi')
				Select LocalNensi
				Scan
					=Seek(LocalNensi.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
					If (Not InList(crSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4) And crSigCdOpd.GrComps = 1 )
						llDesagrega = (crSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1) &&& Tiago - 27/03/2012 - Vianna - Se a última operaçăo da OP for tipo DESAGREGA, entăo traz os itens zerados também, porque se a operaçăo atual estiver para trazer as pedras agregadas na última separaçăo de pedra năo traga as pedras desagregadas novamente
						Exit
					EndIf
				EndScan
				=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
				lcbuscaN1 = LocalNensi.CidChaves
				_ChaveOrig = LocalNensi.Emps + LocalNensi.Dopps + Str(LocalNensi.Numps, 10)
				_TotalNop  = 0
				_RecLocNensi = Recno()
				Scan While Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10) = _ChaveOrig And Not _SepPedra
*!*						If ( Pesos = 0 And Qtds = 0 And Peso2s = 0 ) Or InList(_TrfPesag,2,4) Or Servicos
*!*							If InList(_TrfPesag,2,4) And LocalNensi.cMats <> csResultado.MatPs
*!*								Loop
*!*							Endif
*!*						EndIf
					If ( Pesos = 0 And Qtds = 0 And Peso2s = 0 AND !llDesagrega ) Or Servicos

					ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

*** Tiago - 26/09/2012 - Năo estava sendo usado por nenhum cliente e ninguém sabia pra que servia
*** Vou utilizar a flag PCCS para marcar as OPs como canceladas pela operaçăo de finalizaçăo antecipada
*!*						If CrSigCdOpd.pccs
*!*							If LocalNensi.TpOps = CrSigCdOpd.Retalhos
*!*								Loop
*!*							Endif
*!*							If !Seek( Str( xMFas.Nops, 10 ) + LocalNensi.CMats, 'xNensi','NopCMat' )
*!*								Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, QtFaseAnt, Qtds, ;
*!*													PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Visivel, Rateio, CGrus, MatPrincs, PesoFixs, TpOps, ;
*!*													cUniPs, Peso2s, ps2FaseAnt, CodCors, CodTams) ;
*!*											Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xMFas.Nops, _nOperacao, ;
*!*													LocalNensi.CMats, LocalPro.DPros, LocalPro.CUnis, LocalNensi.Qtds, ;
*!*													LocalNensi.Qtds, LocalNensi.Pesos, LocalNensi.Pesos, .f., ;
*!*													Iif(LocalPro.Varias=1 And LocalNensi.PesoFixs <> 1, 2, 3 ), ;
*!*													LocalPro.CGrus, csResultado.Matps, LocalNensi.PesoFixs, ;
*!*													Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao), ;
*!*													LocalPro.cunips, LocalNensi.Peso2s, LocalNensi.Peso2s, LocalNensi.CodCors, LocalNensi.CodTams)

							  [ And a.Empdnps = b.EmpDnps Order by b.CidChaves Desc]

								llDesagrega = (crSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1) &&& Tiago - 27/03/2012 - Vianna - Se a última operaçăo da OP for tipo DESAGREGA, entăo traz os itens zerados também, porque se a operaçăo atual estiver para trazer as pedras agregadas na última separaçăo de pedra năo traga as pedras desagregadas novamente						
							Endif
							If (InList(crSigCdOpd.SepPedras,1,3,4) And crSigCdOpd.GrComps = 1 And CrSigCdOpd.CHKQTDPS # 3 And crSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 4 And lcEmpDnps <> LocalNensi4.EmpDnps)

*!*								EndIf

									And InList(b.SepPedras,1,3,4) And crSigCdOpd.GrComps = 1 And CrSigCdOpd.CHKQTDPS # 3 ;

									Into Cursor CsSelecao Order by a.CidChaves Desc

										If (!llDesagrega And (!Seek( Str( xMFas.Nops, 10 ) + CsSelecao.CMats, 'xNensi','NopCMat' ) Or lcbuscaN > lcbuscaN1 )) && Tiago - estava OR (!llDesagrega And lcbuscaN > lcbuscaN1 ) - mudei devido estar carregando componente já desagregado
											Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, QtFaseAnt, Qtds, ;

																CsSelecao.Qtds, CsSelecao.Pesos, CsSelecao.Pesos, ;
																Iif(InList(_TrfPesag,2,4),.f.,.t.), ;
																Iif(_TrfPesag=6,5,Iif(LocalPro.Varias=1 And CsSelecao.PesoFixs <> 1, 2, 3 )), ;
																LocalPro.CGrus, csResultado.Matps, CsSelecao.PesoFixs, ;

										Endif

									Skip -1
								Endscan
							Else
								*** Tiago - 30/01/2013 - Se for operaçăo de separaçăo de pedra e teve desagrega pedra, carrega os itens desagreados na grade principal para poder agregar novamente						
								If _SepPedra And crSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1 And lcEmpDnps <> LocalNensi4.EmpDnps

												Endif
											EndIf

												*** Inclui o material que está agregado na OP; năo fica visível na grade de itens
												Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, QtFaseAnt, Qtds, ;

*!*													*** Inclui o material que foi desagregado na grade de itens, para somar com o que falta agregar de pedras

											Endif

							Endif							
						Endscan
