							=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
							_ChaveOrig3 = CsSelecao.Emps + CsSelecao.Dopps + Str(CsSelecao.Numps, 10)
							Scan While Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10) = _ChaveOrig3 And Not _SepPedra
								If Pesos = 0 And Qtds = 0
									Loop
								EndIf
								lcsql = [Select DPros, CGRus, CUnis, Varias, cunips From SigCdPro where cpros = ']+CsSelecao.cmats+[']
								ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')
								*** Tiago - 27/03/2012 - Vianna - Trazia todas as pedras agregadas na última separaçăo de pedra; mudei para checar se já tem o componente agregado nessa operaçăo
								If !Seek( Str( xMFas.Nops, 10 ) + CsSelecao.CMats, 'xNensi','NopCMat' ) Or (!llDesagrega And lcbuscaN > lcbuscaN1 )
									Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, QtFaseAnt, Qtds, ;
														PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Visivel, Rateio, CGrus, MatPrincs, PesoFixs, TpOps, ;
														cUniPs, Peso2s, ps2FaseAnt, CodCors, CodTams, TrfPesa) ;
												Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xMFas.Nops, _nOperacao, ;
														CsSelecao.CMats, LocalPro.DPros, LocalPro.CUnis, CsSelecao.Qtds, ;
														CsSelecao.Qtds, CsSelecao.Pesos, CsSelecao.Pesos, ;
														Iif(InList(_TrfPesag,2,4),.f.,.t.), ;
														Iif(_TrfPesag=6,5,Iif(LocalPro.Varias=1 And CsSelecao.PesoFixs <> 1, 2, 3 )), ;
														LocalPro.CGrus, csResultado.Matps, CsSelecao.PesoFixs, ;
														Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.tpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao ),;
														LocalPro.cUniPs, CsSelecao.Peso2s, CsSelecao.Peso2s, ;
														CsSelecao.CodCors, CsSelecao.CodTams, _TrfPesag)
									If InList(_TrfPesag,2,4) 
										_TotalNop = _TotalNop + CsSelecao.Pesos
									Endif
								Endif
							EndScan
							Skip -1
						Endscan
					Endif
				Endif

				=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
				If ( _CompAgru = 3 )
					Select LocalNensi
					Locate for Recno() =  _RecLocNensi
					Scan While Emps + Dopps + Str(Numps, 10) = _ChaveOrig And Not _SepPedra
						If Pesos = 0 And Qtds = 0
							Loop
						Endif
						Select xNensi
						Set Order to NopCMat
						If Not Seek(Str(xMfas.Nops,10) + csResultado.MatPs)

							lcsql = [Select DPros, CGRus, CUnis, Varias, cunips From SigCdPro where cpros = ']+csResultado.Matps+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

							Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, QtFaseAnt, Qtds, ;
												PsFaseAnt, Pesos, Visivel, Rateio, CGrus, MatPrincs, PesoFixs, TpOps, ;
												cUniPs, ps2FaseAnt) ;
										Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xMFas.Nops, _nOperacao, ;
												csResultado.Matps, LocalPro.DPros, LocalPro.CUnis, 1, ;
												1, 1, 1, .f., ;
												Iif(LocalPro.Varias=1 And LocalNensi.PesoFixs <> 1, 2, 3 ), ;
												LocalPro.CGrus, csResultado.Matps, 0, ;
												Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao), ;
												LocalPro.CuniPs,1)

							_TotalNop = _TotalNop + 1

						EndIf
					EndScan
				Endif

				If (_TotalNop <> 0 And CrSigCdOpd.ReiNops # 1)
					Select xNensi
					Set Order to NEnvCMat
					If Not Seek(_AgrupaOper + Space(10))
						Insert Into xNensi (Nops, Nenvs, Visivel, Rateio, CUnis, MatPrincs, TpOps) ;
									Values (_nAgrupaOper, _nAgrupaOper, .t., 1, crSigCdPam.CuniPPads, csResultado.MatPs, ;
											Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao))
					EndIf
					Replace PsFaseAnt With xNensi.PsFaseAnt + _TotalNop In xNensi
					If InList(_TrfPesag,1,2,5)
						Replace Pesos With psFaseAnt In xNensi
						If InList(crSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4)
							Select xPesa
							Locate For Nops = xMfas.Nops
							Replace Peso With _TotalNop in xPesa
						Endif
					Endif
				EndIf
				
				lcsql = [Select Qtds, empdopnums, citens From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(LocalMFas.Nops)
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalOpi')
				Select LocalOpi
*!*					Sum Qtds To _Qtde

				*** Tiago - 22/10/2010 - Incluído o scan para procurar todas os itens da op, pois pode ter itens que tiveram os componentes substituídos
				Scan 

					_qtde = LocalOpi.qtds
					lcSql = [Select a.Mats, a.Qtds, a.cats, a.grupos, a.ordems, a.cunis as unicompos, a.Pesos, a.units as pcompos, a.moevs as moeds ]+;
							[From SigSubMv a ]+;
							[Where a.empdopnums = '] + LocalOpi.empdopnums + [' and a.Cpros = ']+LocalMFas.CodPds+[' and a.citem2 = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalOpi.citens))
					=ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalCompo')
					
					If Reccount('LocalCompo') = 0
						lcsql = [Select Mats, Qtds, Cats, Grupos, Ordems, UniCompos, Pesos, pCompos, Moeds  From SigPrCpo Where Cpros = ']+LocalMFas.CodPds+[']
						ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
					EndIf

					If Not _NaoAgrega And Not _SepPedra

						Select LocalCompo
						Scan
							lcsql = [Select cpros,CUnis, DPros, CGrus, PesoMs, Varias, cunips, cproEqs From SigCdPro Where cpros = ']+LocalCompo.Mats+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'Localpro')
							IF NOT Empty(Localpro.cproeqs)
								lcsql = [Select cpros, CUnis, DPros, CGrus, PesoMs, Varias, cunips, cproEqs From SigCdPro Where cpros = ']+LocalPro.Cproeqs+[']
								ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'Localpro')
							EndIf 
							
							lcsql = [Select Fators,Cestos,QtEqualPs From SigCdUni Where Cunis = ']+LocalPro.Cunis+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalUni')
							
							lcsql = [Select Fators,Cestos,QtEqualPs From SigCdUni Where Cunis = ']+LocalPro.Cunips+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalUni2')

							lcsql = [Select cestoqs,TpMovs from SigCdGrp where cgrus = ']+localpro.cgrus+[']
							ThisForm.PodataMgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalGru')

							lcQuery = [Select cIdChaves ] + ;
									    [From SigPdMvf ] + ;
									   [Where Nops = ] + Alltrim(Str(xMFas.Nops)) + [ And Emps = ']+_Empr+[' And ] + ;
									   		 [Ordems = ] + Alltrim(Str(xMFas.Ordems + 1))

							If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crBusca') < 1)
								=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crBusca)')
								Return 0
							EndIf
							_JaExiste = (Reccount('crBusca') > 0)

							Select LocalCompo
							llAgrega = .f.
							If CrSigCdPac.AgregaODs = 1
								llAgrega = ( (Grupos = TmpNens.GrupoOs) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1) And (Ordems = xMFas.Ordems) )
							Else
								llAgrega = ( (Grupos = TmpNens.Grupods) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs = 1) And (Ordems = xMFas.Ordems + 1) )
							EndIf
							If llAgrega
								_QtAnt  = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds
								_Ps2Ant = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Pesos

								If Not Empty(LocalPro.Cunips) And ( ( LocalGru.TpMovs <> 1 And LocalUni2.Fators <> 1 ) OR ( LocalUni2.QtEqualPs = [S] ) )
									_PsAnt = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Pesos * LocalUni2.Fators
								Else
									If (LocalUni.Fators = 0)
										_PsAnt = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds * LocalPro.Pesoms
									Else
										_PsAnt = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds * LocalUni.Fators
									EndIf
								Endif
								_CMat = Localpro.Cpros

								If (_CompAgru = 1)
									_DPro = Space(40)
									llVisivel = .f.
								Else
									_DPro = LocalPro.DPros
									llVisivel = .t.
								EndIf

								Select xNensi
								Set Order to NopCMat
								If !Seek(Str(xMfas.Nops,10) + Localpro.cpros )
									Select LocalCompo

									Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, ;
														QtFaseAnt, PsFaseAnt, Visivel, Rateio, FlagIncs, Cats, MatPrincs,;
														TpOps, cidchaves, cUniPs, Ps2FaseAnt) ;
												Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, xMFas.Nops, _nOperacao, ;
														Localpro.cpros, LocalPro.Dpros, LocalPro.CUnis, LocalPro.CGrus, ;
														_QtAnt, _PsAnt, llVisivel, Iif(LocalPro.Varias=1, 2, 3), .t., ;
														LocalCompo.Cats, csResultado.Matps, ;
														Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao), ;
														fUniqueIds(), LocalPro.CuniPs, _Ps2Ant)
								EndIf
								_newChave = xNensi.CidChaves
								If Not Seek(_AgrupaOper + _CMat, 'xNensi', 'NEnvCMat')
									Insert Into xNensi (Nops, Nenvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, ;
														Visivel, Rateio, FlagIncs, Cats, MatPrincs, TpOps) ;
												Values (_nAgrupaOper, _nAgrupaOper, _CMat, _DPro, ;
														LocalPro.CUnis, LocalPro.CGrus, .t., 1, .t., ;
														LocalCompo.Cats, csResultado.Matps, ;
														Iif(Not Empty(CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos),CrSigCdOpd.TpPadraos,_TpOpPadrao))
								ENDIF
								
								IF xNensi.CidChaves # _newchave
									Replace QtFaseAnt  With xNensi.QtFaseAnt  + _QtAnt, ;
											PsFaseAnt  With xNensi.PsFaseAnt  + _PsAnt, ;
											Ps2FaseAnt With xNensi.Ps2FaseAnt + _Ps2Ant, ;
											Qtds       With xNensi.Qtds + _QtAnt, ;
											Peso2s     With xnensi.Peso2s + _Ps2Ant ,;
											Pesos      With xNensi.Pesos + _PsAnt In xNensi
								Else
									Replace Qtds      With xNensi.Qtds   + _QtAnt,;
											Peso2s    with xNensi.Peso2s + _Ps2Ant ,;
											Pesos     With xNensi.Pesos  + _PsAnt In xNensi
								Endif
								If _TrfPesag = 9
									Replace Pesos with 0 in xNensi
								Endif
							EndIf

							Select LocalCompo
							*** Tiago - 25/08/11 - Analisar pois acho que aqui faz o lançamento automático dos serviços
							If (Grupos = TmpNens.Grupoos) And (LocalGru.CEstoqs <> 1) And (Ordems = xMFas.Ordems) And Not Empty(LocalCompo.Cats)
								Select crSigCdSvc
								Set Order to CaGruCo
								Do Case
									Case Seek(LocalCompo.Cats + TmpNens.Grupoos + TmpNens.Contaos)
									Case Seek(LocalCompo.Cats + TmpNens.Grupoos + Space(10))
									Case Seek(LocalCompo.Cats + Space(20))
									Otherwise
										Loop
								EndCase

*!*									If Not Seek(LocalCompo.Cats, 'xNensi', 'Cats') *** Tiago - 25/10/11 - Vianna - Agrega o serviço separado de cada OP; antes agrupava os serviços iguais
								If Not Seek(Str(xMfas.Nops,10) + LocalCompo.Cats, 'xNensi', 'NEnvMCat')
								
									Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, Visivel, Rateio, ;
														FlagIncs, Cats, Servicos, Fators, Moedas, GrupoFins, Retrab, Coefs, Nenvs) ;
												Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, LocalCompo.Cats, ;
														LocalPro.Dpros, LocalPro.CUnis, LocalPro.CGrus, .t., 0, .t., ;
														LocalCompo.Cats, .t., CrSigCdSvc.Coefs, CrSigCdSvc.CMoeds, ;
														CrSigCdSvc.GruFins, 0, CrSigCdSvc.Coefretrs, xMfas.Nops)
									If CrSigCdSvc.Bases = [V]
										Replace Fators   With LocalCompo.pCompos,;
												Moedas   With LocalCompo.Moeds,;
												ServAuto With 1 In xNensI
									EndIf

									_Grupo = TmpNens.GrupoOs
									_Conta = TmpNens.ContaOs
									If (crSigCdOpd.PagServs = 1)
										_Grupo = TmpNens.GrupoDs
										_Conta = TmpNens.ContaDs
									EndIf
									
									lcQuery = [Select a.comis from SigCdCrg a inner join SigCdCli b on a.CCargs = b.CCargs where Iclis = '] + _Conta + [']
									If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalCar') < 1)
										=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalCar)')
										Return .F.
									EndIf
									Select LocalCar
									Go Top
									
									Select xNensi
									Replace Fators 	  With (Fators * LocalCar.Comis) / 100 , ;
											Coefs     With (Coefs  * LocalCar.Comis) / 100
											
									*** Tiago - 26/08/11 - Checa se ja teve servicos lancados nas outras fases. Se tiver, checa se paga retrabalho									
									lcQuery  = [Select top 1 b.cmats from sigPdMvf a inner join sigcdnei b on a.empdnps = b.empdnps ] +;
												[inner join sigcdnec c on a.empdnps = c.empdnps and ] +;
												[((a.grupoos = '] +_Grupo + [' and a.contaos = '] +_Conta+ [') or ]  +;
												[(a.grupods = '] +_Grupo + [' and a.contads = '] +_Conta+ [')) ]  +;
												[Where a.Nops = '] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops))+[' And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ] + ;
												[And b.Cmats = '] + LocalCompo.Cats + [' ] + ;
												[And b.servicos = 1 order by a.cidchaves desc ] &&a.empdnps, b.cats, b.cmats, b.cretrabs 
									If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas2') < 1)
										=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalMFas2 2)')
										Return 0
									EndIf

									Select LocalMFas2
									If !Eof()
										replace TmpNens.Retrabs with .t. in TmpNens
										replace xNensi.Retrab with 1 in xNensi

										lcQuery = [Select Rclis from SigCdCli where Iclis = '] + _Conta + [']
										If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalCliSer') < 1)
											=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalCliSer)')
											Return 0
										EndIf									

										If Messagebox([O.P. ] + Alltrim(Str(_Nops))+ [] + [ já possui o serviço '] + ;
													 LocalMFas2.cMats + [ - ] + Alltrim(LocalPro.Dpros) + ['] + Chr(13) + ;
													 [ lançado para ] + _Grupo + [/] +  _Conta + [ - ] + Alltrim(LocalCliSer.Rclis) + [.] + Chr(13) + ;
													 [Será lançado um retrabalho com pagamento?],4+48+256) = 7
											replace xNensi.Fators with 0, ;
													xNensi.Coefs with 0 in xNensi													 
										EndIf
									EndIf
									*****									
								EndIf
								Replace Qtds With xNensi.Qtds + (_Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds) In xNensi
							EndIf

						EndScan

					EndIf

					Select LocalCompo
					Scan
						lcsql = [Select MedTmps From SigCdUni Where Cunis = ']+LocalCompo.UniCompos+[']
						ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalUni')
						Select Localcompo
						If (Grupos = TmpNens.Grupoos And Ordems = xMFas.Ordems And LocalUni.MedTmps = [S])
							Replace BaseMins With BaseMins + (_Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds ) in xMfas
						EndIf

						*** Tiago - 27/10/11 - Vianna - Checa na finalizaçăo da OP se os componentes estăo agregados corretamente
						If !_SepPedra and CrSigCdOpd.ChkQtdps = 4					
							lcsql = [Select CGrus, Varias From SigCdPro Where cpros = ']+LocalCompo.Mats+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'Localpro')
							If Localpro.Varias <> 1 And Empty(LocalCompo.Cats) 
								lnQtdCmp = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds &&LocalMFas.Qtds * LocalCompo.Qtds
								lnPesoCmp = _Qtde * LocalCompo.Pesos &&LocalMFas.Qtds * LocalCompo.Pesos
							
								If Not Seek(Str(_nOperacao, 10) + Localpro.Cgrus, 'xNensiP', 'NenvsCgrus')
									Insert Into xNensiP (NEnvs, CMats, Cgrus ) ;
												Values (_nOperacao, '', Localpro.Cgrus )
								EndIf
								Replace Qtds  With Qtds + lnQtdCmp ,;
										Pesos With Pesos + lnPesoCmp In xNensiP
							EndIf
						EndIf
						***
					Endscan

					*** Tiago - 27/10/11 - Vianna - Checa na finalizaçăo da OP se os componentes estăo agregados corretamente
					If !_SepPedra and CrSigCdOpd.ChkQtdps = 4					
						lcOrder = Set("Order")
						Select xNensi
						Set Order To tag NopCMat

						Select Cgrus, Cunis, Cunips, Sum(Qtds) as Qtds, Sum(Peso2s) as Pesos from xNensi where Nops = _nOperacao And Rateio = 3 And !Servicos GROUP By Cgrus, Cunis, Cunips Into Cursor TmpTotAgre

						Select a.Cgrus, a.Qtds as QtdCompo, a.Pesos as PesoCompo, Nvl(b.Qtds,0) as QtdAgre, Nvl(b.Pesos,0) as PesoAgre, Nvl(b.Cunis,'') as Cunis, Nvl(b.Cunips,'') as Cunips ;
							from xNensiP a Left Join TmpTotAgre b on a.Cgrus = b.Cgrus Into Cursor TmpDifAgre
						Select TmpDifAgre
						Scan
							lcSql = [Select cEstos, Fators From SigCdUni Where cunis = ']+TmpDifAgre.cunis+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpUni')
							lcSql = [Select cEstos, Fators From SigCdUni Where cunis = ']+TmpDifAgre.cuniPs+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpUni2')

							lcSql = [Select Premios From SigCdGrp Where cGrus = ']+TmpDifAgre.cGrus+[']
							ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpGrp')

							xDif  = TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo - Nvl(TmpDifAgre.QtdAgre,0)
							xDifp = abs( xDif / TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo * 100 )
							xDif2  = TmpDifAgre.PesoCompo - Nvl(TmpDifAgre.PesoAgre,0)
							xDifp2 = abs( xDif2 / TmpDifAgre.PesoCompo * 100 )

*!*								If (TmpUni.Fators = 1 And !Empty(TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo) And TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo <> Nvl(TmpDifAgre.QtdAgre,0)) or (TmpUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(TmpDifAgre.cUniPs) And TmpDifAgre.PesoCompo <> Nvl(TmpDifAgre.PesoAgre,0))
							If (TmpUni.Fators = 1 And !Empty(TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo) And TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo <> Nvl(TmpDifAgre.QtdAgre,0)) Or ;
								(TmpUni.Fators <> 1 And !Empty(xDif) And xDifp > TmpGrp.Premios) Or ;
								(TmpUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(TmpDifAgre.cUniPs) And TmpUni2.Fators = 1 And TmpDifAgre.PesoCompo <> Nvl(TmpDifAgre.PesoAgre,0)) Or ;
								(TmpUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(TmpDifAgre.cUniPs) And TmpUni2.Fators <> 1 And xDifp2 > TmpGrp.Premios)
																
								=MessageBox([Algum componente do Grupo = '] + TmpDifAgre.Cgrus + [' está com quantidade ou peso diferente do cadastro do produto.] + Chr(13) +;
											[Composiçăo: Qtde = ] + Str(TmpDifAgre.QtdCompo,12,3) + [  /  Peso = ] + Str(TmpDifAgre.PesoCompo,12,3) + Chr(13) + ;
											[Agregado  : Qtde = ] + Str(TmpDifAgre.QtdAgre,12,3) + [  /  Peso = ] + Str(TmpDifAgre.PesoAgre,12,3),48,[Dif. Composiçăo x Material Agregado])
								Ok = .f.
							EndIf
						EndScan

						Select TmpDifAgre
						Use
						Select TmpTotAgre
						Use
						
						If !Ok
							This.Value = 0
							Select TmpNens
							Return 0
						EndIf						
						Select xNensi
						Set Order To tag lcOrder
					EndIf
					***

					If _SepPedra
						lcSql = [Select a.Mats, a.Qtds, a.Pesos ]+;
								[From SigSubMv a ]+;
								[Where a.empdopnums = '] + LocalOpi.empdopnums + [' and a.Cpros = ']+LocalMFas.CodPds+[' and a.citem2 = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalOpi.citens))
						=ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalCompo')
						
						If Reccount('LocalCompo') = 0
						
							*--Rafael - 31/08/2016 - Busca a movimentaçăo do subnivel caso nao localiza a substituiçăo
							lcQuery = [select a.emps + b.dopes +str(a.numes,6) as EDN ]+;
								[from sigmvpec a ]+;
								[join sigcdope b on b.ndopes = convert(int,a.codigos/1000000) ]+;

							=Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,[LocalEDN])

							If Reccount('LocalEDN') > 0
								lcSql = [Select a.Mats, a.Qtds, a.Pesos ]+;
									[From SigSubMv a ]+;
									[Where a.empdopnums = '] + LocalEDN.EDN + [' and a.Cpros = ']+LocalMFas.CodPds+[' and a.citem2 = ] + Alltrim(Str(LocalOpi.citens))
								=ThisForm.Podatamgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'LocalCompo')
							Endif

							If Reccount([LocalCompo]) = 0	
								lcsql = [Select Mats, Qtds, Pesos From SigPrCpo where Cpros = ']+LocalMFas.CodPds+[']
								ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCompo')
							EndIf 
						EndIf
						Select LocalCompo
						Scan
							lcsql = [Select a.CUnis, a.DPros, a.CGrus, a.cunips, b.SemiAcabs From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b Where a.cpros = ']+LocalCompo.Mats+[' ]+;
									[And a.Cgrus = b.Cgrus ]
							Thisform.podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')

							If ( Not IsEmpty(CrSigCdPam.cGruEstPs) )

									Loop
								EndIf
							Else
*!*									If Not InList(LocalPro.SemiAcabs,1,3)
								If (CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests <> 5 and Not InList(LocalPro.SemiAcabs,1,3)) or (CrSigCdOpd.ChkDests = 5 and LocalPro.SemiAcabs <> 4) && Tiago - 05/08/11 - Vianna
									Loop
								Endif
							EndIf

*!*								_Qtde = LocalMFas.Qtds * LocalCompo.Qtds
*!*								_Peso = LocalMFas.Qtds * LocalCompo.Pesos
							*** Tiago - 17/07/2012 - Vianna - Incluído checagem de crSigCdOpd.nCarQtds = 1 (năo carrega qtde e peso na separaçăo de pedra)
							lnQtdCmp = Iif(crSigCdOpd.nCarQtds = 1, 0, _Qtde * LocalCompo.Qtds)
							lnPesoCmp = Iif(crSigCdOpd.nCarQtds = 1, 0, _Qtde * LocalCompo.Pesos)

							If Not Seek(Str(_nOperacao, 10) + LocalCompo.Mats, 'xNensiP', 'Nenvs')

*!*													Values (_nOperacao, LocalCompo.Mats, LocalPro.Cgrus )

										&& _Qtde

								If Not Seek( Str(Iif(CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras=4,0,Iif(CrSigCdOpd.SepPedras=3,LocalMfas.Nops,_nOperacao)),10) + LocalCompo.Mats, 'xNensi', 'NopCMatV') && Tiago - 30/01/2013 - Alterei para usar o índice NopCmatV que só filtra os itens que estăo visíveis na grade
									Insert Into xNensi (Emps, Dopps, Numps, Nops, NEnvs, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, ;

								Thisform.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'LocalUni2')

								If CrTmpGru.TpMovs <> 1
									If LocalUni.Fators <> 1
										Select xNensi
										Replace Pesos With (xNensi.Qtds * LocalUni.Fators) In xNensi
									Else
										If LocalUni2.Fators <> 1 And Not Empty(CrtmpPro.CUniPs)
											Replace Pesos With (xNensi.Peso2s * LocalUni2.Fators) In xNensi
										EndIf
									Endif
								EndIf
								
								Replace Qtds  With Iif(Qtds < 0, 0, Qtds ) ,;
										Pesos With Iif(Pesos< 0, 0, Pesos),;
										Peso2s With Iif(Peso2s< 0, 0, Peso2s),;
										Aqtds With Qtds,;
										aPesos With Peso2s In xNensi

								Select xNensi
								If Qtds <= 0
									Delete
								Endif
							Endscan
						Endscan
					Endif
					=Seek(LocalNensi4.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')
					If !llDesagrega 
						llDesagrega = (crSigCdOpd.ReiNops = 1) &&& Tiago - 27/03/2012 - Vianna - Se a última operaçăo da OP for tipo DESAGREGA, entăo traz os itens zerados também, porque se a operaçăo atual estiver para trazer as pedras agregadas na última separaçăo de pedra năo traga as pedras desagregadas novamente						
					Endif
					=Seek(TmpNens.Dopps, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')					
				Endscan
			EndIf

			lcQuery = [Select a.Nenvs, a.GrupoDs, a.ContaDs, a.GrupoOs, a.ContaOs, a.Dopps, a.EmpDnPs, a.cRetrabs, ]+;
						[c.EmpDopNums From SigPdMvf a, SigCdOpd b, SigOpPic c, SigCdSvc d ]+;
						[Where a.nenvs = ]+Str(_noperacao)+[ And a.Dopps=b.Dopps And b.PagServs = 3 And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ]+;
						[And a.Nops = c.Nops And a.GrupoDs = d.Grupos And a.ContaDs = d.Contas order by a.CidChaves ]

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalMFas4') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalMFas4)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			
			Select LocalMfas4
			If Reccount() > 0
				Go Bott
				Select CsContas
				Set Order To NenvGruCon
				If Not Seek(Str(Localmfas4.Nenvs))
					Append Blank
					Replace Nenvs  With LocalMfas4.Nenvs,;
							Grupos With Localmfas4.grupods,;
							Contas With LocalMfas4.Contads
				EndIf
				
				lcsql = [Select Cpros,Dpros,Moedas,Qtds,EmpDopNums,Dopes From SigMvItp Where EmpDopNums = ']+LocalMfas4.EmpDopNums+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpEsti3')
				
				Select TmpEsti3
				Scan
					llRetrab = Not Empty(LocalMfas4.cRetrabs)
					
					lcsql = [Select DigEnves From SigCdOpe Where Dopes = ']+TmpEsti3.dopes+[']
					Thisform.Podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'Crope')
					
					lcsql = [Select Dpros,Cunis,Cgrus, cUniPs From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+TmpEsti3.Cpros+[']
					Thisform.podatamgr.sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalPro')
					
					Insert Into xNensIs (Emps, Dopps, Numps, CMats, CDescs, CUnis, CGrus, Visivel, Rateio, ;
										FlagIncs, Cats, Servicos, Moedas, Retrabs, Qtds, Nenvs, Pesos, ;
										cRetrabs, OsRets) ;
								Values (TmpNens.Emps, TmpNens.Dopps, TmpNens.Numps, TmpEsti3.cpros, ;
										LocalPro.Dpros, LocalPro.CUnis, LocalPro.CGrus, .t., 0, .t., ;
										Left(TmpEsti3.Cpros,3), .t., TmpEsti3.Moedas, llRetrab,;
										TmpEsti3.Qtds, LocalMfas4.Nenvs, TmpEsti3.Qtds, LocalMfas4.cRetrabs, ;
										Iif(CrOpe.DigEnves>0,.t.,.f.))

					If InList(crSigCdOpd.Etiqs, 1, 3, 4)
						Replace GrupoFs With LocalMfas4.GrupoDs,;
								ContaFs With LocalMfas4.ContaDs in xNensIs
					Endif

				EndScan
			Endif
			
			lcQuery = [Select a.Nenvs, a.GrupoDs, a.ContaDs, a.Dopps, a.Numps, a.cRetrabs, a.datas, b.descs, c.Rclis ]+;
					  [From SigPdMvf a, SigPrCrt b, SigCdCli c ]+;
					  [Where a.nenvs = ]+Str(_noperacao)+[ And a.cRetrabs<>' ' And ]+;
					  [a.cRetrabs=b.Cods And a.ContaDs = c.Iclis And a.Emps = ']+_Empr+[' ]

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'Lcmfas5') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Text - LocalMFas5)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			
			Select Lcmfas5
			Scan
				Insert Into xNensiR (nenvs, EmpDopNums, Datas, Destinos, Retrabs, Rclis ) Values ;
					(lcmfas5.nenvs, Alltrim(lcmfas5.dopps)+'-'+Alltrim(Str(lcmfas5.Numps,10)),lcmfas5.datas,;
					 Alltrim(lcmfas5.grupods)+'/'+Alltrim(lcmfas5.contads),;
					 lcmfas5.cretrabs+'-'+lcmfas5.descs, Alltrim(lcmfas5.rclis) )
			EndScan
			
			With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados
				lcsql = [Select Rclis From SigCdCli where Iclis = ']+TmpNens.contaos+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCli')
				If Not Eof('LocalCli')
					.origem.get_dconta.Value = LocalCli.RClis
				Else
					.origem.get_dconta.Value = ''
				EndIf

				lcsql = [Select Rclis From SigCdCli where Iclis = ']+TmpNens.contaDs+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCli')
				If Not Eof('LocalCli')
					.destino.get_dconta.Value = LocalCli.RClis
				Else
					.destino.get_dconta.Value = ''
				EndIf

				lcsql = [Select Rclis From SigCdCli where Iclis = ']+TmpNens.vends+[']
				ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalCli')
				If Not Eof('LocalCli')
					.Responsavel.get_dconta.Value = LocalCli.RClis
				Else
					.Responsavel.get_dconta.Value = ''
				EndIf
			EndWith

			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Refresh
			Select TmpOperacao
			If ((CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 1 And ThisForm.tiposubnivel = 'OP') Or ;
				(CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 2 And ThisForm.Tiposubnivel = 'ENV')) And TmpOperacao.Apontas = 0
				llRet = .t.
			Else
				Skip
				If Eof()
					Append Blank
					Keyboard '{DNARROW}'
				EndIf
				ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Refresh
			EndIf
			Return .t.
		Else
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Select TmpNens
		Return 0
	Endif
EndIf
Select xNensi
Set Order To

=Seek(ThisForm._Dopp, 'crSigCdOpd', 'Dopps')

Select TmpNens
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Refresh
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
ThisForm._OldCodigo = This.Value
If Not InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') Or TmpOPeracao.Autos
	Return .f.
EndIf
Set Confirm On

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.GradeOperaçăo.Column2.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 74
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Select TmpOperacao
_Operacao  = Right(Str(TmpOperacao.codigos, 12), 10)
_nOperacao = Val(_Operacao)
If TmpOperacao.TmpMins > 0 And ThisForm.tiposubnivel = 'ENV'
	Select xMFas
	Set Order to
	Sum BaseMins to xBase for Nenvs = _nOperacao
	If xBase = 0
		Sum Qtds to xBase for Nenvs = _nOperacao
		Scan For Nenvs = _Noperacao
			Replace TmpMins With ( Qtds / xBase * TmpOperacao.TmpMins )
		Endscan
	Else
		Scan For Nenvs = _Noperacao
			Replace TmpMins With ( BaseMins / xBase * TmpOperacao.TmpMins)
		Endscan
	EndIf
EndIf
Select TmpOperacao
Delete For Codigos = 0
Set Order To Codigos
Seek 0
If Eof()
	Insert Into TmpOperacao (Codigos) Values (0)
EndIf
Set Order To
Go Bott
Keyboard '{PGDN}'

Thisform.Pagina.Dados.GradeOperaçăo.Refresh

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Local llRet
llRet = .f.
If (CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 1 And ThisForm.tiposubnivel = 'OP') Or ;
	(CrSigCdOpd.Apontas = 2 And ThisForm.Tiposubnivel = 'ENV')
	llRet = .t.
Endif
ThisForm._OldCodigo = This.Value
llOk = (InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And llRet And TmpOperacao.codigos > 0 And TmpOperacao.Apontas = 0 )
Return ( llOK )

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.get_codobs
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 79
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pIni, pFim

loCnx = ThisForm.poDataMgr

If Not Empty(This.Value) And (Thisform.AntValue <> This.Value)
	loCnx.CursorQuery('SigCdOpd', 'LocalOpp', 'Dopps', TmpNens.Dopps, 'ObsPads, ObsInis, ObsFins')
	pIni = Iif(Not Eof('LocalOpp') And Not Empty(LocalOpp.ObsInis), LocalOpp.ObsInis, 000)
	pFim = Iif(Not Eof('LocalOpp') And Not Empty(LocalOpp.ObsFins), LocalOpp.ObsFins, 999)

	lcQuery = [Select Codigos, Descrs ] + ;
			    [From SigCdObs ] + ;
			   [Where Codigos BetWeen ?pIni And ?pFim]

	If (loCnx.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crLocalObs') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crLocalObs)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Select crLocalObs
	Index On Codigos Tag Codigos
	Index On Descrs Tag Descrs

	Set Near On
	If Not Seek(This.Value, 'crLocalObs', 'Codigos')
		m.loBrowse = CreateObject('fwbuscasel', 'crLocalObs', 'Codigos', This.Value, 'Observaçőes')
		m.loBrowse.AddColuna('Codigos', '999', 'Cód.', .t., 'Codigos')
		m.loBrowse.AddColuna('Descrs', '', 'Descriçăo', .t., 'Descrs')
		m.loBrowse.Show
	Endif
	Set Near Off

	If (Lastkey()=27)
		Return 0
	EndIf

	This.Value = crLocalObs.Codigos
	loCnx.Cursorquery('SigCdObs','CrSigCdObs','Codigos',This.Value)
	Select crSigCdObs
	This.parent.Mm_obs.Value = crSigCdObs.Observas
	This.refresh
EndIf
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Thisform.AntValue = This.Value
Return Inlist( ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR' )

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.EtqCompo
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 84
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If MessageBox('Confirma Impressăo das Etiquetas?',4+32+256,'') = 7
	Return
EndIf

Select xNensi
Create Cursor TmpDistrib (Nops n(10), Nenvs n(10), CodPds c (10), CMats c(14), CUnis c(3), Qtds n(10,3), Pesos n(10,3), ;
						  Qtds2 n(10,3), Pesos2 n(10,3), CDescs c(40), CGrus c(3), TpOps c(15), nLotes n(10))
Select xNensi
Set Order to NopCMat
Scan
	If Visivel &&And Not FlagIncs
		Loop
	EndIf
	_Qtds  = QtFaseAnt
	_Pesos = PsFaseAnt
	lcSql = [Select Cpros From SigOpPic Where Nops = ]+Str(xnensi.Nops)
	=Thisform.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcsql,'TmpOpi')
	Insert Into TmpDistrib (Nops, Nenvs, Qtds2, Pesos2, CUnis, CMats, CDescs, CGrus, Qtds, Pesos, nLotes, CodPds) ;
					Values (xNensi.Nops, xNensi.Nenvs, _Qtds, _Pesos, xNensi.CUnis, xNensi.CMats, xNensi.CDescs, ;
							xNensi.CGrus, xNensi.Qtds, xNensi.Pesos, xNensi.nLotes, TmpOpi.Cpros)
EndScan

Select TmpDistrib
Index On Str(Nenvs, 6) + CodPds + CMats Tag Impressao

Create Cursor dbImpressao (Pedido C(30), Cpros C(14), Qtds N(10,3), QtdeEtiq N(10,3), Obs C(10), PVens n(12,2), PrecoDe N(12,2), Parcelas N(2,0), ;
						   CPro1 c(14), Pr1Lt1 c(36), Pr1Lt2 c(36), Pr1Lt3 c(36), Pr1Lt4 c(36), ;
						   CPro2 c(14), Pr2Lt1 c(36), Pr2Lt2 c(36), Pr2Lt3 c(36), Pr2Lt4 c(36), ;
						   CPro3 c(14), Pr3Lt1 c(36), Pr3Lt2 c(36), Pr3Lt3 c(36), Pr3Lt4 c(36))

Select NEnvs, CodPds, CMats, Qtds, Pesos ;
  From TmpDistrib ;
 Order By NEnvs, CodPds, CMats ;
  Into Cursor crImps
  
lnNen = 9999999999
lnEti = 1
lnPro = 1
lnLot = 1

Select crImps
Scan
	If (lnNen <> crImps.Nenvs) Or (lnPro > 3) Or (lnLot > 4)
		lnNen = crImps.Nenvs
		lnEti = 1
		lcLin = []
		Insert Into dbImpressao (Pedido, CPros, Qtds, QtdeEtiq) ;
						 Values (Alltrim(Str(crImps.Nenvs,10)), crImps.CodPds, 1, 1)
	EndIf

	lnPro = 1
	Do While (lnNen = crImps.Nenvs) And (lnPro <= 3) And Not Eof()
		lcPrd = Alltrim(Str(lnPro))
		
		Replace CPro&lcPrd. With crImps.CodPds In dbImpressao

		lnLot = 1
		lcPro = crImps.CodPds
		Do While (lcPro = crImps.CodPds) And (lnLot <= 4) And Not Eof()
			lcLot = Alltrim(Str(lnLot))
			
			Replace Pr&lcPrd.Lt&lcLot. With crImps.CMats + Str(crImps.Qtds, 13, 3) + Str(crImps.Pesos, 13, 3) In dbImpressao
			Skip In crImps
			lnLot = lnLot + 1
		EndDo
		lnPro = lnPro + 1
	EndDo
	Skip -1 In crImps

	lnEti = lnEti + 1
EndScan

Select dbImpressao
Go Top

Do Form SigOpEtS with Thisform, ThisForm.DataSessionId

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Etiquetas
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 87

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click

PROCEDURE Click
Local _TrfPesag
If (ThisForm.pcEscolha <> 'PROCURAR')
	ThisForm.Enabled = .f.
	Select xNensi
	Set Order To
	ThisForm.Enabled = .f.

	_TrfPesag = CrSigCdOpd.TrfPesas
	If _TrfPesag = 7
		=Seek(TmpNens.GrupoOs,'TmpGccr','BalCodigo')
		_TrfPesag = Iif(TmpGccr.TrfPesas=2,5,Iif(TmpGccr.TrfPesas>=4,0,TmpGccr.TrfPesas))
	Endif

	If (crSigCdPam.AltPesas = 1) And _TrfPesag <> 1
		Select xOpi
		Go Top

		Do Form SigPdMp3 With ThisForm, ThisForm.DataSessionId
	Else
		Select xPesa
		Go Top

		Do Form SigPdMp9 With ThisForm
	EndIf
Endif

* OBJETO: SIGPDMP6.Pagina.Dados.Componentes

If (ThisForm.pcEscolha <> 'PROCURAR')
	
	ThisForm.Enabled = .f.
	Select xNensi
	Set Order To
	
	If CrSigCdOpd.Reinops = 1 And ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'INSERIR'
		Select xNensi
		Go Top
		If Not Eof()
			Do Form SigPdMp4 With ThisForm
		Else
			ThisForm.Enabled = .t.
		EndIf
	Else
		SELECT TmpOperacao
		SUM 1 TO _TotEnv FOR NOT EMPTY(codigos)

		IF ( _TotEnv = 0 AND CrSigCdOpd.EnvObrigs = 1 ) And InList(Thisform.pcEscolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR')
			ThisForm.Enabled = .t.
			=MessageBox('Nenhuma OP ou Envelope foi informado!', 48, 'Aviso')
		Else
			SELECT xNensi
			GO Top
			Do Form SigPdMp2 With ThisForm, ThisForm.DataSessionId
		Endif
	Endif
EndIf
